- **Contradictions:** None observed. The M05.A–F deviations are all forward-compat (capability primitives ship complete; wire-up deferred via ADR-0009) or interpretation-gap (phase doc vs spec text in the §8.security L4 + L5 + L3 cases, with phase doc winning as merged contract).

- **Ambiguity:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §8.security L1 — enforcer error variant set: spec doesn't enumerate `NoDeclarations` vs `NoMatchingGrant` distinct error reasons. M05.B ships both as discriminated variants of `CapabilityError::Denied`. Lock the choice in spec.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §8.security L4 — `HitlContext::BudgetThreshold(percent)` precondition: exact threshold % vs ≥ threshold %. M04.E ships ≥ semantics; M05 didn't touch. M04 carry-forward.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §3 — `gap-node-${gapId}` keying convention for GapNode (M05.A ships `${kind}:${name}:${agent_id}`-keyed idempotence). Spec doesn't pin; bundle.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §13.5 — audit log retention policy: spec doesn't address rotation / archival / disk-quota. v0.1 ships unbounded growth per phase doc E.3.1 + M05.E Decision E1; v1.0+ may add rotation.

- **Open questions:**
  - When does the M06 plan_loop driver land — SDK-side wrapper around `run_agent_with_provider_stream` or Tauri-managed orchestrator? ADR-0009 names "M06 Stage A" as the wire-up moment but doesn't pin the architectural placement; M06 prep should lock.
  - The `tier_violation` event payload: M05.D ships `{agent_id, current_tier, capability_kind}` but doesn't yet carry the requested-action shape that triggered the rejection. v1.0 may want this for the renderer's Settings-panel modal narrative. Defer.
  - The audit log's `session_id` per-call vs per-process: M05.E carries session_id per-call for v1.0 multi-session readiness; v0.1 single-session passes the live session id. Adequate; flagged here for the eventual M11+ multi-session work.
  - When does the `framework.budget.downshift_hook.tool_name` framework-tool-dispatch wire up — M5/M9 generators per the M04 carry-forward? M05 didn't address; M09 owns.

- **Recommended spec changes:** Bundle the items listed in "Missing items" + "Ambiguity" above into a post-M05 `docs(spec):` PR. Target: open before M06 Stage A authoring begins. The bundle now spans M02 + M03 + M04 + M05 spec items — 18+ entries — and warrants its own focused session.

### M05.V findings carry-forward

Per the closeout prompt's `<special_check>` (V→closeout handoff verification):

- **🔴 Finding #1 (L1 capability enforcer never invoked from production SDK)** — **RESOLVED via ADR-0009 waiver** (`a3f677f`). Architectural deferral to M06 Stage A. Carry-forward: M06 Stage A phase doc must include explicit `enforcer.check(agent_id, &needed)` deliverable before `provider.invoke`; M06.V Wire pass will trace and emit 🔴 if missing.
- **🔴 Finding #2 (L2a `narrow()` never invoked from sub-agent spawn path)** — **RESOLVED via ADR-0009 waiver** (same waiver covers both findings; M05.V Decision 1 recommended a single combined ADR). Architectural deferral to M06 Stage A. Carry-forward: M06 Stage A phase doc must include explicit `narrow(parent_grants, proposed_child_grants)` deliverable before `AgentSpawned` emission.
- **🟡 Finding #3 (Phase-doc-vs-implementation file drift)** — Carried forward to the 🟡 fix backlog above. The two files (`crates/runtime-sandbox/src/ipc.rs` + `crates/runtime-main/src/tier/transition.rs`) exist + are documented in CLAUDE.md §5 retroactively but not in their respective stages' X.2 Files to Change tables. M06.A `<read_prior_milestones>` references this finding. v1.6 `<phase_doc_inventory_audit>` extension proposal (inverse-direction check) is the protocol-level close.
- **🟢 Findings** — None this run. (M04.V's TD-001..004 entries remain in `docs/tech-debt.md` per the append-only ledger contract; no new TD-NNN entries from M05.V because no 🟢 findings.)

V→closeout handoff disposition: **clean**. 🔴 findings absorbed via ADR-0009 (the protocol's waiver lane, validated for the first time in v1.5). 🟡 finding carries into Carry-forward above. 🟢 findings absent. No work duplicated between V and closeout — V's role is contract-fidelity; closeout's role is product↔spec drift + protocol-iteration carry-forward. The structural-separation discipline held.

**Summary:** 47 stage-gotcha + stage-friction-event + Stage-V observation entries across A–F+V → 47 total dispositions:
- **resolved:** 30 (stage-local fixes that committed and have no forward applicability — phase-doc drift corrections, §12 own-technical-decisions resolutions, scope-downs, ADR-0009 waiver coverage, ContextType reconcile, etc.).
- **graduated:** 9 (recurring or forward-applicable patterns to `docs/gotchas.md`: typify-Eq #73; windows-sys-feature-by-parameter-type; tokio::io::duplex buffer-vs-payload; FFI-wrapper decomposition for coverage; refutable bindings break on enum variant addition; clippy doc_lazy_continuation; Zustand v5 useShallow; graphStore.clear() preserves user-preference; the V coverage-recheck convention).
- **kept:** 8 (still apply forward; stay in per-stage `<gotchas>` of M06+ stages that touch the same surface: typify-AgentId-private-field; canonical-AgentEvent re-export; rustdoc::broken_intra_doc_links #55 recurrence; Windows-local llvm-cov flake #56 recurrence; clippy unused-import false-positive; clippy lint clusters #21/#48 recurrence; significant_drop_tightening lock-held-across-IO; Vite cold-start #53 recurrence).
- **expired:** 0.

The 9 graduations populate `docs/gotchas.md` from the post-M04.6 ~66 entries → ~75 entries at the post-M05 protocol-iteration session ("M05.6"). M05 closeout's `<gotchas_graduation>` is the third to ship this section (M03.F first; M04.G second); the v1.5 protocol enforcement held cleanly.

Carry-forwards to the v1.6 STAGE-PROMPT-PROTOCOL.md protocol-iteration session (post-M05 — "M05.6"):

## M06 — MCP Basic (2026-05-16, Stage G commit on parent-milestone branch `claude/m06-mcp-basic`)

> Author: Claude (per `CLAUDE.md` §20)
> Stages aggregated: M06.A (ADR-0009 closure — L1 `enforcer.check` + L2a `narrow()` SDK wire-up + M05.V #3 X.2 truth-up + M04 carry-forwards), M06.B (`runtime-mcp` crate + rmcp 1.7.0 stdio/http transport + `schemas/mcp.v1.json` — new safety primitive ≥95%), M06.C (`runtime-mcp::client` lifecycle — install + per-server auth + connection mgmt + audit emissions), M06.D (§5a Tool Namespace Resolution + MCP dispatch through L1+L2a + ADR-0010 dependency inversion + 5 new event variants + audit), M06.E (renderer — MCPNode live wiring + Settings → MCP Servers Add/Remove/Test UI), M06.F (src-tauri `Arc<dyn McpToolDispatch>` injection + live `ProviderEvent::ToolUse` run-loop interception + gotcha #68 fix + ADR-0011 F-scope split), M06.V (in-band verifier — four-pass contract-fidelity check; 0🔴 / 2🟡 / 2🟢).
> Reviewed against: `agent-runtime-spec.md` §0–§0d, §1b, §2c, §3 (Phase 5 MCP Node), §5 (MCP Manager), §5a (Tool Namespace Resolution, locked WI-11), §6a (`on_capability_violation` reuse), §8.security L1+L2a (ADR-0009 closure), §13, §13.5; `schemas/*.v1.json` (mcp [new], event, capability, audit, framework, common); M06.A–F retrospectives + M06.V verifier retrospective + `M06-summary.md`; ADR-0006/0007/0008/0009/0010/0011; `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-001..006; M01 + M02 + M03 + M03.5 + M04 + M05 entries' Carry-forward backlogs.
> First milestone authored + executed under the v1.6 XML stage-prompt protocol. First to consume `<scope_change>` blocks at Stage V (the ADR-0011-into-V mechanism). First to run `<simplify_pass>` at Stage G. First to close an ADR-0008 waiver (ADR-0009) via a verified next-milestone production wire-up. Cumulative M06 diff ~14,657 / 102 across 91 files.

### Codebase deep dive (cumulative — M01 + M02 + M03 + M04 + M05 + M06)

M06 turns the M05 safety boundary into a working external-tooling surface and closes the one structural debt M05 left open. The headline: the ADR-0009 waiver (L1+L2a primitives shipped at M05 at 100% coverage but unwired to a production call site) is **closed with verified call sites** — `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/event_pipeline.rs:215` calls `enforcer.check` before the `ToolInvoked` push; `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/agent_sdk.rs:356` calls `narrow` before `AgentSpawned`. M06.V Wire-pass traces #1 + #2 confirm both SATISFIED. The new surface:

- **§8.security L1+L2a SDK wire-up** (Stage A). The M05.B enforcer + narrowing primitives wired into the production streaming dispatch path + spawn path. ~700 lines production + ~700 lines integration tests (4 L1 + 4 L2a). M05.V Finding #3 X.2 truth-up applied (the M05 phase-doc file-drift correction — the structural close moved the M05 phase doc into editable scope ONLY for the truth-up). The TDD-ordering lapse (Process Q3=2, G5 fail → maintainer override) is the negative case the v1.7 protocol exists to prevent.

- **`runtime-mcp` workspace crate** (Stage B; NEW safety primitive). `crates/runtime-mcp/src/{lib,error}.rs` + `transport/{mod,stdio,http,mock}.rs` + `schemas/mcp.v1.json`. rmcp 1.7.0 as the protocol library (stdio subprocess JSON-RPC + streamable HTTP per MCP spec 2025-11-25) behind a small async `Transport`/`Connection` trait pair. Mock-transport unit tests (M05.C1 `sandbox_ipc` archetype) + wiremock for HTTP failure paths (M02.C `anthropic_sse` archetype) + feature-gated reference-MCP-server smoke. Gate excludes `lib.rs` (pub-mod + re-exports) + `transport/stdio.rs` + `transport/http.rs` (rmcp-wrapper `connect()` happy paths need a real MCP peer — OS-call holdouts parallel to runtime-main `providers/anthropic.rs`). In-gate aggregate 99.02% at B end.

- **`runtime-mcp::client` lifecycle** (Stage C). `client/{mod,registry,auth,auth_keyring,lifecycle,error}.rs`. Add/Remove/Test/List; per-server auth via the M02 `key_store` keychain surface (`KeyringSecretStore`); connect/disconnect/health-ping; SQLite `mcp_servers` registry lit up (the M02-created table) via `Registry::open(path: &Path)` reusing `runtime_drone::db::init` for WAL+migrations — the path-agnostic-persistence archetype ported to a new crate. Two new OS-call holdouts excluded: `client/auth_keyring.rs` (real OS keychain; parallel to runtime-main `key_store.rs`) + `client/lifecycle.rs` (`spawn_health_pinger` tokio-spawn'd infinite loop delegating to the in-gate `run_health_pass`; parallel to drone `lib.rs`). Strict v1.7 two-commit TDD (red `2ff18ca` → impl `c9d3000`); in-gate aggregate 96.64% line. The `cargo llvm-cov clean`-before-measure gotcha (gotcha #81; ~10 min lost to a phantom 92.07% vs true 96.64%) graduated to CLAUDE.md §6.

- **§5a Tool Namespace Resolution + MCP dispatch** (Stage D). `crates/runtime-mcp/src/namespace/` + `dispatch.rs` + `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/mcp_dispatch.rs`. Canonical `<server>__<tool>` (split on first `__` from left); short-name alias when unambiguous; `mcp_aliases` framework-JSON override; `tool_alias_ambiguous` warning on connect/disconnect re-resolution. MCP dispatch routed through Stage A's L1+L2a gates. **ADR-0010 (dependency inversion)** filed: the concrete `McpDispatcher` depends on a `ConnectionResolver` trait so `runtime-main` doesn't take a hard `runtime-mcp` dependency cycle; the `<phase_doc_inventory_audit verified>` slot over-trusted symbol existence and missed the cycle at authoring time (→ `<construction_reachability_check>` proposal). 5 new event variants extend `schemas/event.v1.json`. namespace 99.11% / dispatch.rs 100% / aliases 100% / sdk/mcp_dispatch.rs 100%; runtime-mcp aggregate 97.16%.

- **Renderer MCP surface** (Stage E). `src/components/nodes/MCPNode.tsx` extended with a `mcp-node--conn-*` connection-status class family coexisting with the M03 `mcp-node--<NodeStatus>` lifecycle family (backward-compat constraint: the 5 M03 MCPNode tests pin the lifecycle axis); `src/components/MCPServerSettings.tsx` + `MCPServerAddModal.tsx` (Settings → MCP Servers Add/Remove/Test). `graphStore.ts` gains `currentMcpServers` (persistent across `clear()`, follows the M05.D `currentTier` pattern) + `activeMcpCalls` (per-session). Playwright Add-flow behavior test. Renderer vitest 97.98% line; `src/components` 98.18%.

- **Production wire completion** (Stage F; maintainer-inserted post-E). `AgentSdk` gains `Option<Arc<dyn McpToolDispatch>>` + a `with_mcp_dispatch` builder seam; `run_agent_with_provider_stream` intercepts `ProviderEvent::ToolUse` and dispatches MCP-first. The gotcha #68 fix: the run loop emits **agent_id-correct** `ToolInvoked`/`ToolResult` directly for the `Invoked` success path, leaving `apply_mcp_dispatch` + `McpDispatchOutcome::Invoked {server,tool,value}` + the D-frozen `mcp_dispatch_wire.rs` integration test untouched. **ADR-0011** filed: F.1's "running app end-to-end" over-reached the code reality; honest F scope = SDK seam + src-tauri injection seam (mock-verified per the `Arc<dyn _>` archetype); concrete `McpDispatcher` construction + live agent-loop exercise = explicit M07 carry-forward. Phase-doc F.5/F.6 forward-corrected (executed-stages-only grandfathering precedent — F was unexecuted).

What's solid (cumulative): M06 lands ONE new safety primitive (`runtime-mcp`) at ≥95% on the gated files and closes the ADR-0009 debt with verified production call sites — the ADR-0008 waiver→next-milestone-deliverable chain proven end-to-end for the first time. The `*_with` testable-seam, mock-transport, path-agnostic-persistence, and `Arc<dyn _>` injection-seam archetypes all ported cleanly to a new crate without divergence. Schema-as-source-of-truth held across 14 schemas (added `mcp.v1.json`; extended `event.v1.json`). Zero-telemetry boundary held end-to-end across all six work stages + V (rmcp + reqwest + tower add no phone-home; the MCP registry is local SQLite only). DCO sign-off + Conventional Commits held on every commit. The strict v1.7 two-commit TDD discipline (red commit → impl commit with verifiable empty test-diff invariant) ran cleanly at C/D/E/F after A's lapse — the protocol self-corrected mid-milestone (v1.7 merged PR #76 before D ran). `forbid(unsafe_code)` held for `runtime-mcp` (no `unsafe`; rmcp/reqwest/tower safe at the touched surfaces).

What's structurally weak and likely to compound: (1) **ADR-0011 M07 carry-forward** — `runtime-mcp` ships the §5a primitive + dispatch + lifecycle complete + tested, but the concrete `McpDispatcher` is not constructed in `src-tauri` (no `impl ConnectionResolver for McpClient`; no shell-constructed enforcer/resolver). The production driver is one milestone out, sharing a maintainer-adjudicated ADR root cause. M06.V Wire trace #11 correctly SPLIT (11a delivered/mock-verified, 11b M07). (2) **M06.V 🟡 #1 — §5a re-resolution-on-connect has no production driver.** The `connect_server`/`disconnect_server`/`re_evaluate_short_names` primitive is implemented + unit-tested but `McpClient` holds no `NamespaceResolver`; `tool_alias_ambiguous` emits on the *dispatch-time* Ambiguous outcome but not on lifecycle connect/disconnect. Same ADR-0011 root cause; not enumerated in any `<scope_change>` — must be explicitly added to M07's ADR-0011 carry-forward (b). (3) **`apply_mcp_dispatch` Invoked-arm is dead in production** — it builds events with `agent_id: String::new()` and is reachable only by the D-frozen wire test; the run loop special-cases `Invoked`. Documented inline (gotcha #68); the type-level fix (split `Blocked|Ambiguous` enum so the function can't take `Invoked`) perturbs the M06.V-verified D-frozen test, so it is deferred. (4) **Transport-helper copy-paste** — `rmcp_tool_to_mcp_tool` + `value_to_object` verbatim in `transport/stdio.rs` + `transport/http.rs`; drift trap when the rmcp `Tool` shape changes. (5) **`kind_to_ref`/`tier_to_ref` 3-module duplication** (`event_pipeline.rs` + `agent_sdk.rs` + `commands.rs`) — every new `CapabilityKind`/`Tier` variant requires 3 edits (clippy `non_exhaustive_patterns` catches a miss at compile time, so risk is bounded). (6) **`status: String` stringly-typed** in `McpServerRecord`/`McpServerSummary` where a `ServerStatus` enum belongs — no active bug (status is always written `"configured"` at insert; `run_health_pass` does not yet write `"connected"`/`"errored"`), but the lifecycle state machine evolves at M07. (7) **gotcha #56 Windows-local llvm-cov gap** — `drone_ipc_loopback.rs` nested-cargo build aborts under llvm-cov instrumentation on Windows; runtime-main ≥95% gate not locally measurable (TD-005). CI-Linux authoritative; runtime-mcp gate independently green. (8) **runtime-mcp `client/mod.rs` 94.64% + `client/registry.rs` 94.12% per-module** (in-gate aggregate 96.64% ≥95%) — error-path branches the MockTransport surface can't reach; injectable-failure SecretStore/Registry seam is the M06.D+ lift path documented in CLAUDE.md §5.

What surprised: time-box ratio 0.73× (M01 0.3× / M02 0.7× / M03 0.32× / M04 0.55× / M05 0.64× / M06 0.73×), converging toward 1× as archetypes settle; but novel-protocol Stage B came in at 0.35× (vs the assumed M02.C-anthropic_sse ~1× anchor) because rmcp's `ServiceExt::serve`/`Peer::call_tool` is far more abstracted than hand-rolled reqwest+SSE — recommend novel-protocol stages anchor ~0.4–0.5× when an abstracted SDK + full v1.6 slot coverage exist. The first `<simplify_pass>` (three parallel review agents vs the M06.A..HEAD cumulative diff) found the diff broadly clean — the proposal set was small and mostly mechanical, validating that the v1.6 slot suite + strict TDD keeps the cumulative diff in shape rather than accreting debt across stages.

### Adherence to spec

- ✅ **§8.security L1 — capability enforcer wired into the production dispatch path.** `enforcer.check(agent_id, &needed)` before the `ToolInvoked` push at `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/event_pipeline.rs:215`. **ADR-0009 closure trace #1 SATISFIED** (M06.V Wire pass — verified production call site). The M05.V Finding #1 🔴 (waived via ADR-0009) is RESOLVED at M06.A.
- ✅ **§8.security L2a — sub-agent narrowing wired into the production spawn path.** `narrow(parent_grants, proposed_child_grants)` before `AgentSpawned` emission at `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/agent_sdk.rs:356`. **ADR-0009 closure trace #2 SATISFIED** (M06.V Wire pass). The M05.V Finding #2 🔴 (waived via ADR-0009) is RESOLVED at M06.A. 4 L1 + 4 L2a integration tests replace the M05.B `capability_enforcer_smoke.rs` "what-SDK-will-call" stand-in.
- ✅ **§5 MCP Manager — add by URL/local path, test-connection, connect/disconnect, list tools, per-server auth, health monitoring.** Code at `crates/runtime-mcp/src/{transport,client}/`. Matches spec §5 "Manager Capabilities" (Connect/Disconnect + Tool Discovery + Health Monitoring + Multi-Server + per-server auth in keychain not session state). rmcp 1.7.0 stdio + streamable HTTP per MCP spec 2025-11-25.
- ✅ **§5a Tool Namespace Resolution — canonical `<server>__<tool>`, short-name alias, `mcp_aliases` override, server-names-cannot-contain-`__`, split on first `__` from left.** Code at `crates/runtime-mcp/src/namespace/`. Matches the WI-11-locked algorithm steps 1–4 verbatim. Step 5 (re-resolution on connect/disconnect emits `tool_alias_ambiguous`) — the **primitive** is implemented + unit-tested; the **production driver** is absent (see ⚠️ below — M06.V 🟡 #1).
- ✅ **§3 Phase 5 MCP Node in Graph — server name, connection-status live indicator, active tool calls.** Code at `src/components/nodes/MCPNode.tsx`. The `mcp-node--conn-*` class family carries connection status; `activeMcpCalls` drives the active-call indicator. Tool-call-count / avg-latency / error-rate hover detail is v1.0 (spec §3 MCPNode lists them; phase doc E scoped the live-status subset).
- ✅ **§6a `on_capability_violation` reuse for the MCP-deny path.** The `Blocked` MCP outcome routes through the existing M04.E `await_capability_violation_hitl` seam (ADR-0007) — no new modal, no new HITL primitive. Code at `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/agent_sdk.rs:499`.
- ✅ **§13.5 audit emissions — every MCP lifecycle event appends to `skills.audit.jsonl`.** `mcp_installed` / `mcp_uninstalled` / `mcp_auth_granted` / `mcp_request_blocked` via the M05.E `AuditWriter` (consumes the existing primitive; no new audit surface). Code at `crates/runtime-mcp/src/client/mod.rs` + `sdk/mcp_dispatch.rs`.
- ✅ **§0d Release scope — single-session, Anthropic-only, STANDARD mode, `fresh_context_per_task`, Windows-only (CI all three OSes).** No multi-session MCP registry; MCP tools dispatch through the existing `AnthropicProvider`; no mode-aware MCP gate; per-installation registry only.
- ✅ **Schema-as-source-of-truth — `schemas/mcp.v1.json` authored hand-first + `cargo xtask regenerate-types`; 5 new event variants extend `event.v1.json`.** `regenerate-types --check` exit 0 at every stage pre-flight.
- ✅ **`forbid(unsafe_code)` held for `runtime-mcp`.** No `unsafe`; rmcp + reqwest + tower safe at the touched surfaces. Workspace lint unchanged.
- ⚠️ **§5a step 5 — re-resolution-on-connect/disconnect has no production driver** (M06.V Wire 🟡 #1). `McpClient` holds no `NamespaceResolver` field; `re_evaluate_short_names`/`connect_server`/`disconnect_server` are implemented + unit-tested but have zero production consumers. `tool_alias_ambiguous` emits on the *dispatch-time* `Ambiguous` outcome (`sdk/mcp_dispatch.rs` → `graphStore.ts`) but NOT on lifecycle connect/disconnect. Same ADR-0011 root cause as the M07 concrete-construction carry-forward. **Not 🔴** (primitive delivered+tested; root cause = an already-accepted ADR's named carry-forward) but NOT explicitly enumerated in any `<scope_change>` — carried forward to M07 Stage A with mandatory ADR-0011 (b) enumeration. M07.V Wire trace #6 is the expected endpoint.
- ⚠️ **ADR-0011 M07 carry-forward — concrete `McpDispatcher` not constructed in the shell.** No `impl ConnectionResolver for McpClient`; no shell-constructed `CapabilityEnforcer`/`NamespaceResolver`; `run_smoke_session` passes `None` for dispatch. The §5 dispatch primitive ships complete+tested; the production driver + first live agent-with-tools loop = explicit M07 (a)–(d) carry-forward. M06.V Wire trace #11 SPLIT: 11a (seam + injection seam, mock-verified) DELIVERED; 11b (concrete construction + live exercise) = M07, NOT a 🔴. Maintainer-adjudicated via ADR-0011.
- ⚠️ **`apply_mcp_dispatch` Invoked-arm dead in production** (simplify-pass CQ-2/reuse-5). Builds events with `agent_id: String::new()`; reachable only by the D-frozen `mcp_dispatch_wire.rs` test. The run loop special-cases `Invoked` to emit agent_id-correct events (gotcha #68 fix, documented inline). The type-safety improvement (split `Blocked|Ambiguous` enum) perturbs the M06.V-verified D-frozen test — deferred to M07 alongside the `ServerStatus` enum + the live-dispatch wiring (TD-008).
- ⚠️ **`status: String` stringly-typed** in `McpServerRecord`/`McpServerSummary` (simplify-pass CQ-6). A `ServerStatus` enum belongs here; no active bug (always `"configured"` at insert; `run_health_pass` does not yet write status transitions). Land the enum with M07's health-ping state machine (TD-009).
- ⚠️ **Spec §5 Health Monitoring says "Drone pings MCP servers on heartbeat cycle"; M06 ships an in-`runtime-mcp` `spawn_health_pinger` (30s default), not a drone-driven ping.** The v0.1 architecture has no drone↔MCP path; the in-crate health pinger is the merged-contract reading. Spec §5 should pin the v0.1 in-crate-pinger-vs-drone-pinger distinction. Bundle into the post-M05/M06 `docs(spec):` PR.
- ⚠️ **Spec §5 "Dead server → node goes offline → auto-retry with backoff" + "Configurable retry policy per server" — M06 ships rmcp-default reconnect only.** Phase doc §"What's not in scope" explicitly defers sophisticated auto-reconnect + per-server retry policy to v1.0. Spec §5 should note the v0.1 rmcp-defaults scope. Bundle.
- ⚠️ **`spawn_health_pinger` docstring claims "abort on `McpClient` drop"** (simplify-pass EFF-9) — false: `McpClient` holds no `JoinHandle`; the spawned loop holds an `Arc<McpClient>` so the client is never dropped while the loop runs. No leak (Arc keeps it alive), but the "abort on drop" guarantee is untrue. Docstring-only correction (TD-010 or simplify-approved commit — see Simplify pass subsection).
- ⚠️ **`McpClient::new` vs `new_with_audit` dual constructor + `McpDispatcher::new` 5-arg constructor** (simplify-pass CQ-3/CQ-10) — premature dual-constructor / builder-vs-positional inconsistency. Pure-refactor, no behavior change; deferred to tech-debt.
- ⚠️ **Spec §4a `hook_*` vs codebase `verify_*` naming** (M04.V Decision 2, surfaced at M06.A) — maintainer-decision item. Default recommendation: update spec §4a text to `verify_*` (M04+M05+M06.A consistent on `verify_*`). STAYS DEFERRED to the post-M05/M06 `docs(spec):` PR pending maintainer sign-off; not blocking.
- ❌ **None observed.** No code ships behavior the spec forbids or vice versa. All deviations are forward-compat (the §5a re-resolution + concrete-dispatcher production drivers ship as tested primitives, drivers deferred via the maintainer-adjudicated ADR-0011 chain), v0.1-scoped (rmcp-default reconnect; in-crate health pinger; live-status MCPNode subset), documentation-side (spec §5 health/retry pinning bundled), or honest debt (the documented-by-design `apply_mcp_dispatch` Invoked split; stringly-typed status with no active bug).

### Spec review (forward-looking)

- **Missing items:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §5 — pin the v0.1 health-monitoring architecture: in-`runtime-mcp` `spawn_health_pinger` (30s default), NOT a drone-driven heartbeat ping; "auto-retry with backoff" + "configurable retry policy per server" are v1.0 (v0.1 = rmcp-default reconnect). Bundle into the post-M05/M06 `docs(spec):` PR.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §5a step 5 — note that v0.1 emits `tool_alias_ambiguous` on the *dispatch-time* Ambiguous outcome; the *connect/disconnect re-resolution* driver lands at M07 (ADR-0011 (b) carry-forward). Pin so M07.V Wire trace #6 has a spec endpoint.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §5a — server-name constraints: M06 ships split-on-first-`__`-from-left + server-names-cannot-contain-`__`; the spec §5a step 4 already states this. Confirm whether kebab-case-only / underscore-banned server-name validation is owed (M06 phase doc G.3 flagged this as a spec-review item) — recommend the spec pin the exact server-name charset.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §3 MCPNode — clarify which MCPNode hover-detail fields (tool-call count, avg latency, error rate) are v0.1 vs v1.0 (M06 ships the live-status subset).
  - All prior-milestone "Missing items" (§4b severity matrix, 4-kind `request_capability`, §8.security L1/L2a/L3/L4/L5 pins, §4a `hook_*`/`verify_*`, §11 sessions FSM diagram, §2a budget shape, §1d reconnect surface, §2c `signature_delta`/`ping`, §3a `plan_loop.rs`, model deprecation policy) — STILL OPEN; folded into the post-M05/M06 `docs(spec):` PR (now ~22 entries; warrants its own focused session before M07 Stage A authoring).
- **Contradictions:** None observed. M06 deviations are forward-compat (ADR-0011 production-driver deferral) or v0.1-scope-locked (rmcp-default reconnect; in-crate pinger).
- **Ambiguity:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §5 — health-ping cadence: spec says "on heartbeat cycle" (drone's cadence); M06 ships a standalone 30s default. Lock the v0.1 choice.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §5a — does an `mcp_aliases` entry pointing at a now-disconnected server resolve, error, or silently pass through? M06 ships pass-through-to-resolution (alias is a name rewrite; resolution then fails if the canonical target is absent). Spec doesn't pin; bundle.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §13.5 — MCP audit `kind` values (`mcp_installed`/`mcp_uninstalled`/`mcp_auth_granted`/`mcp_request_blocked`): spec doesn't enumerate the MCP-specific audit kinds. M06 ships these four; lock in spec §13.5.
- **Open questions:**
  - When does `impl ConnectionResolver for McpClient` + the shell-constructed enforcer/resolver land — M07 Stage A per ADR-0011, or does M07's registry-import scope reshuffle the construction site? M07 prep should lock the construction-root placement (same open-question shape as M05→M06's "where does plan_loop land").
  - The `ServerStatus` enum + `run_health_pass` writing `"connected"`/`"errored"` to the `mcp_servers.status` column — M07 health-ping state machine. Currently status is write-once `"configured"`.
  - Health-ping batched-SQL (`UPDATE … WHERE name IN (…)` vs K sequential per pass) — efficiency-pass EFF-4; defer to M07 when multi-server is exercised.
- **Recommended spec changes:** Bundle §5 health/retry pinning + §5a step-5 driver-timing + §5a server-name charset + §3 MCPNode v0.1/v1.0 split + §13.5 MCP audit-kind enumeration into the post-M05/M06 `docs(spec):` PR (target: open before M07 Stage A authoring; now ~22 entries spanning M02–M06).

### Fix backlog

Severity is non-elastic. Critical = "must fix before M07 starts."

- 🔴 **Critical** (must fix before M07 starts): **None.** All MVP §M6 acceptance criteria met. ADR-0009 closure SATISFIED with verified production call sites (M06.V traces #1+#2). M06.V produced 0🔴. The one hard-gate violation (M06.A G5 TDD-ordering) was a documented maintainer override per `CLAUDE.md` §12 (project process governance is user-domain) with the structural close (v1.7 `<tdd_discipline>`) merged mid-milestone (PR #76, commit `2649c36`, before D ran) — a protocol-fit gap, not a work-correctness gap; no shipped behavior is incorrect. Aggregate axis means healthy (Process 38.0/40, Product 38.17/40, Pattern 30.17/35).

Candidates: `<construction_reachability_check>` slot (M06.D + M06.F — the deepest M06 insight); `<wire_signature_audit>` slot (M06.E); `<wire_trace_vs_adr_reconcile>` authoring check (M06.V Decision 6); verifier-template codification of the "primitive-delivered-but-driver-deferred-via-accepted-ADR ⇒ 🟡-mandatory-enumeration" rule (M06.V Decision 6); M07.V `--features integration` reference-MCP-server smoke requirement (M06.V Decision 7); the phase-doc-authoring pre-PR-checklist meta-iteration (still recurring — 5/6 M06 work stages hit phase-doc drift caught at pre-flight).
  - **M06 phase-doc authoring-rigor signal — first-class, 5 instances.** Owner: docs / protocol. Phase-doc-vs-codebase drift surfaced at pre-flight in **5 of 6 M06 work stages** — A (`graphStore.test.ts` path + 3-vs-4 schema kinds, pre-existing M05.A class), B (`NonEmptyString` $ref non-existence + rmcp API drift), D (ADR-0010 cross-crate dependency cycle the `<phase_doc_inventory_audit verified>` slot over-trusted), E (renderer pseudocode drifted from the shipped store shape), F (F.1 over-framed an injection whose ctor inputs don't exist in-shell → ADR-0011). Every instance was caught by the v1.6 slot suite at pre-flight (no instance reached code), but the *recurrence rate itself* is the signal: per-stage slots catch drift; they do not prevent it. The structural fix is a **phase-doc-authoring pre-PR checklist** that runs the v1.5/v1.6 slot greps + the `<construction_reachability_check>`/`<wire_signature_audit>`/`<wire_trace_vs_adr_reconcile>` proposals BEFORE the milestone phase-doc PR opens (recurring observation M05.A→M06.F; structurally distinct from any single per-stage slot). Elevated here from the M06.6 bullet's sub-clause to a first-class backlog item per the M06.G immutability review. Target: M06.6 protocol-iteration session, as its headline deliverable.
  - **CLAUDE.md slim + §5 per-module baseline-ledger externalization.** Owner: docs. CLAUDE.md §5 has grown a per-milestone per-module coverage-baseline ledger (drone → runtime-main → runtime-sandbox → tier/audit → **runtime-mcp** at M06, plus the M06.G CQ-1 `transport/mod.rs` baseline-shift note) that is now a multi-paragraph inline block read into every session's context. The baseline ledger is reference data, not execution protocol — it belongs in a dedicated `docs/coverage-baselines.md` (or `docs/gap-analysis.md`-adjacent ledger) that CLAUDE.md §5 *links* rather than *inlines*. M06 is the fifth primitive added to the inline ledger; the trend compounds every milestone and dilutes the load-bearing §4/§6/§8 rules with append-only coverage trivia. Target: M06.6 (paired with the protocol-iteration session, since both touch the docs-architecture surface). Pattern bit: this is the cumulative-context-bloat analogue of the append-only gap-analysis discipline — the fix is externalize-and-link, not edit-in-place.
  - **`ci-failures.txt` 4th-recurrence cleanup.** Owner: ops / repo hygiene. A `ci-failures.txt` working-artifact has recurred uncommitted-but-present across milestone closeouts (now its 4th recurrence at M06.G). It is a local CI-triage scratch file that should be (a) `.gitignore`d if it is a legitimate local triage aid, or (b) deleted and its function folded into the `docs/gotchas.md` #56 / TD-005 CI-parity tracking if it is stale. Recurrence-without-resolution is itself the debt. Target: bundle into the gotcha #56 / TD-005 focused CI-infrastructure session (same owner, same surface).
  - **`<red_phase_gate>` v1.8 protocol candidate.** Owner: docs / protocol. v1.7 `<tdd_discipline strict="true">` (PR #76) mandates the red-commit-before-impl two-commit *convention* and M06.C validated it empirically (~10% overhead, structural defense vs gotcha #66). The next hardening is a **structural gate** (not just a convention): a `<red_phase_gate>` that makes the red-phase commit + its user-approval a *blocking* CI/protocol checkpoint (the impl commit's verifiable invariant `git diff <red-sha>..<impl-sha> -- '**/tests/**'` is EMPTY, enforced by a CI check, not just asserted in the commit body). M06.A's G5 TDD-ordering failure is the negative case the *convention* alone did not prevent (it relied on agent self-discipline); the v1.8 gate closes the residual "agent silently edits tests to pass" hole structurally. Target: v1.8 protocol-iteration (post-M06.6), cited from M06.A's retro + the TDAD arXiv:2603.17973 structural-enforcement evidence already in CLAUDE.md §5.
  - **`docs/gotchas.md` consolidation from M06 closeout.** Owner: docs. Graduate the M06 `<gotchas_graduation>` items below (gotcha #81 `cargo llvm-cov clean`-before-measure already landed in CLAUDE.md §6; confirm the gotchas.md numbering at the M06.6 session).

Now demonstrated 4× (M04.C ApprovalSeam + M04.E HitlSeam + M05.F capability-violation modal + M06.F MCP-Blocked→`await_capability_violation_hitl` reuse). - **resolved:** 9 (stage-local fixes / own-technical-decisions / calibration refinements / V→carry-forward absorptions with no recurring-pattern residue).

- **kept:** 6 (still apply forward in M07+ stages touching the same surface: typify #43 recurrence, clippy #21 cluster, M04.V Dec 2 spec-decision, gotcha #68 [resolved at F, residue is a TD not a gotcha], gotcha #56 recurrence, M06.6 phase-doc-authoring discipline).
- **expired:** 0.

3 graduations already RESOLVED at the protocol level mid-milestone (v1.7 `<tdd_discipline>` PR #76 + gotcha #81 in CLAUDE.md §6) — the protocol self-correcting before M06 even closed. The remaining 5 graduations populate the M06.6 protocol-iteration session (`<construction_reachability_check>`, `<wire_signature_audit>`, `<wire_trace_vs_adr_reconcile>`, verifier-template codification, M07.V integration-smoke). M06's `<gotchas_graduation>` is the fourth to ship this section (M03.F first; M04.G second; M05.G third; v1.5+ protocol enforcement held cleanly).

### Simplify pass outcome (v1.6 `<simplify_pass>` — first milestone to run this at closeout)

Per the M06.G `<deliverables><simplify_pass>` + `<special_check>`. The `simplify` skill ran three parallel read-only review agents (code-reuse / code-quality / efficiency) against the M06.A..HEAD cumulative diff (`030089f^..HEAD`, 91 files / +14,657 / −102). **This was a proposal pass — `<approval_required>true</approval_required>` — no changes auto-applied.** Aggregate verdict from all three agents: **the cumulative M06 diff is broadly clean** (good layering, the ADR-0011 scope boundary cleanly respected, all hot-path choices correct for v0.1 single-session scale). No high-severity reuse issues; the one "high" code-quality flag (`apply_mcp_dispatch` Invoked-arm) is a documented-by-design gotcha #68 / D-frozen-test constraint, not accidental debt.

Refactor proposals surfaced (13 distinct, deduplicated across agents):

| ID | Proposal | Sev | Recommendation |
|---|---|---|---|
| CQ-1 | `rmcp_tool_to_mcp_tool` + `value_to_object` copy-pasted verbatim in `transport/stdio.rs` + `transport/http.rs` → move to a shared `transport` location | Med | **Apply now** — mechanical, zero behavior change, removes a concrete rmcp-shape drift trap |
| EFF-9 | `spawn_health_pinger` docstring claims "abort on `McpClient` drop" — false (client holds no `JoinHandle`; loop holds an `Arc`) | Med | **Apply now** — docstring-only correction, no behavior change |
| CQ-4 | `kind_to_ref`/`tier_to_ref` duplicated across `event_pipeline.rs` + `agent_sdk.rs` + `commands.rs` → extract to `sdk` shared location | Med | **Maintainer's call** — pure extract, but touches the M06.V-verified ADR-0009 wire path; safe but on a safety-primitive surface |
| CQ-2 / reuse-5 | `apply_mcp_dispatch` Invoked-arm dead in production (empty `agent_id`); type-level fix = split `Blocked\|Ambiguous` enum | High* | **Defer to M07** — perturbs the M06.V-verified D-frozen `mcp_dispatch_wire.rs` test; bundle with the ADR-0011 live-dispatch wire + `ServerStatus` enum |
| CQ-6 | `status: String` stringly-typed in `McpServerRecord`/`McpServerSummary` → `ServerStatus` enum | Med | **Defer to M07** — land with the health-ping state machine that writes `"connected"`/`"errored"` |
| CQ-3 / CQ-10 | `McpClient::new` vs `new_with_audit` dual constructor + `McpDispatcher::new` 5-arg vs builder inconsistency | Low | **Defer to tech-debt** — pure refactor, no runtime cost |
| reuse-1 | `now_unix_ms` defined a 3rd time (`registry.rs`) — `audit::entry::now_unix_ms` already in scope | Low | **Defer to tech-debt** — i64/u64 cast difference; cosmetic |
| reuse-7 | `ipc.ts` `McpTool`/`McpServerSummary` hand-written non-schema mirrors | Low | **Defer to tech-debt** — documented deliberate; schema-coverage gap (these are `transport`/`client` response types, not in `mcp.v1.json`) |
| EFF-1 | per-`ToolUse` `mcp_aliases` HashMap→BTreeMap clone in `try_mcp_dispatch` | Med | **Defer to tech-debt** — warm path, small constant at v0.1 alias counts; one-line lift (cache outside the loop) |
| EFF-2/3 | `disconnect_server` provably-empty double O(S*T) scan (+ `connect_server` double scan) | Low | **Defer to tech-debt** — cold path; comment documents the invariant |
| EFF-4 | `run_health_pass` K sequential SQLite `UPDATE` vs 1 batched | Med | **Defer to M07** — zero cost at v0.1 single-server; land with multi-server exercise |
| EFF-5 | `tool_result` runs `activeMcpCalls` filter even for non-MCP results (no empty-guard / no ref-equality) | Low | **Defer to tech-debt** — small map; add an empty-guard early-return |
| EFF-6 | `MCPNode` two `useGraphStore` subscriptions where one combined `useShallow` selector suffices | Low | **Defer to tech-debt** — immaterial at v0.1 node counts |

**Recommended maintainer-approved subset (focused refactor commit before PR opens):** CQ-1 (transport-helper dedupe) + EFF-9 (docstring correction). Both are mechanical / docstring-only with zero behavior change and remove concrete drift/correctness-doc hazards; both are inside `runtime-mcp` (not the M06.V-verified ADR-0009 wire path). CQ-4 is offered as a maintainer's-call addition (clean extract, but on the safety-primitive wire surface — defer if the maintainer prefers the M06 PR diff stay scoped to V-verified surfaces). **All non-approved proposals defer to `docs/tech-debt.md` as TD-007..TD-013** (entries appended in the same closeout commit cluster, final disposition gated on the maintainer's subset decision per the approval surface).

> **Maintainer decision (M06.G):** approved subset = **CQ-1 + EFF-9**. CQ-4 deferred (→ TD-007); all other non-approved proposals → `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-007..TD-013 (appended this closeout). The focused-refactor commit lands on `claude/m06-mcp-basic` BEFORE the M06 PR opens and becomes the FINAL commit on the branch (the gap-analysis commit lands one prior, per the G.5 `<context>`).
>
> **Per-module baseline shift from CQ-1 (recorded per CLAUDE.md §5).** Consolidating `rmcp_tool_to_mcp_tool` + `value_to_object` from the gate-*excluded* `transport/stdio.rs`+`transport/http.rs` into the in-gate `transport/mod.rs` moved 9 lines of `rmcp_tool_to_mcp_tool` (an rmcp-wrapper helper exercised only via the `connect()` happy-path — the same OS-call-holdout class as the files it moved from) into a gated file. `transport/mod.rs` per-module line coverage shifts from the M06.C-baseline 95.35% to 87.50%; the 3 `value_to_object` unit tests moved with the helper (100% on `value_to_object`), but `rmcp_tool_to_mcp_tool` has no dedicated unit test (it never did — only the excluded `connect()` path exercises it). **The runtime-mcp in-gate aggregate stays compliant at 96.50% line ≥ 95% (gate exit 0; was 97.16% at M06.V — the delta is the relocation of excluded-class lines into the gate, not new untested code).** Carry-forward to M07: either add a `rmcp_tool_to_mcp_tool` unit test (construct an `rmcp::model::Tool` fixture) to lift `transport/mod.rs` back toward its baseline, or extend the runtime-mcp `--ignore-filename-regex` rationale in CLAUDE.md §5 to note the helper is the same OS-call-holdout class regardless of which transport-module file it lives in.
>
> If the maintainer had approved zero refactors, the gap-analysis commit would have been the final commit and all 13 proposals would defer to tech-debt.

## M07 — Registry Import (2026-05-19, Stage G commit on parent-milestone branch `claude/m07-registry-import`)

> Author: Claude (per `CLAUDE.md` §20)
> Stages aggregated: M07.A (M06 gap-analysis carry-forward absorption — TD-002/005/006, M04 plan_loop descope, M05 enforcer TierForbidden, M06.V 🟡#2 X.2 truth-up + the ADR-0011 `<construction_reachability_check>` groundwork), M07.B (`skills.lock` integrity primitive + `schemas/skills-lock.v1.json` + `artifact_hash_mismatch` event — new safety primitive, ADR-0014), M07.C (import-pipeline backend — URL/file fetch → schema-validate → L3 → tier-gate → install → lock; §15c; ADR-0005 `share_provenance`), M07.D1 (ADR-0011 (a)–(c) — `impl ConnectionResolver for McpClient` + concrete `McpDispatcher` ctor in `src-tauri` + CQ-6 `ServerStatus` enum + migration 003 + EFF-4 batched health pass), M07.D2 (ADR-0011 (d) — multi-turn agent-with-tools loop + `token_usage` projector + surgical CQ-2 `RenderableOutcome`), M07.E (Builder Import panel renderer + ADR-0015 enriched `ImportOutcome`), M07.V (in-band verifier — four passes; 1🔴 / 4🟡 / 1🟢).
> Reviewed against: `agent-runtime-spec.md` §0–§0d, Phase 7 §2152–2211 (registry import + `skills.lock`), §5a (Tool Namespace Resolution re-resolution), §8.security L1/L3/L4, §15/§15c/§15d (artifact metadata + `compatible_os` + `requires_secrets`), §2c.3, §13 (zero telemetry); `schemas/*.v1.json` (added `skills-lock.v1.json`; extended `event.v1.json`); M07.A–E retrospectives + M07.V verifier retrospective + `M07-summary.md`; ADR-0005/0008/0010/0011/0012/0013/0014/0015/0016; `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-001..013; `docs/coverage-policy.md` §A–§D; M01–M06 gap-analysis entries + the M06.5 IRL fix-cycle (`M06.5-summary.md`).
> First milestone authored + executed end-to-end under the v1.8 stage-prompt protocol (the three new audit slots `<construction_reachability_check>` / `<wire_trace_vs_adr_reconcile>` / `<wire_signature_audit>` used where they bite; first v1.8 Stage V with the **mandatory** `--features integration` reference-MCP-server smoke). First to discharge the largest open architectural carry-forward (ADR-0011 (a)–(d)). First milestone whose Stage V produced a 🔴 routed via a fix-cycle-scheduling waiver (ADR-0016 → M07.5). Cumulative M07 diff ~9,546 / 372 across 78 files (`e677d93..HEAD`).

### Codebase deep dive (cumulative — M01 + M02 + M03 + M04 + M05 + M06 + M07)

M07 turns the M06 external-tooling surface into a registry-import feature and closes the largest structural debt the ledger carried — the ADR-0011 (a)–(d) concrete-construction carry-forward. The headline: the `runtime-mcp` §5 dispatch primitive, complete-but-unconstructed since M06, now has a real production construction graph — `src-tauri/src/commands.rs::build_mcp_dispatcher` constructs a concrete `McpDispatcher` from a Tauri-managed `Arc<McpClient>` (now `impl ConnectionResolver`), a real `NamespaceResolver`, and a real `CapabilityEnforcer`; the multi-turn `AgentSdk::run_agent` loop consumes it. The new surface:

- **`skills.lock` integrity primitive** (Stage B; NEW safety primitive). `crates/runtime-main/src/skills_lock/` + `schemas/skills-lock.v1.json` + the `artifact_hash_mismatch` event variant. SRI-encoded SHA-256 (`sha256-<base64>`) content hash; canonical sorted serialization producing a byte-identical lock file regardless of install order (spec §2204 cross-machine reproducibility); `verify` returns `HashMismatch` on drift. Path-agnostic (`&Path`; the Tauri shell resolves the framework-root path) — the `audit::file_path` archetype. ADR-0014. Module `skills_lock/mod.rs` 98.15% line ≥95.
- **Import-pipeline backend** (Stage C). `crates/runtime-main/src/import/` — each stage an injected-seam pure function (`fetch_with`/`validate`/`l3_with`/`tier_gate`/`install_with`) composed by `import_artifact_with`; the only OS-call wrapper is `import/fetch.rs` (real `reqwest` GET, Category-3 holdout, four-mirror-synced exclusion). Reuses M05 `runtime-sandbox` (L3) + L4 `tier` + M07.B `skills_lock` + the M06 `runtime_mcp::Registry` (dependency-inverted around the `runtime-mcp → runtime-main` Cargo cycle — the ADR-0010 archetype, concrete `RegistryAdapter` in `src-tauri`). §15c `compatible_os` mismatch blocks before L3; ADR-0005 `share_provenance` is runtime-to-runtime only (`rebake_changes: []`).
- **ADR-0011 (a)–(c) concrete construction** (Stage D1). `crates/runtime-mcp/src/client/connection_resolver.rs` (`impl ConnectionResolver for McpClient`); `build_mcp_dispatcher` in `src-tauri`; the §5a re-resolution driver `McpDispatcher::on_server_connected`/`on_server_disconnected` (M06.V Dec-6 reconcile honored — the trace is on `McpDispatcher`, not `McpClient`). CQ-6: `status: String` → the generated `ServerStatus` enum, with migration `003_mcp_server_status.sql` realigning the stale `000_initial.sql` `CHECK` constraint. EFF-4: `run_health_pass` → one batched `update_health_batch`.
- **ADR-0011 (d) agent-with-tools loop** (Stage D2). `AgentSdk::run_agent` re-streams the provider after every dispatched tool (message-history re-streaming — no new `LLMProvider` method); `ProviderEvent::Usage → AgentEvent::TokenUsage →` the new `runtime-drone/src/token_usage.rs` projector (third projector, same `handle_write_signal` transaction as `vdr`+`plan_projector`; no new `DroneCommand`, no §11 ADR). The assembled regression `agent_with_tools_loop_persists_signals_and_token_usage` drives the real loop + real drone subprocess + concrete `McpDispatcher` and asserts `token_usage > 0` — **closing the M06.5 `token_usage = 0` finding in production.** Surgical CQ-2: `RenderableOutcome`/`apply_renderable` (cannot express `Invoked`).
- **Builder Import panel** (Stage E). `src/components/ImportPanel.tsx` — paste-GitHub-raw-URL form + the §M7 tier-gate review modal (capability disclosure + L3 report + ADR-0005 trust line + §15d secrets) + the `artifact_hash_mismatch` Reinstall/Remove prompt. ADR-0015 additively enriches `ImportOutcome` with data `import_artifact_with` already computes.

What's solid (cumulative): M07 lands ONE new safety primitive (`skills_lock`) at ≥95% and discharges ADR-0011 (a)–(d) — the M06.F seam over-reach corrected and closed across D1/D2 with a V-readable construction graph. Schema-as-source-of-truth held (added `skills-lock.v1.json`; extended `event.v1.json`; `regenerate-types --check` clean every stage). Zero-telemetry held (the import fetch GETs only the user-supplied URL — Hard Rule 4). `forbid(unsafe_code)` held. Strict v1.8 two-commit TDD ran cleanly on every code stage (the `'**/tests/**'`-EMPTY invariant verified; binary-crate scoped-diff variant at D2/E). The v1.8 audit slots earned their place — the A→D1→D2 `<construction_reachability_check>` chain and E's 6-drift `<wire_signature_audit>` both worked as designed. The mandatory `--features integration` smoke ran 1/1.

What's structurally weak and likely to compound: (1) **M07.V 🔴 #1 — `tier_gate` defined but never invoked.** A Novice "Reject" does not roll back the `skills.lock` entry (or, for `mcp_server`, the registry row) — spec §8.security L4 contract drift. Waived to the M07.5 fix-cycle via ADR-0016 (see Fix backlog; blast radius bounded — no production path loads/executes an imported artifact in v0.1). (2) **`EnforcerGate::check` is a tautological capability gate** (simplify-pass CQ-M07-1) — `src-tauri/src/commands.rs:1071–1075` constructs a fresh `CapabilityEnforcer`, grants exactly the `decl` it then checks, so the import-fetch network check always passes; it functions as a host-string validator, not an L1 capability gate, and its doc comment overstates it as "default-deny + domain scope". No active security gap (Hard Rule 4 holds structurally — `fetch_with` GETs only the user-supplied URL), but the phase-doc-intended L1 enforcement is decorative. (3) **The Dec-6 cluster** — `skills_lock::verify`, `McpDispatcher::on_server_connected`, and the agent-with-tools loop are all delivered + tested but have no production *driver/trigger* in v0.1 (no production code path loads or executes an imported artifact — the smoke session is no-tools); all three converge on M08.A. (4) **The file-picker UI is not shipped** (MVP §M7 acceptance criterion) — backend accepts `ImportSource::File`, the renderer surface is M08.A. (5) **`apply_mcp_dispatch` Invoked-arm + `status` stringly-typed** — TD-008 was partly addressed (CQ-2 surgical split shipped `RenderableOutcome`; the dead `Invoked` arm in `apply_mcp_dispatch` remains, reachable only by the D-frozen test); TD-009 CLOSED (CQ-6 `ServerStatus` enum shipped at D1).

What surprised: D1's CQ-6 — phase-doc-framed as the "small" item — was the milestone's largest single source of work (a stale DB `CHECK` mirror forced a table-rebuild migration rippling into 3 in-source test blocks across 2 crates). D2's Windows `link.exe` LNK1xxx errors were disk exhaustion (2 GB free), not a code/dependency-graph defect — a multi-cycle misdiagnosis, retracted; `cargo clean` freed 87.9 GiB and cleared it. Time-box ratio (deliverable-time, excluding D2's environment detour) ~0.75×, in the M06 ~0.7× band.

### Adherence to spec

- ✅ **§2181–2214 `skills.lock` — per-framework artifact-integrity ledger; hash-on-load; reproducible across machines.** Code at `crates/runtime-main/src/skills_lock/` + `schemas/skills-lock.v1.json`. SRI-encoded SHA-256; canonical byte-identical serialization (the `canonical_serialization_is_byte_identical_regardless_of_install_order` test pins §2204); `verify` → `HashMismatch` → `AgentEvent::ArtifactHashMismatch`. ADR-0014. The lock key is `installed` per spec §2200 (the phase doc B.3.1 said `entries` — surfaced pre-red, maintainer chose the spec-faithful key).
- ✅ **§2152–2211 / MVP §M7 — import an artifact by GitHub-raw URL or local file → fetch → schema-validate → L3 → tier-gate review → install → lock.** Backend code at `crates/runtime-main/src/import/` + `src-tauri/src/commands.rs::import_artifact`. URL fetch + file read both shipped + tested; skill/tool/agent/MCP-server-config all flow. ⚠️ **the local-file picker UI is not shipped** (M07.V 🟡 #4 — see below); the backend accepts `ImportSource::File`.
- ✅ **ADR-0011 (a)–(c) concrete construction DISCHARGED at M07.D1.** `impl ConnectionResolver for McpClient` (`crates/runtime-mcp/src/client/connection_resolver.rs`); concrete `McpDispatcher` constructed at `src-tauri/src/commands.rs::build_mcp_dispatcher` from a real `NamespaceResolver` + `CapabilityEnforcer` + Tauri-managed `Arc<McpClient>`; `run_smoke_session` threads `Some(dispatcher)` (was `None`). The A-authored `<construction_reachability_check>` map (all wires `inputs_reachable="false"`) was inverted to `true` with file:line at D1. M07.V Wire pass verified.
- ✅ **ADR-0011 (d) agent-with-tools loop DISCHARGED at M07.D2.** `AgentSdk::run_agent` is the multi-turn loop; consumes D1's concrete dispatcher. The assembled regression drives the real loop + real drone + concrete dispatcher end-to-end. M07.V Behavior pass verified (`agent_with_tools_loop_persists_signals_and_token_usage` PASS).
- ✅ **§5a step 5 — re-resolution on connect/disconnect; `tool_alias_ambiguous` on newly-ambiguous short names.** `McpDispatcher::on_server_connected`/`on_server_disconnected` (`crates/runtime-mcp/src/dispatch.rs:141/155`). The M06.V Dec-6 `<wire_trace_vs_adr_reconcile>` is honored — the driver is on `McpDispatcher`, not `McpClient`. ⚠️ no production *connect-handler caller* yet (M07.V 🟡 #3 — M08.A).
- ✅ **M06.5 `token_usage` finding RESOLVED at M07.D2.** `crates/runtime-drone/src/token_usage.rs::project_signal` is the first production `token_usage` writer; the assembled regression asserts `input_tokens=1234 / output_tokens=56` projected from a real run. The M06.5 open finding (sole INSERT was `#[cfg(test)]` in `vdr.rs`) is closed.
- ✅ **§15c `compatible_os` mismatch → blocking error.** `import/mod.rs` raises `ImportError::OsMismatch` and short-circuits BEFORE L3 (pinned by the `PanicSandbox` test).
- ✅ **§15d / ADR-0005 `share_provenance` — populated on export, surfaced on import; runtime-to-runtime only (no rebake, no Share It module).** `export_with_provenance` always sets `rebake_changes: []`; round-trip asserted. v0.1-scope-correct.
- ✅ **Schema-as-source-of-truth (Hard Rule 5).** `schemas/skills-lock.v1.json` authored hand-first; `artifact_hash_mismatch` extends `event.v1.json`; types regenerated via `cargo xtask regenerate-types` (`--check` clean every stage).
- ✅ **§8.security L3 — import artifacts pass the `runtime-sandbox` validator before install.** Reused, not rebuilt; the `SandboxAdapter` runs a conservative `Read`/`Pure` declaration.
- ✅ **CQ-6 — `ServerStatus` enum + migration `003_mcp_server_status.sql`** (closes TD-009). **EFF-4 — batched `run_health_pass`** (closes the M06 EFF-4 carry-forward).
- ✅ **Zero telemetry; `forbid(unsafe_code)`.** Held end-to-end. `reqwest` import fetch hits only the user-supplied URL.
- ❌ / ⚠️ **§8.security L4 — "Novice — every install is reviewed; explicit Install click" — NOT satisfied (M07.V 🔴 #1).** `tier_gate` (`import/mod.rs:491`) has zero call sites; `import_artifact_with` always installs + hash-locks; the renderer "Reject" does no backend rollback and no `uninstall_artifact`/`skills_lock::remove` exists. A Novice "Reject" is a no-op against the backend. **Waived to the M07.5 fix-cycle via ADR-0016** (maintainer-adjudicated, commit `8a861cd`). This is the one genuine spec-contract drift M07 ships — waived, scheduled, blast-radius-bounded; not absent.
- ⚠️ **§8.security L1 — import-fetch network capability enforcement is decorative** (simplify CQ-M07-1). `EnforcerGate::check` (`commands.rs:1071–1075`) grants the `decl` it then checks against a fresh enforcer — always passes. The phase-doc intent ("enforced through the M05 L1 enforcer") is unmet; the gate is a host-string validator. No active security gap (Hard Rule 4). 🟡 — see Fix backlog.
- ⚠️ **`skills_lock::verify` has no production load-path caller** (M07.V 🟡 #2). The primitive + the `HashMismatch → ArtifactHashMismatch` mapping are delivered + unit-tested; v0.1 has no production code path that byte-loads an imported artifact. Dec-6 carry-forward → M08.A.

### Spec review (forward-looking)

- **Missing items:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §8.security L4 — pin the v0.1 install-review *contract*: install-after-confirm (V's Option A — `tier_gate` between L3 and `install_with`; `complete_`/`cancel_` commands) vs lock-then-uninstall (Option B). M07.5 picks one; the spec should then pin it so M08.V has an endpoint.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §M7 / §2152 — clarify the v0.1 import surface: URL + local-file are both spec'd; v0.1 ships URL-UI + file-*backend*; the file-picker UI is M08. Pin the v0.1/v1.0 split.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §8.security L1 — pin whether import-fetch network access is a real capability-gated check or is constrained structurally (user-supplied URL only). The current `EnforcerGate` claims the former, ships the latter.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §2152 — `skills.lock` key name: the spec §2200 sketch says `installed`; M07.B ships `installed`. The §2205 hash sketch said `sha256:<hex>`; M07.B ships SRI `sha256-<base64>` (ADR-0014). Pin the SRI choice in the spec.
- **Contradictions:** None unresolved. The 🔴 #1 contract drift is a code-vs-spec gap waived to M07.5, not a spec self-contradiction.
- **Ambiguity:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §2214 — "validates `content_hash` on every load" — does not name the load-path call site; v0.1 has no such path (M07.V 🟡 #2). The spec should note the v0.1 deferral and name M08's Builder-Canvas Test/Run as the production trigger.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §15c — `compatible_os` for a multi-OS artifact on a host not in the list: M07 ships hard-block. Confirm the spec intends block (not warn).
- **Recommended spec changes:** A focused post-M07 `docs(spec):` pass — §8.security L4 install-review contract (after M07.5 decides), §M7 URL/file v0.1-split, §8.security L1 import-fetch-gate honesty, §2214 load-path trigger naming. The prior post-M05/M06 `docs(spec):` PR (~22 entries) **landed** as `ae69f9b` (PR #86) — the M07.A pre-flight gate; this is a fresh, smaller batch.

### Fix backlog

Severity is non-elastic. Critical = "must fix before M08 starts."

- 🔴 **Critical** (must fix before M08 starts):
  - **M07.V 🔴 #1 — `tier_gate` defined but never invoked; a Novice "Reject" does not reject.** Spec §8.security L4 contract drift. **Waived to the dedicated M07.5 fix-cycle via ADR-0016** (maintainer-adjudicated, commit `8a861cd`; D.fix WIP preserved on `m07.5-salvage` — red `518f6cf` + impl `bb71dbf`). Owner: M07.5 fix-cycle, V's Option A (gate-then-install split + `complete_import_artifact`/`cancel_pending_import` commands + the `reject_rolls_back_lock_and_registry` assembled regression). **The M07.5 fix-cycle MUST run before M08 Stage A** — M08 introduces the production artifact-load path, after which the gap would have a blast radius. Blast radius for the M07→M07.5 interval is bounded: every artifact still passes schema-validation + L3 before install; no production path loads/executes an imported artifact in v0.1 (M07.V #2/#5).

- 🟡 **Important** (should fix this release cycle):
  - **`EnforcerGate::check` tautological import-fetch capability gate** (simplify CQ-M07-1). Owner: code. `commands.rs:1071–1075` grants the `decl` it then checks — the L1 gate is decorative; the doc comment overstates it. Fix: gate against a real pre-existing policy, OR correct the comment to state honestly that v0.1 import egress is constrained structurally (user-supplied URL only), not by a capability check. Target: **M07.5** (re-touches the import-command surface) — fold into the fix-cycle.
  - **M07.V 🟡 #2 — `skills_lock::verify` no production load-path caller.** Owner: code / M08.A. Wire `verify` into the artifact-load path (the Builder-Canvas Test/Run on a framework with imported skills/tools); map `HashMismatch → AgentEvent::ArtifactHashMismatch`; refuse load. Cite ADR-0014.
  - **M07.V 🟡 #3 — `McpDispatcher::on_server_connected`/`on_server_disconnected` no production connect-handler caller.** Owner: code / M08.A. Wire into the production connect handler; translate each `NewAmbiguity → AgentEvent::ToolAliasAmbiguous` (spec §5a step 5).
  - **M07.V 🟡 #5 — agent-with-tools production driver absent.** Owner: code / M08.A. The multi-turn loop + concrete dispatcher are ready (D2 shipped + assembled-tested); only a production tool-emitting session (Builder-Canvas Test/Run on a framework with imported tools/MCP servers) is missing. **#2 + #3 + #5 are a coupled set — all close together at M08.A** (per M07.V Decision 7).

Needs `@tauri-apps/plugin-dialog` + Rust registration + capability registration; the backend already accepts `ImportSource::File`. The M07 phase doc carries no `<scope_change><descope/>` block for this — consider a retroactive annotation (M07.V Decision 4) so a future V re-run does not re-surface it as 🔴.
