### Simplify pass outcome (v1.6 `<simplify_pass>`)

Per the M07.G `<deliverables><simplify_pass>`. Three parallel read-only review agents (code-reuse / code-quality / efficiency) ran against the cumulative M07 diff (`e677d93..HEAD`, 78 files / +9,546 / −372). **Proposal pass — `<approval_required>true</approval_required>` — no changes auto-applied.** Aggregate verdict: **the cumulative M07 diff is structurally sound** — the import pipeline, `skills_lock`, the `token_usage` projector, `connection_resolver`, and `ImportPanel` are tightly scoped and reuse the M05/M06 primitives as specified; the CQ-2 `RenderableOutcome` split is correctly wired (the run-loop match is exhaustive, no catch-all). 17 proposals surfaced (deduplicated):

| ID | Proposal | Sev | Recommendation |
|---|---|---|---|
| CQ-M07-1 | `EnforcerGate::check` (`commands.rs:1071`) grants the `decl` it then checks — the import-fetch L1 capability gate is tautological; the doc comment overstates it | **High** | **Promoted to a 🟡 Fix-backlog item** (above). NOT a simplify auto-apply — capability-enforcement surface (Hard Rule 8). Fold the fix into M07.5. |
| CQ-M07-4 | `describeProvenance` (`ImportPanel.tsx:294`) casts `unknown` without a runtime object-guard — a non-object provenance value yields `null` silently | Low | **Apply now** — add a `typeof === 'object' && !== null` guard; renderer-only, defensive, zero behavior change on the well-formed v0.1 path |
| RU-M07-1 | `record_to_transport` (`connection_resolver.rs`) duplicates `McpClient::transport_from_config` logic for a different input shape | Med | Defer → TD-016 |
| RU-M07-2 | `token_usage.rs` defines a 3rd `SignalRow`-shaped struct (after `vdr.rs`, `plan_projector.rs`) | Low | Defer → TD-014 |
| RU-M07-3 | `tier_wire` is a 3rd `Tier→string` mapping with no shared home | Low | Defer → TD-017 (fold into the TD-007 resolution) |
| RU-M07-4 | `RegistryAdapter::upsert` field-by-field copy `McpServerImport→McpServerRecord`, no `From` impl | Low | Defer → TD-017 (single-site; premature) |
| RU-M07-5 | `capability_summary` iterates a hard-coded capability-key list | Low | Defer → TD-017 |
| CQ-M07-2 | `import_err_to_cmd` collapses all `ImportError` variants to `internal(...)`, erasing actionable signal | Med | Defer → TD-015 (M07.5 re-opens the import-command surface) |
| CQ-M07-3 | `try_mcp_dispatch` returns `Result<Option<Option<DispatchedTool>>>` — a 3-state discriminant that should be an enum | Med | Defer → TD-015 (M07.5) |
| CQ-M07-5 | `token_usage.rs` `timestamp.parse().unwrap_or(0)` silently inserts epoch-0 for a corrupt row | Low | Defer → TD-018 (add a `tracing::warn!`) |
| CQ-M07-6 | `#[allow(too_many_arguments)]` on `import_artifact_with` (10 params) | Low | Defer → TD-015 (M07.5 changes the signature anyway) |
| CQ-M07-7 | `connection_resolver.rs` `from_str(...).unwrap_or_default()` swallows malformed registry JSON | Low | Defer → TD-016 (NOT apply-now — returning an error is a behavior change on a V-verified safety primitive) |
| CQ-M07-8 | `kind_to_ref` second copy in `agent_sdk.rs` | Low | Already TD-007 — no new severity |
| EFF-M07-7 | `try_mcp_dispatch` rebuilds the `mcp_aliases` `BTreeMap` per `ProviderEvent::ToolUse` (warm path) | Med | Defer → TD-018 (extends EFF-1 / TD-012) |
| EFF-M07-8 | double `args.clone()` at the `dispatch_if_mcp` call site | Low | Maintainer's call (touches the V-verified `McpToolDispatch` trait signature) → TD-018 |
| EFF-M07-9 | `validate()` clones the parsed `serde_json::Value` 3× (once per schema variant) | Low | Maintainer's call — mechanical, but on the V-verified import pipeline → defer TD-015 unless the maintainer adds it to the approved subset |
| EFF-M07-10 | `ImportPanel.tsx` runs `Object.values` + `.find` + 2× `.filter` — three O(N) scans, immaterial at v0.1 N | Low | Defer → TD-018 |

**Recommended maintainer-approved subset (focused refactor commit before the PR opens):** **CQ-M07-4** only — the renderer `describeProvenance` object-guard. It is the single proposal that is mechanical, defensive, renderer-only (off every Stage-V-verified safety-primitive wire), and zero-behavior-change on the well-formed v0.1 path. EFF-M07-9 is offered as a maintainer's-call addition (mechanical, but it touches the V-verified import pipeline — the M06.G CQ-4 precedent for an offered-but-not-recommended item). **CQ-M07-1 is deliberately NOT in the subset** — it is a capability-enforcement-surface finding (Hard Rule 8), promoted to a 🟡 Fix-backlog item and folded into M07.5, not patched at closeout. **All non-approved proposals defer to `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-014..TD-018** (entries appended in this closeout commit; final disposition gated on the maintainer's subset decision per the approval surface).

> **Maintainer decision (M07.G):** approved subset = **CQ-M07-4** only (the renderer `describeProvenance` object-guard). **EFF-M07-9 deferred** to `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-015 — the maintainer's rationale: do not modify V-verified import-pipeline code in the closeout for a non-correctness gain; M07.5 restructures that pipeline and absorbs it. CQ-M07-4 lands in a focused `refactor(M07.G)` commit AFTER the gap-analysis/closeout commit (the closeout commit is the final-but-one; the refactor commit is the final commit on the branch — the M06.G ordering). All other proposals defer to `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-014..TD-018 (appended in the closeout commit).

### Sign-off

**Claude:** I have generated this gap analysis after the final stage of M07 (Stage G — this commit, modulo an approved Simplify-pass refactor commit). This is my honest assessment of the cumulative code-vs-spec state across M01–M07 + the M06.5 IRL fix-cycle. M07 discharged the ADR-0011 (a)–(d) concrete-construction carry-forward (the largest open architectural debt in the ledger) and shipped the registry-import feature, the `skills.lock` integrity primitive (ADR-0014), and the Builder Import panel (ADR-0015). The M06.5 `token_usage = 0` finding is RESOLVED in production at M07.D2. M07.V produced **1🔴 / 4🟡 / 1🟢**: the 🔴 (`tier_gate` never invoked — a Novice "Reject" does not roll back the install; spec §8.security L4 drift) is **waived to the dedicated M07.5 fix-cycle via ADR-0016** (maintainer-adjudicated; the M07.5 fix-cycle MUST run before M08 Stage A; blast radius bounded — no production path loads/executes an imported artifact in v0.1). The 4🟡 carry to M08.A (#2/#3/#5 a coupled Dec-6 set; #4 the file-picker UI); the 🟢 → TD-014. The simplify_pass independently surfaced one finding V missed — `EnforcerGate::check` is a tautological import-fetch capability gate (CQ-M07-1) — promoted to a 🟡 Fix-backlog item, folded into M07.5. All six hard gates passed in every stage A–E; aggregate axis means healthy (Process 37.5/40, Product 37.83/40, Pattern 29.33/35); deliverable time-box ~0.75×. The largest residual clusters are the M07.5 fix-cycle (🔴 #1 + the `EnforcerGate` gate + the Reinstall round-trip), the M08.A coupled Dec-6 set (skills_lock-verify / on_server_connected / agent-with-tools production drivers + the file-picker UI), and the v1.9 protocol iteration (the recurring phase-doc-authoring + mechanical-test-file friction). User review pending; per `CLAUDE.md` §20 this entry is **IMMUTABLE once committed** — future milestones report status updates via their Carry-forward sections only.

**Surfaced at:** 2026-05-19 (UTC).

## M08 — Workbench (Builder Canvas) (2026-05-21, Stage H closeout commit on parent-milestone branch `claude/m08-workbench`)

> Author: Claude (per `CLAUDE.md` §20)
> Stages aggregated: M08.A (post-M07 carry-forward absorption + intake + the `<construction_reachability_check>` groundwork for the three M07.V Dec-6 wires — M04 `plan_loop` driver shell, M07-IRL #2/#3/#7, M06.5 IRL 🟡-1/-2/-3, the #5/§1c intake), M08.B (Builder backend — `validate_framework` + framework save/load + capability summary + the first production `skills.lock` reader + narrowing exposure), M08.C (Builder shell + 5-tab Palette + `@tauri-apps/plugin-dialog` local-file picker — ADR-0020 filed), M08.D1 (Builder Canvas node editor — drag-drop + inline config + per-node capability disclosure), M08.D2 (Builder Canvas edges — 4 edge types + Agent→Agent narrowing + continuous validation badges), M08.E (Inspector + canvas↔JSON two-way binding), M08.F1 (Tester backend — isolated session + the M07.V Dec-6 discharge — ADR-0019 filed), M08.F2 (Tester modal renderer), M08.G (Settings panel + Novice↔Promoted tier promotion), M08.V (in-band verifier — four passes; 0🔴 / 2🟡 / 2🟢).
> Reviewed against: `agent-runtime-spec.md` §0–§0d, Phase 9 ~§2495–2543 (Visual Canvas and Tester), §3/§3a (live graph + plan), §5a (MCP re-resolution), §6 (framework loader), §8.security L1/L2/L4, §9 (the workbench framing — "output is the source of truth, the canvas is the editor"; "no duplication of validation logic between TS and Rust"), §1c (multi-session), §13 (zero telemetry); `schemas/{framework,skill,tool,agent,common}.v1.json` (consumed; `framework.v1.json` TS type newly added to the xtask codegen targets — no schema *change*); the nine M08.A–G stage retrospectives + the M08.V verifier retrospective + `M08-summary.md`; ADR-0019 + ADR-0020 (filed this milestone); `docs/M07-irl-findings.md` (the carry-forward routing source); `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-001..TD-020; `docs/coverage-policy.md` §A–§D; M01–M07 gap-analysis entries + the M06.5 / M07.5 IRL fix-cycle records.
> M08 is the largest milestone in the MVP — nine work stages (D split D1/D2, F split F1/F2) + Stage V + this Stage H closeout. It delivers spec Phase 9 (the Workbench / Builder Canvas + the sandboxed Tester + the Settings panel) and absorbs the entire post-M07 carry-forward backlog: the coupled M07.V Dec-6 set (🟡 #2/#3/#4/#5), the eight M07-IRL findings, the M06.5 IRL 🟡-1..4, and the M04 `plan_loop` driver. Cumulative M08 diff ~14,862 / 92 across 98 files (`ea95bdc..HEAD`).

### Codebase deep dive (cumulative — M01 + M02 + M03 + M04 + M05 + M06 + M07 + M08)

M08 is the milestone that turns v0.1 from a runtime *spectator* into a *workbench*. Through M07 the renderer had exactly one top-level surface — the read-only live-execution graph (`GraphCanvas` + `graphStore`). M08 adds a second, disjoint surface: a build-mode three-panel Builder (Palette / React-Flow canvas / Inspector) backed by a new `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/` module and a new, separate `builderStore`. The new surface:

- **Builder backend** (Stage B). `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/` — `validate.rs` (the single continuous validator — reuses `framework_loader::walk` + `capability/narrowing.rs`, no second TS validator, spec §9), `persist.rs` (path-agnostic `&Path` save/load of `framework.json` + companion `.md` — byte-stable round-trip), `summary.rs` (whole-framework capability summary aggregating `framework_loader::capability_map`), `error.rs`, plus `list_installed` — the **first production `skills.lock` reader** (M07's lock was a closed write-only ledger until here). Four thin `async` Tauri commands over `*_with` seams.
- **Builder canvas + state model** (Stages C/D1/D2/E; ADR-0020). `src/lib/builderStore.ts` holds `framework: Framework` (the schema-generated type) as the **single source of truth**; the React-Flow canvas is a pure projection (`canvasNodes`/`canvasEdges`), and the Canvas|JSON two-way binding falls out for free — both edit directions reduce to "mutate `framework`, re-render". D1 ships the node editor (drag-drop instantiation, inline config, per-node capability disclosure reusing the M05/M07.E plain-English component — its third reuse via a behavior-preserving extraction to `CapabilityDisclosure.tsx`); D2 ships the four edge types, Agent→Agent capability narrowing surfaced *verbatim* from the Rust `narrow()` (no TS intersection), and debounced continuous validation with red node badges; E ships the Inspector + the JSON tab.
- **The sandboxed Tester** (Stages F1/F2; ADR-0019). `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/tester.rs` + the `test_framework` shell command run a candidate framework in an **isolated session**: a throwaway `temp_dir()` SQLite DB, `HitlSeam::test_defaults()` so capability violations become test failures instead of blocking HITL prompts, teardown deleting the DB. It reuses the smoke-session construction (`AgentSdk::with_capability_wiring → run_agent`) — no new session engine — and is the production code path that **discharges three M07.V Dec-6 carry-forwards on one wire**. F2's modal renders the run in a graph pane scoped to a second `createGraphStore()` instance so a test run never touches the live `graphStore`.
- **Settings panel** (Stage G). `src/components/SettingsPanel.tsx` surfaces the existing `request_tier_transition` command (Novice↔Promoted) — making the §0d-scoped Promoted tier *reachable* for the first time — and the global budget cap. It surfaces, it does not reimplement (zero edits under `crates/runtime-main/src/tier/` — Hard Rule 8 held).

What's solid (cumulative): M08 ships ADR-0020's single-source-of-truth state model cleanly — the spec-§9 "canvas is the editor, output is the source of truth" intent is structural, not aspirational, and the two-way binding needs no reconciliation engine. Validation is genuinely one validator with two triggers (D2's debounced continuous pass + E's Validate button both call the one Rust `validate_framework`). The Tester's isolation is real and verifier-confirmed (throwaway DB, test-defaults HITL, byte-untouched user DB). Schema-as-source-of-truth held (no schema *change*; the missing `framework.ts` was *generated* via the xtask pipeline, not hand-written — §14). `forbid(unsafe_code)` and zero-telemetry held. Strict v1.8 two-commit TDD ran cleanly in all nine stages. The A→F1 `<construction_reachability_check>` chain completed and Stage V independently confirmed it. What's structurally weak and likely to compound: (1) **`TestOutcome.vdr` is structurally dead** — `fold_outcome` (`tester.rs:121`) hardcodes `vdr: Value::Null` on every path (`tester.rs:153`); the field renders as `null` in the modal. The gap originates in the phase doc's own F1.3.1 pseudocode and is M08.V 🟡 #1. (2) **`plan_loop::drive_plan` has no production caller** — the M04 driver shell was delivered + tested at M08.A (7 tests, 100% line) but v0.1 has no plan-orchestrated session entrypoint; M08.V 🟡 #2. (3) The Builder has no Task node — the spec's fourth edge type (Hook→Task) is `connectEdge`-level + unit-tested only, not canvas-drawable. (4) `builderStore.removeNode` is a permanent typed no-op stub (TD-020) — node deletion is genuinely out of M08 scope but the dead interface surface is latent risk.

What surprised: `src/types/framework.ts` did not exist — the xtask TS-codegen target list never included `framework` (resolved at C via the generation pipeline). `runtime_core::event::AgentEvent` is a *hand-rolled* curated union, not the typify-generated `generated/event.rs` enum (caught at F1). The Cargo dependency graph (`runtime-mcp` depends on `runtime-main`) forced the §5a MCP connect handler into the shell `commands.rs` rather than `tester.rs` — recorded in ADR-0019. Time-box ratio ~0.73× (deliverable time ~71.5 h vs the ~97.5 h midpoint estimate) — squarely in the M06/M07 ~0.7–0.75× band.

### Adherence to spec

The eight MVP §M8 acceptance criteria, each cited against shipped code + the Playwright behavior test that demonstrates it:

- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 1 — drag an Agent node onto an empty canvas; set role/model/`allowed_*` inline; capability disclosure renders.** Code: `src/components/builder/BuilderCanvas.tsx` + `NodeConfigPanel.tsx` + `CapabilityDisclosure.tsx` (the M05/M07.E disclosure surface, behavior-preservingly extracted — third reuse). Demonstrated end-to-end by `tests/e2e/builder_canvas_nodes.spec.ts` (6/6).
- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 2 — connect Agent→Skill → skill added to `allowed_skills`.** Code: `builderStore.connectEdge` (`src/lib/builderStore.ts:492`) + the `parseNodeId` helper. Demonstrated by `tests/e2e/builder_edges.spec.ts`.
- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 3 — connect Agent→Agent → child `allowed_*` intersected with parent; UI surfaces narrowing.** Narrowing computed in Rust — `crates/runtime-main/src/capability/narrowing.rs:38` (`narrow`, the M05.B L2a primitive — NOT reimplemented in TS, spec §9), aggregated by `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/summary.rs`; surfaced by `src/components/builder/NarrowingNotice.tsx`. The `surfaces_the_backend_narrowed_caps_verbatim_no_TS_intersection` contract test (gotcha #66) is the guard.
- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 4 — click Validate → schema validation runs; errors at the offending node.** Validator: `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/validate.rs` (command `src-tauri/src/commands.rs:1395`, returns `FrameworkValidationReport`). Red badges: `src/components/builder/nodes/NodeValidationBadge.tsx`. Validate button: `src/components/builder/Inspector.tsx` — calls the *same* `validate_framework` D2's continuous pass uses.
- ⚠️ **MVP §M8 criterion 5 — click Test → task → Tester modal → sandboxed session → graph + VDR + token spend + pass/fail.** Test button: `Inspector.tsx` → `builderStore.openTester`. Backend: `src-tauri/src/commands.rs:1630` (`test_framework`) → `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/tester.rs:295` (`run_test_session_with`). Modal: `src/components/builder/TesterModal.tsx`. **Four of the five surfaces of criterion 5 — the scoped graph pane, token spend, pass/fail, the full trace — populate correctly; the distinct VDR object does not.** `fold_outcome` (`tester.rs:121`) hardcodes `vdr: serde_json::Value::Null` (`tester.rs:153`) on every path — it never reads the `decision_record` event the run emits — and `TesterModal` renders `JSON.stringify(outcome.vdr)` = `null`. M08.V 🟡 #1; the gap originates in the phase doc's own F1.3.1 pseudocode. Carried to M09.A.
- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 6 — Canvas | JSON tabs; edit JSON; switch back shows the updated canvas.** Code: `src/components/builder/JsonView.tsx`; the binding is structurally trivial per ADR-0020 (`builderStore.framework` is the single source of truth; a valid JSON edit calls `replaceFramework`, the canvas projection re-derives; an invalid edit surfaces an inline parse error and never reaches `replaceFramework` — the verified no-desync guard). Demonstrated by `tests/e2e/builder_inspector.spec.ts`.
- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 7 — save framework to disk → `framework.json` + companion `.md`.** Backend: `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/persist.rs::save_framework` (command `commands.rs:1412`); Save affordance: `Inspector.tsx` + the `@tauri-apps/plugin-dialog` picker (M07.V 🟡 #4).
- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 8 — reload from disk → canvas reconstructs identical.** Backend: `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/persist.rs::load_framework` (command `commands.rs:1441`); the `save_load_save_cycle_is_byte_stable` test pins byte-stability; the canvas re-derives from the loaded `framework` (ADR-0020).
- ✅ **ADR-0019 — the Tester isolated-session model.** `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/tester.rs` + `src-tauri/src/commands.rs` (`throwaway_test_db_path:1505` resolves `temp_dir()/runtime-tester-<uuid>.sqlite` — never `app_local_data_dir`; `connect_test_session_mcp:1519`; teardown deletes the DB). `HitlSeam::test_defaults()` woven so §8.security L2 violations fold onto `TestOutcome.capability_failures` as test failures, not live HITL — `CapabilityEnforcer::check` unchanged (Hard Rule 8). The Tester is a sequential build-time throwaway session, **not** the §0d-❌ §1c multi-session pool. Filed `Proposed`; flips `Accepted` in the M08 PR.
- ✅ **ADR-0020 — the Builder canvas ↔ `framework.json` state model.** `src/lib/builderStore.ts` — `framework` is the single source of truth; the canvas is a pure projection. Filed `Proposed`; flips `Accepted` in the M08 PR.
- ✅ **Spec §9 — "no duplication of validation logic between TS and Rust."** `validate_framework` (Rust, `builder/validate.rs`) is the only validator; D2's debounced continuous pass and E's explicit Validate button both call it. There is no TS-side validator. Confirmed by M08.V's Wire pass + the `the_validate_button_uses_the_same_validate_framework_the_continuous_pass_uses` contract test.
- ✅ **Spec §5a step 5 — MCP re-resolution on connect.** `connect_test_session_mcp` (`commands.rs:1519`) drives `McpDispatcher::on_server_connected` — the production connect-handler caller M07.V 🟡 #3 lacked.
- ✅ **Spec §8.security L4 — tier promotion.** `request_tier_transition` (`commands.rs:573`) surfaced by `SettingsPanel.tsx`; the displayed tier updates through the existing `tier_transition` reducer (`graphStore.ts:1549`) — G adds no new reducer case, no tier-logic edit. Operator is never surfaced (§0d: v0.1 is Novice + Promoted only).
- ⚠️ **Spec Phase 9 — "drone-managed sandbox per §1c" vs §0d (§1c multi-session ❌ for v0.1).** Reconciled by ADR-0019: the Tester needs *an* isolated session, run sequentially from build mode where no live session executes — not the §1c concurrent-session pool. Not a contradiction once the spec phrasing is read against §0d; recorded as a spec-refinement (below).
- ⚠️ **Spec Phase 9 — the fourth edge type (Hook→Task) is not canvas-drawable in v0.1.** The Builder has no Task node (the Palette has 5 tabs — Tools/Skills/Agents/HITL/Hooks). `connectEdge` implements `hook->task` per the phase doc and unit-tests it directly with a synthetic `task:` target, but it is unreachable from the canvas. No MVP §M8 criterion needs it; recorded for completeness.

### Spec review (forward-looking)

- **Missing items:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` Phase 9 — the spec does not name where the Tester's `TestOutcome.vdr` is populated from. M08 ships the field structurally dead (always `Value::Null`). The spec should name the VDR source — the test session's `decision_record` events folded in `fold_outcome`, or a query of the drone's VDR projection before teardown — so M09's intake has an endpoint.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §3a / Phase 9 — v0.1 has no plan-orchestrated session entrypoint at all (the smoke session and the Tester both call `run_agent` directly). The `plan_loop`/`drive_plan` driver shipped at M08.A has no v0.1 home. The spec should pin whether a plan-driven session is a v0.1 surface or a v1.0 item.
- **Contradictions:** None unresolved.
- **Ambiguity / §12-owned technical decisions the build resolved:**
  - **§1c-multi-session vs the Tester's isolated session.** Spec Phase 9 says the Tester runs a "drone-managed sandbox per §1c"; §0d marks §1c multi-session ❌ for v0.1. Stage A's intake (A.3.9) surfaced the reconciling reading and the maintainer confirmed it: the Tester is a *sequential, throwaway, build-time* test session — it needs *an* isolated session, not the §1c concurrent-session pool. Recorded in **ADR-0019**. The spec should add a one-line note to Phase 9 that "per §1c" means the isolated-session *model*, not the concurrent-session *pool*, for v0.1.
  - **`validate_framework` command-return vs spec-§9 "posts results back as events".** Spec Phase 9 describes continuous validation as posting results "back as events". M08 ships `validate_framework` as a Tauri command returning `FrameworkValidationReport` synchronously (request/response) — the project's IPC matured to synchronous command returns since the spec was written (M07's `import_artifact` / `request_tier_transition` set the precedent). A §12-owned technical decision (Stage B); no schema, no event variant, no ADR. The spec should refine the Phase 9 phrasing to "returns a validation report" rather than "posts events".
- **Recommended spec changes:** A focused post-M08 `docs(spec):` pass — the Phase 9 §1c-vs-isolated-session note, the `validate_framework` return-shape phrasing, the `TestOutcome.vdr` source, and the `plan_loop` v0.1/v1.0 disposition. Smaller than the post-M07 batch.

### Fix backlog

Severity is non-elastic. Critical = "must fix before M09 starts."

- 🔴 **Critical** (must fix before M09 starts):
  - **None.** Stage V produced **zero 🔴**. M08 ships no spec-contract drift requiring a pre-M09 fix.

- 🟡 **Important** (should fix this release cycle):
  - **M08.V 🟡 #1 — `TestOutcome.vdr` is structurally dead (always `Value::Null`).** Owner: code / M09.A. `fold_outcome` (`crates/runtime-main/src/builder/tester.rs:121`/`:153`) never reads the `decision_record` `AgentEvent`. Fix: fold the trace's `decision_record` events in `fold_outcome`, or query the drone VDR projection before teardown. MVP §M8 criterion 5 is 4/5 satisfied; the field renders harmlessly as `null`. Not 🔴 — the gap originates in the phase doc's own F1.3.1 pseudocode.
  - **M08.V 🟡 #2 — `plan_loop`/`drive_plan` shipped but has no production caller.** Owner: code / M09.A. `crates/runtime-main/src/plan/plan_loop.rs::drive_plan` was delivered + tested at M08.A (7 tests, 100% line); `commands.rs` documents the deferral inline. v0.1 has no plan-orchestrated session entrypoint. M09.A decides whether `plan_loop` wiring has a v0.1 home or is a v1.0 item — and (the M06.V Dec-6 standing rule for a delivered/driver-absent primitive) **files the ADR-class carry-forward record the deferral currently lacks**. The M08 phase-doc V.2 table over-claimed here (it told the verifier to expect "a production caller from the session entrypoint" that Stage A's A.2/A.3.1/A.4.6 never contracted) — reconciled at this closeout.

  - **v1.9 protocol iteration.** Owner: docs / protocol. M08's recurring friction names the candidates concretely: formalise `<pre_red_mechanical_sweep>` (A ran 5 red-commit amends; B–G ran zero after adopting it); a `<layout_shift_audit>` slot (the React-Flow e2e layout-shift regression recurred E→G); a `<test_interaction_audit>` slot (a mount-time `invoke` breaking pre-existing `mockResolvedValueOnce`-chain tests recurred A→C); a crate-dependency-direction check for a wire's `<construction_reachability_check>` `constructor` file (F1's Cargo cycle); the v1.9 `<data_flow_audit>` candidate (the phase-doc pseudocode-vs-shipped-wire drift recurred every renderer stage, and the `vdr: Value::Null` pseudocode shipped verbatim). M08.V's special-log additionally proposes a v1.9 check that the V.2 "What V checks" column be *derived from* the owning stage's acceptance criteria, not authored aspirationally.

### Carry-forward from prior milestones

For every Important item from prior gap-analysis entries + the M07.V findings + the M07-IRL walk-through + the M06.5 IRL findings, status as of the M08 Stage H commit:

- **M07.V 🟡 #2 (`skills_lock::verify` no production load-path caller)** — **RESOLVED at M08.F1.** `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/tester.rs:181` (`load_verified_artifact`) calls `crate::skills_lock::verify` on the Tester's artifact-load path; production path `test_framework` → `run_test_session_with` → `verify_framework_artifacts` (`tester.rs:238`) → `load_verified_artifact`. M08.V's Wire pass confirmed a genuine production caller (not a `#[cfg(test)]` block). FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M07.V 🟡 #3 (`McpDispatcher::on_server_connected` no production connect-handler caller)** — **RESOLVED at M08.F1.** `src-tauri/src/commands.rs:1519` (`connect_test_session_mcp`) is the production caller. Placement diverged from the F1 phase-doc `<construction_reachability_check>` (which named `tester.rs`) — forced by the `runtime-mcp → runtime-main` Cargo dependency direction; reconciled and recorded in **ADR-0019**. M08.V's Wire pass confirmed it. FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M07.V 🟡 #4 (local-file picker UI not shipped)** — **RESOLVED at M08.C.** `@tauri-apps/plugin-dialog` 2.7.1 registered (npm dep + Rust crate + `dialog:allow-open` capability); wired into the Builder import affordance and the M07 Import panel's "Browse…" companion. FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M07.V 🟡 #5 (agent-with-tools production driver absent)** — **RESOLVED at M08.F1.** `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/tester.rs::run_test_session_with` drives `AgentSdk::run_agent` with a tool-bearing candidate framework — the second production caller of `run_agent` (the first, `run_smoke_session`, is no-tools). The assembled regression `tester_runs_a_tool_bearing_framework_through_the_real_loop_and_persists_signals` drives a real `ProviderEvent::ToolUse` with `token_usage > 0`. M08.V's Behavior pass confirmed it. FINAL DISPOSITION. (#2/#3/#5 were the coupled M07.V Dec-6 set — all closed at F1 on one wire, exactly as M07.V Decision 7 designed.)
- **M07-IRL #5 🔴-candidate (no tier-promotion UI; Promoted tier + MCP management unreachable)** — **RESOLVED at M08.G.** `src/components/SettingsPanel.tsx` ships the Novice↔Promoted control over the existing `request_tier_transition` command; the §0d-scoped Promoted tier is reachable for the first time. FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M07-IRL #2 🟡 (token in/out breakdown not populated)** — **RESOLVED at M08.A.** The `graphStore` `token_usage` reducer arm now attributes input/output to the running agent (was a graph-no-op `case`); 4 vitest tests. FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M07-IRL #3 🟡 (import UI text near-invisible — contrast)** — **RESOLVED at M08.A.** One CSS root cause — `.import-*` selectors set `background` but no `color`; `color` pinned to `--node-fg`/`--node-fg-muted`; 3 CSS-content vitest tests. FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M07-IRL #6 🟡 (Import panel does not reload installed artifacts after restart — no `skills.lock` reader)** — **RESOLVED at M08.B + M08.C.** B ships `list_installed` (the first production `skills.lock` reader); C wires `ImportPanel` + the Palette to call `list_installed_artifacts` on mount. FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M07-IRL #7 🟡 (API key does not persist across an app restart)** — **RESOLVED at M08.A.** Root cause was an absent startup read (no `has_api_key` command; `App.tsx` hardcoded `useState(false)`), not a write failure. `key_store::has_api_key` + the `has_api_key` command + the App-mount read; 2 Rust seam tests + 2 App-mount vitest tests. FINAL DISPOSITION.
- **M06.5 IRL 🟡-1 (HITL `ui_variant` not honored)** — **RESOLVED (documented structural close) at M08.A.** The finding was already closed in an intervening stage — all three HITL components branch on `uiVariant`, the reducer maps `event.ui_variant`. Pinned by 3 cross-variant green tests. FINAL DISPOSITION.

The *production caller* of that shell is a distinct gap M08.V surfaced as 🟡 #2 → M09.A (see Fix backlog). The M04 row itself closes here; the new finding carries forward.

### Simplify pass outcome (v1.6 `<simplify_pass>`)

Per the M08.H `<deliverables><simplify_pass>`. Three parallel read-only review agents (code-reuse / code-quality / efficiency) ran against the cumulative M08 diff (`ea95bdc..HEAD` = `main..HEAD`, 98 files / +14,862 / −92). **Proposal pass — `<approval_required>true</approval_required>` — no changes auto-applied.** Aggregate verdict: **the cumulative M08 diff is structurally sound.** The milestone's primary obligations are all met correctly — the Tester reuses `AgentSdk::with_capability_wiring → run_agent` rather than rebuilding a session engine; `createGraphStore()` is shared between the live graph and the scoped test-session graph; the Rust `narrow()` is never reimplemented in TS; the builder module hand-mirrors Rust structs to TS only where the schema pipeline does not cover them; the canvas projection memoization correctly addresses the `useSyncExternalStore` infinite-loop hazard; the debounced validation coalesces burst edits. **No O(N²) loops, no unbounded allocations, no hot-path re-derivation material at v0.1 scale.** The findings (deduplicated):

| ID | Proposal | Sev | Recommendation |
|---|---|---|---|
| RU-M08-1 | `kind_to_ref` is a byte-identical 5-arm match defined independently in `sdk/agent_sdk.rs:756` + `sdk/event_pipeline.rs:322` | Med | Defer → TD-021. **Pre-M08 duplication** (already TD-007's class); compiler-exhaustiveness-checked, no behavior risk. |
| RU-M08-2 | `builder/tester.rs:207` `capability_kind_label` hand-maps `CapabilityKindRef` (a hand-rolled enum with no `Display`) | Low | Defer → TD-021. The right fix (a `Display`/`label()` on `CapabilityKindRef` in `runtime-core`) crosses a crate boundary, out of M08 scope. |
| RU-M08-3 | `BuilderToolNode.tsx` / `BuilderSkillNode.tsx` are structurally identical (Handle+badge+name+Handle); distinct CSS only | Low | Defer → TD-022. Re-evaluate at M09 if `BuilderHitlNode`/`BuilderHookNode` make four leaf-alike nodes. |
| EFF-M08-1 | `canvasEdges()` rebuilds the `nodeIds` `Set` from a re-projected node list each call | Low | Defer → TD-023. Immaterial at v0.1 N (tens of nodes). |
| EFF-M08-4 | `validate.rs:87` `serde_json::from_value(doc.clone())` clones the whole JSON tree; the Tauri wrapper could pass an owned `Value` | Med | Defer → TD-023. Immaterial at v0.1 framework sizes. |
| EFF-M08-5 | `summary.rs:111/114` `parent_grants_for_agent` re-computed once per child inside the spawn-edge loop (could hoist) | Low | Defer → TD-023. One-line hoist; immaterial at v0.1 spawn-edge counts. |
| EFF-M08-6 | `summary.rs:120` `parent_caps.clone()` per child edge | Low | Defer → TD-023. Pairs with EFF-M08-5. |
| CQ-M08-1 | `builderStore.ts:484` `updateNode` extracts the agent id with an ad-hoc `nodeId.replace(/^agent:/,'')` regex instead of the exported `parseNodeId`; silently no-ops on a non-agent id | Med | Defer → TD-024. Off every safety wire; current callers pass agent ids only. |
| CQ-M08-2 | `builderStore.ts:327` `memoizedCanvasEdges` takes a `nodeIds` arg the cache key ignores — a signature trap for a future caller | Low | Defer → TD-024. Documentation/signature smell, not a logic error. |
| CQ-M08-3 | `builder/mod.rs:44` over-exports `fold_outcome`/`load_verified_artifact` from the crate surface — neither has an external consumer | Low | Defer → TD-024. Unnecessary public-API surface. |
| CQ-M08-4 | `builderStore.ts:69` `updateNode`'s `patch` is `Record<string,unknown>` — stringly-typed; a `Partial<Pick<Agent,…>>` would compile-guard the keys | Low | Defer → TD-024. |
| EFF-M08-2/3/7, CQ-M08-5 | `NodeValidationBadge` intermediate-array allocs; `BuilderAgentNode` per-node `spawn_edges` scan; `Inspector` un-memoized `reportErrors`; the documented `as unknown as Framework/Agent` pre-valid casts | Low | **Leave** — immaterial / idiomatic React / the documented correct boundary strategy; not worth a tech-debt entry. |

**Recommended maintainer-approved subset (focused refactor commit before the PR opens):** **none — the empty subset.** Of the 15 deduplicated proposals, every one is either (a) pre-M08 debt (RU-M08-1 — TD-007's class), (b) a cross-crate change out of M08 scope (RU-M08-2), (c) immaterial at v0.1 scale (the EFF cluster, RU-M08-3), or (d) a low-severity structural/signature smell with no behavior change under current callers (the CQ cluster). No proposal is the mechanical / off-every-safety-wire / zero-behavior-change *and correctness-or-clarity-gaining* shape that qualifies for an apply-now closeout refactor; the strongest candidate (CQ-M08-1, the `updateNode` ad-hoc regex) is a real inconsistency but its fix is best landed at the next builder-store touch (M09+) alongside `removeNode`/TD-020, not patched in isolation at closeout. An empty approved subset is an explicitly valid `<simplify_pass>` outcome (the phase doc — "An empty pass is a valid outcome"). **The 11 deferred proposals route to `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-021..TD-024** (appended in this closeout commit); 4 (EFF-M08-2/3/7, CQ-M08-5) are left with no entry. The simplify pass surfaced **no finding the verifier missed of correctness or security significance** — unlike M07's CQ-M07-1.

> **Maintainer decision (M08.H):** [pending — surfaced for approval. Recommended: approve the empty subset; defer TD-021..TD-024.]

## M08.6 — Framework Representation Reconciliation (2026-05-26, Stage F closeout commit on parent-milestone branch `claude/m08.6-framework-representation`)

> Author: Claude (per `CLAUDE.md` §20)
> Stages aggregated: M08.6.A (intake + carry-forward absorption + the four-wire loader-resolution `<construction_reachability_check>` groundwork — the M08 Stage-A → F1 pattern; also closed M08.5-IRL 🟡 #8 docs typo as a Stage-A docs-only edit), M08.6.B (the loader: `load_framework` resolves `{id,path}` agents → inline + reads tools/skills body refs as `Companion`s via the new `split_frontmatter` + `serde_yaml` parse; broken-reference → `BuilderError::ReferenceResolution`; ADR-0022 flipped Proposed → Accepted), M08.6.C (the save half: `save_framework` re-splits to the modular subdirectory layout + emits `{id,path}` framework.json + canonicalizes through `serde_json::Value` for byte-stability against the typify-generated `Framework`'s `HashMap` fields), M08.6.D (the canvas auto-layout on LOAD only via the new `applyLoadedFramework` store action + the `layoutGraph` generic widening + the `window.__builderStore` test seam — 🟡 #4 RESOLVED), M08.6.E (the Palette populated from the loaded framework's resolved artifacts by `(kind, ref)` dedup with built-ins → installed → framework precedence; the visible `· framework` badge + `data-source` discriminator), M08.6.V (in-band verifier — four passes; 0🔴 / 2🟡 / 2🟢; archetype-fidelity confirmed + ADR-0022 single-boundary grep-verified).
> Reviewed against: `agent-runtime-spec.md` §0–§0d, §6 (Framework JSON Loader), §9 (Phase 9 the Canvas), §0b (the Tool/Skill/Agent model); `schemas/framework.v1.json` + `schemas/agent.v1.json` (consumed; **no schema change** — the `agents[]` `oneOf(inline | {id,path})` already permits both forms; M08.6 decides which is canonical and where resolution happens, not the schema); the six M08.6 retrospectives + `M08.6-summary.md`; ADR-0022 (filed Proposed alongside this phase doc, flipped Accepted at Stage B); ADR-0020 (preserved: `nodePositions` is editor-local view state — Stage D's load-only auto-layout invariant); `docs/M08-irl-findings.md` (the carry-forward source); `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-001..TD-032 (this closeout adds TD-028 + TD-029 from V's 🟢 + TD-030/031/032 from the simplify-pass deferrals); `docs/coverage-policy.md` §A–§D + the §C M08.6 entry appended in this closeout; M01–M08 gap-analysis entries; the M08.5 + M08.5.5 fix-cycle summaries (both work-stage-class per CLAUDE.md §20 — their 🔴 closures + the dropped Sub-fix 2 of M08.5.5 flow into THIS entry's Carry-forward).
> M08.6 is a milestone-class follow-on to M08 (not in the original M01–M11 sequence, cut to resolve the post-M08 IRL finding). Five work stages (A intake, B loader, C save, D auto-layout, E Palette) + Stage V verifier + Stage F closeout. Cumulative M08.6 diff: 14 commits (`6c486c5..b2819be`) ahead of `main` at the start of this Stage F.

### Codebase deep dive (cumulative — M01 + M02 + M03 + M04 + M05 + M06 + M07 + M08 + M08.6)

M08.6 is the milestone that turns v0.1's Builder from *capable-of-saving-its-own-format* into *capable-of-loading-the-archetype*. Through M08 the Builder shipped green for an inline-only `framework.json` with flat top-level companion files — a format the Builder authored to disk and re-read perfectly, but that the project's two archetype frameworks (`examples/aria/`, `examples/ralph/`) do not use. The archetype uses `framework.json` `{id, path}` references into subdirectories (`agents/orchestrator.md`, `tools/git_checkpoint.md`, `skills/planning.md`) with YAML frontmatter + markdown bodies, plus cross-framework `../` references (Ralph reads ARIA's tools at `../aria/tools/…`). The M08 Builder couldn't even render `examples/aria/` as a connected workflow — every agent stacked at `{0,0}`, no edges projected — because `load_framework` returned the `{id,path}` agents raw, `projectCanvasEdges` (which derives edges from inline agents) found none, and `projectCanvasNodes` had no `nodePositions` to lay out by. ADR-0022 settled the question: the modular multi-file form is canonical on disk; reference resolution lives at one seam (`load_framework`); save re-splits back to the modular form. M08.6 executes that decision.

The shipped surfaces:

- **The resolver boundary** (Stage B). `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/persist.rs::load_framework` — a single addition that walks the framework directory, reads each `{id,path}`-referenced `.md`, splits its YAML frontmatter via the new `split_frontmatter` helper (a 7-line utility that handles CRLF + the `---\n…\n---` envelope), and parses through `serde_yaml` (an existing workspace dep wired into `runtime-main/Cargo.toml`) into the inline `Agent` type. The schema asymmetry surfaced at B's red phase: only `FrameworkAgentsItem` has an inline `oneOf` variant; `FrameworkSkillsItem` and `FrameworkToolsItem` are flat structs with `name + path? + registry_id? + source` — they have no inline variant to flip to. The resolver is correspondingly asymmetric: agents flip variant (`Object → Agent(_)`); tools/skills get their bodies captured as `Companion { file_name: "tools/git_checkpoint.md", body }` (the existing `Companion` mechanism, now drawing from subdirectories rather than the top level). The downstream consumers — the canvas projection, the Tester, `spawn_framework_subagents`, `framework_capability_summary` — are untouched: they receive a fully reference-resolved inline `Framework`. ADR-0022's single-resolution-boundary holds (V's Wire pass grep-confirmed it — every `serde_yaml` + frontmatter parse + path-ref resolution is in `persist.rs` + its test files, no leaks).

- **The save re-split** (Stage C). `save_framework` becomes the inverse — given a resolved (inline) `Framework`, it emits `framework.json` with `{id, path}` references and writes the agent/tool/skill `.md` files (frontmatter via `serde_yaml::to_string` if no captured companion body exists, otherwise the captured body verbatim) into `agents/`, `tools/`, `skills/` subdirectories. The byte-stable round-trip was the load-bearing acceptance: stage C surfaced the HashMap-iteration trap that the M08-era `save_load_save_cycle_is_byte_stable` test had missed because its fixture had no HashMap content. `Framework` carries three `HashMap<String, _>` fields (`hook_defs`, `mcp_aliases`, `per_mode_overrides`); Rust's `HashMap` iteration is randomized per process; `serde_json::to_string_pretty(&Framework)` therefore produces non-deterministic output for any framework that exercises those fields. The fix is one line: route through `serde_json::to_value(&on_disk)?` before `to_string_pretty` — `serde_json::Map` is backed by `BTreeMap` (the workspace doesn't enable the `preserve_order` feature), so every nested object's keys serialize alphabetically. The behavioral change: `framework.json` field order is now alphabetical (was struct-definition order via typify); the byte-stable round-trip is what MVP §M8 criterion 8 actually requires.

- **The canvas auto-layout** (Stage D). `src/lib/builderStore.ts` gains a new `applyLoadedFramework(loaded)` action — the LOAD-only seam — that projects nodes + edges from the resolved framework, runs the existing `src/lib/layout.ts::layoutGraph` (the dagre top-down layout the live `GraphCanvas` already uses), and seeds `nodePositions` from the layout result. `Inspector.onLoad` switches from `replaceFramework` to `applyLoadedFramework`. The seam choice was load-bearing: `replaceFramework` is also called by the JSON-tab edit path, where auto-layouting would discard the user's manual node positions — ADR-0020's "nodePositions is editor-local view state" invariant. A third unit test pins this (`replaceFramework_does_not_auto_layout_so_JSON_tab_edits_preserve_manual_positions`) — a regression-guard that would BREAK on a naïve move of layout into `replaceFramework`. `layoutGraph` itself widens its generic signature from narrow `(GraphNode[], GraphEdge[]) => GraphNode[]` to `<N extends Node, E extends Edge>(N[], E[]) => N[]` so the Builder's narrower agent/tool/skill/hitl/hook node types flow through (both existing callers — `GraphCanvas`, `TesterGraphPane` — continue to pass `GraphNode[]` unchanged). A `window.__builderStore` expose parallels `window.__graphStore` (per `src/App.tsx:50-52`) for the tauri-driver real-app test seam — no production-only conditional. The regression test (`tests/e2e-tauri/builder_load_aria.e2e.ts`) drives the real Tauri app: load `examples/aria/` → assert ≥2 distinct node positions (not the {0,0} pile) AND ≥1 `.react-flow__edge` rendered. The structural composition: Stage B made `projectCanvasEdges` see inline agents (so edges paint); Stage D wired the dagre layout into the load (so nodes occupy distinct positions). 🟡 #4 (stack-on-load) is RESOLVED.

- **The Palette as a third item source** (Stage E). `src/components/builder/Palette.tsx::paletteItemsForTab` becomes `(tab, installed, framework)` — the three sources unioned, deduped by `(kind, ref)` with built-ins → installed → framework precedence (installed wins on a collision; the framework source is the document-reference fallback). New helpers `frameworkItemsForKind` + `dedupeByKindRef` + a `PaletteItemSource = 'builtin' | 'installed' | 'framework'` discriminant; a `data-source` HTML attribute per `<li>` (the testable invariant); a visible `· framework` badge that distinguishes framework-sourced items at a glance. The dedup test surfaced its own tautology at red — a bare `length === 1` check passed on `main` pre-E because the framework source isn't read at all, so the installed-only result happens to have length 1. Tightened to assert `data-source="installed"` on the survivor (an attribute that doesn't exist pre-E) — the test then failed right-reason. The Palette's `useBuilderStore((s) => s.framework)` selector is a bare-object selector (returns the same reference until `set()` swaps it) so no `useShallow` is needed; gotcha #75 applies only to derived array/filter/map selectors. The regression (`tests/e2e-tauri/builder_palette_aria.e2e.ts`) drives the real Tauri app: load `examples/aria/` → assert ARIA's `orchestrator` agent appears in the Palette Agents tab with `data-source="framework"`.

What's solid (cumulative): M08.6 ships ADR-0022 as designed — one resolution boundary in `load_framework`, an exact-inverse re-split in `save_framework`, downstream consumers untouched. The construction-reachability chain (A's four wires `inputs_reachable="false"` on `main`; B/C/D/E each invert one to `"true"`; V's Wire pass confirms each closure against the shipped code) executes the M08 A→F1 pattern cleanly. Strict v1.8 two-commit TDD held on all four code stages — every red commit is standalone with the falsifiable hypothesis stated, every impl commit's `git diff <red>..<impl> -- '<tests>'` is EMPTY, no amend dances. The audit-first-author-second pattern from M08.6.A (the phase-doc audit commit `6936106` against the M08.5.5 cumulative carry-forward) collapsed Stage A's intake friction to near-zero and the pre-resolved carry-forward routings flowed forward through every subsequent stage. Schema-as-source-of-truth held (no schema change). Archetype-fidelity held — every regression test on the central surfaces loads the real `examples/aria/` (and where relevant `examples/ralph/`) — closing the structural shape of the M08 escape (the M08 Builder shipped green because the archetype was never in the test loop). Gotcha #66 closure is explicit.

What's structurally weak and likely to compound: (1) **`builder/persist.rs` per-file coverage at 84.73% line is below the 95% per-file aspiration** despite the package gate `runtime-main` 95.40% line ≥95 PASSING. The strict v1.8 invariant locks the test files post-red; phase-doc B.4 + C.4 enumerated the central regressions but not every error-path branch (broken-tool-ref, broken-skill-ref, no-frontmatter-found, YAML-parse-error, the `is_outside_framework_dir` true branch, the Object-variant write paths). M08.6.V 🟡 #2; resolution: M09.A adds targeted error-path tests OR records the aggregate-passes policy explicitly. (2) **Two multi-call invariants lack per-surface tests** — `load_framework(examples/aria/)` twice → identical result (the surface is structurally pure but not pinned by a test); `applyLoadedFramework(A) → applyLoadedFramework(B)` replaces A's positions with B's fresh layout (structurally correct via Zustand `set()` wholesale-replacement but not pinned). Two ~5-min tests due; M08.6.V 🟡 #1. (3) **Two defensive `FrameworkAgentsItem::Object` branches are structurally unreachable on a loaded framework post-ADR-0022** — `walker.rs::agents_item_id:169` + `capability_map::inline_agents:324-333`. TD-028 (logged this closeout). Tighten to `unreachable!()` once the renderer surface is confirmed never to produce Object variants in `builderStore.framework.agents[]` (it doesn't today). (4) **No e2e-tauri assertion that the Inspector capability summary populates on loaded ARIA** — the Stage A 🟡 #5 triage hypothesis (Stage B's resolution incidentally fixes the blank summary) is structurally sound and V's Wire pass confirmed it, but no test asserts the rendered surface text is non-empty. TD-029.

What surprised: the M08.6.A intake's zero-friction outcome (a strong audit-first-author-second pattern signal); the schema asymmetry surfaced twice at red phase (B + C) where phase-doc text described the behavior correctly but underspecified the generated-type reality; the HashMap canonicalization carried a latent regression-guard exposure (the M08-era byte-stability test passed only because its fixture had no HashMap content); the Inspector.test.tsx reframe at Stage D had a narrow blast radius (exactly ONE test affected — the ADR-0020 single-source-of-truth model pays forward at refactor time); the Palette additive-source had zero impact on existing tests (the default `emptyFramework()` has empty arrays, the new framework source contributes zero items at default). Time-box ratio ~0.24–0.34× across A–E + V (consistent under-run, mirroring the M08.5 + M08.5.5 calibration pattern).

### Adherence to spec

The M08.6 acceptance bar maps to MVP §M8 criteria + ADR-0022 (the Builder loads, renders, persists the archetype frameworks). Citations against shipped code + the regression test that demonstrates each:

- ✅ **MVP §M8 criterion 8 — reload from disk → canvas reconstructs identical to save state.** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/persist.rs::load_framework` (the resolver) + `save_framework` (the re-split + `serde_json::Value` canonicalization for byte-stability). Demonstrated by `crates/runtime-main/tests/framework_save_resplit.rs::save_then_load_round_trips_a_modular_framework` + `save_load_save_is_byte_stable_on_a_modular_framework` (the byte-stable invariant) — both **load the real `examples/aria/`** (the archetype-fidelity closure of gotcha #66). The pre-existing `save_load_save_cycle_is_byte_stable` (`crates/runtime-main/tests/builder.rs:609`) is preserved + now strengthened (it passed `main` only because its empty-HashMap fixture masked the iteration trap).
- ✅ **ADR-0022 — canonical framework representation, single-resolution-boundary.** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/persist.rs::load_framework` is the single boundary; `save_framework` is its exact inverse. V's Wire pass grep-confirmed: every `serde_yaml` + frontmatter parse + path-ref resolution lives in `persist.rs` and its test files only. No `.md` resolution leaks into `src/lib/builderStore.ts`, the Tester, `spawn_framework_subagents`, `framework_capability_summary`, or any other consumer — they all consume the resolved inline `Framework`. ADR-0022 flipped Proposed → Accepted at the M08.6.B impl commit (`b2acf41`).
- ✅ **ADR-0022 — cross-framework `../` references resolve.** Code: `load_framework` resolves `dir.join(path)` deliberately (no glob, no symlink-escape). Demonstrated by `crates/runtime-main/tests/framework_load_resolution.rs::load_framework_resolves_ralph_cross_framework_refs` — loads `examples/ralph/`, asserts `../aria/tools/…` references resolve.
- ✅ **ADR-0022 — broken reference is a `BuilderError`, not a silent drop.** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/error.rs::BuilderError::ReferenceResolution { reference, cause }` (the new variant). Demonstrated by `crates/runtime-main/tests/framework_load_resolution.rs::load_framework_broken_reference_is_a_builder_error` — a `tempfile` framework whose `framework.json` references a missing `.md` returns the error variant naming the bad reference. Partial-inline-framework gap-tolerance preserved (`crates/runtime-main/tests/framework_load_resolution.rs::load_framework_partial_framework_still_loads`).
- ✅ **🟡 #4 (loaded framework stacks at {0,0}) — RESOLVED.** Code: `src/lib/builderStore.ts::applyLoadedFramework` (the load-only seam) + `src/lib/layout.ts::layoutGraph` (reused; widened generic). Demonstrated by `tests/e2e-tauri/builder_load_aria.e2e.ts` — load `examples/aria/` in the running Builder, assert ≥2 distinct node positions AND ≥1 React Flow edge. The load-only invariant (auto-layout fires on LOAD only, not on every framework mutation) pinned by `tests/unit/lib/builderStore.loadLayout.test.ts::replaceFramework_does_not_auto_layout_so_JSON_tab_edits_preserve_manual_positions`.
- ✅ **A loaded framework's resolved artifacts surface in the Palette as reusable drag sources.** Code: `src/components/builder/Palette.tsx::paletteItemsForTab(tab, installed, framework)` + the new `frameworkItemsForKind` + `dedupeByKindRef` helpers + the `PaletteItemSource` discriminant + the `data-source` HTML attribute + the visible `· framework` badge. Demonstrated by `tests/e2e-tauri/builder_palette_aria.e2e.ts` — load `examples/aria/` in the running Builder, assert ARIA's `orchestrator` agent appears in the Palette Agents tab with `data-source="framework"`. Dedup precedence (built-ins → installed → framework) pinned by `tests/unit/components/builder/Palette.test.tsx`'s `palette_de_duplicates_a_kind_ref_present_in_both_installed_and_framework` (the tautology-fixed version asserting `data-source="installed"` on the survivor).
- ✅ **ADR-0020 — `nodePositions` is editor-local view state, preserved through JSON-tab edits.** The Stage D load-only seam (`applyLoadedFramework` vs `replaceFramework`) preserves the ADR-0020 invariant. Pinned by the third unit test (above) — `replaceFramework_does_not_auto_layout`.
- ✅ **`spec §6` Framework JSON Loader.** Code: `load_framework`'s resolution + the existing schema validation pipeline (unchanged — ADR-0022 reconciles between forms the schema already permits via the `oneOf(inline | {id,path})` on `agents[]`).
- ✅ **`spec §0b` Tool/Skill/Agent model.** The agent `.md` body is captured on resolution per `agent.v1.json::system_prompt_template`; *applying* it at run time is the M09 carry-forward (M08.5 decision 1 reaffirmed). Captured here; M09 applies.
- ✅ **`schemas/framework.v1.json` unchanged** — M08.6 reconciles between two forms the schema already permits. No schema bump, no §14 schema ADR.

### Spec review (forward-looking)

- **Missing items:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §6 — the spec describes the loader at a behavioral level but does not name the modular-vs-inline framework-representation reconciliation (the structural premise ADR-0022 introduces). A one-paragraph addition to §6 noting that the canonical on-disk form is the modular multi-file `{id, path}` representation, resolved at the loader boundary into the inline form downstream consumers speak, would let a future reader of the spec arrive at ADR-0022 from spec context rather than having to read the ADR alone.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §9 — the Phase 9 Canvas description does not name an auto-layout-on-load contract. M08.6 Stage D's `applyLoadedFramework` is the load-only seam (per ADR-0020's `nodePositions` editor-local-view-state invariant); a one-line note in §9 would pin the load-vs-edit asymmetry.
- **Contradictions:** None unresolved.
- **Ambiguity / §12-owned technical decisions the build resolved:**
  - **Schema asymmetry between agents and tools/skills.** The phase doc B.3.2 described the resolution behavior uniformly across agents/tools/skills, but only `FrameworkAgentsItem` has an inline `oneOf` variant in `framework.v1.json` (resolved via typify into `crates/runtime-core/src/generated/framework.rs:1375`); `FrameworkSkillsItem` (`:2786`) and `FrameworkToolsItem` (`:3029`) are flat structs. Resolved at Stage B: agents flip variant (`Object → Agent(_)`); tools/skills get their bodies captured as `Companion`s. A §12-owned implementation decision documented in the B retrospective + B's impl commit body. Forward: the schema asymmetry could be documented as a one-line note in `agent.v1.json` / `tool.v1.json` / `skill.v1.json` headers OR in the §6 spec addition above.
  - **HashMap iteration breaks byte-stable serialization.** The phase doc C.3 required "preserve the deterministic serialization (pretty-print, stable field order, trailing newline)" — but typify generates `HashMap<String, _>` fields on `Framework` whose iteration is randomized. Resolved at Stage C: route through `serde_json::Value` for canonicalization before `to_string_pretty`; alphabetical field order is the stable order. A §12-owned technical decision (Stage C). The behavioral change (alphabetical `framework.json` field order, was struct-definition order) is deliberate; no test asserted struct-order. Forward: the v1.9 STAGE-PROMPT-PROTOCOL.md candidate "Schema/contract reality check" would catch this class at phase-doc authoring time.
  - **Auto-layout fires on LOAD only, not on every framework mutation.** Stage D's seam choice: `applyLoadedFramework` (new, runs layout) vs `replaceFramework` (preserved, no layout). The phase doc D.3 named both options + the load-only invariant; the build chose the new-action seam over a `replaceFramework({ autoLayout })` option to keep ADR-0020's invariant explicit at the call site. A §12-owned technical decision; the third unit test is its regression guard.
  - **Palette dedup precedence: built-ins → installed → framework.** Stage E's design: installed wins on a `(kind, ref)` collision (installed entries carry version pins + install timestamps + L3 reports; a framework reference is a document reference; built-ins are runtime primitives that never displace). A §12-owned technical decision (E retro [LIVE] Design decisions); the `palette_de_duplicates_a_kind_ref_present_in_both_installed_and_framework` test pins the precedence.
- **Recommended spec changes:** A focused post-M08.6 `docs(spec):` pass — the §6 modular-vs-inline reconciliation paragraph (with a forward pointer to ADR-0022); the §9 auto-layout-on-load contract; the schema-asymmetry note (header of `agent.v1.json` vs `tool.v1.json` / `skill.v1.json`, OR in the §6 addition). Smaller than the post-M08 batch; not blocking.

### Fix backlog

Severity is non-elastic. Critical = "must fix before M09 starts."

- 🔴 **Critical** (must fix before M09 starts):
  - **None.** Stage V produced **zero 🔴**. M08.6 ships no spec-contract drift requiring a pre-M09 fix.

- 🟡 **Important** (should fix this release cycle):
  - **M08.6.V 🟡 #1 — multi-call invariants lack per-surface tests for two of the four named invariants.** Owner: code / M09.A. `crates/runtime-main/tests/framework_load_resolution.rs` (11 tests) does not assert `load_framework(examples/aria/)` twice → identical resolved `Framework`. `tests/unit/lib/builderStore.loadLayout.test.ts` (3 tests) does not assert `applyLoadedFramework(A) → applyLoadedFramework(B)` replaces A's positions with B's fresh layout. The underlying behaviors are structurally correct (`load_framework` is a pure function over the on-disk framework; `applyLoadedFramework` is a Zustand `set()` that replaces `framework + nodePositions` wholesale), so the absence is a test-coverage gap, not a behavior defect. Two ~5-min tests due. Resolution: a quick `M08.6.F1` follow-up commit (build's call) OR fold into M09.A `<read_prior_milestones>`.
  - **M08.6.V 🟡 #2 — `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/persist.rs` per-file coverage 84.73% line below the 95% per-file aspiration.** Owner: code / M09.A. Package gate `runtime-main` 95.40% line ≥ 95 PASSES (the aggregate gate is the enforced mirror — the M08.6 surface lifted the package gate; per-file under-coverage is below the aspiration but above zero). 53 of 347 lines uncovered — mostly the error-path branches of `BuilderError::ReferenceResolution` (broken-tool-ref + broken-skill-ref are not exercised; only broken-agent-ref is), `is_outside_framework_dir` save-side branch, Object-variant write paths (`persist.rs:141-153`), the cross-framework save preserve path, no-frontmatter-found, YAML-parse-error. The strict v1.8 invariant locks the test file post-red so additional error-path tests would land as a separate labelled follow-up. Resolution paths (M09.A's call): (a) add targeted tests for the uncovered branches (~30–45 min, +10pp on persist.rs per-file); or (b) explicit policy entry in `docs/coverage-policy.md` §C M08.6 noting aggregate-passes is the gate intent and per-file divergence is acceptable. Recommend (a) — the uncovered surface is the very `BuilderError::ReferenceResolution` path ADR-0022 added; an error-branch unit test pays the gate target directly. The coverage policy reconciliation appended to §C in this closeout reflects (b)-style language pending the M09.A decision.
  - **🔴 #4 (tier UI/backend desync) — carried to M09** (NOT framework-representation work; Stage A triage routed). `src/components/SettingsPanel.tsx` + `src-tauri/src/commands.rs::request_tier_transition`. Joined with 🟡 #6 (UI does not disclosure-gate by tier) as the M09 tier-state-machine work block.
  - **🔴 #5 (Builder Canvas state not persisted across app restart) — carried to M09 UX work** (default route per Stage A's static analysis: no autoload exists; user must Load on each launch; fix is "save reminder on quit" + "Open Recent" Inspector surface). The static evidence (`src/lib/builderStore.ts:460` initial state is `emptyFramework()`; no `localStorage` / autoload read; `Inspector.tsx:76-89` `onLoad` is the only load path requiring explicit user action) strongly supports interpretation (a) UX issue. Conditional: an IRL re-walk during M09 Stage 0 may surface interpretation (b) (save-then-restore broken); if so, route to a save-path adjacent surface.
  - **`system_prompt_template` application gap — carried to M09.** M08.6 Stage B's loader CAPTURES the agent `.md` body in the resolved `Agent` (per `agent.v1.json::system_prompt_template`); APPLYING it at run time is the M09 generator/run carry-forward (the M08.5 decision 1 reaffirmed; the M08.6 Background section confirmed). M09's generator wiring + the `run_agent` system-prompt construction site are the natural homes.
  - **The 13 🟡 + 🟢 elevation triage carry-forward from M08.5 IRL + M08.5.5 IRL re-verify** — Stage A recorded routing per item with file:line evidence: tier-UI 🟡 (Promote-label not updating; Settings panel always-visible bar; UI does not disclosure-gate) → M09 (joined with 🔴 #4); Builder-validation 🟡 (invalid agent id format `demo-agent@1.0.0`; missing `capabilities` block; `session_root_agent` no UI surface; Configure modal no Save guidance; Inspector→Save no filename preload) → M09; UX 🟡 (cryptic MCP error; Command-vs-Args modal split) → M09; resolved-by-prior-work 🟡 (wdio workspace path, sibling subprocess build, Edge 148+ dragstart) — verified resolved on `main`; the docs-fix 🟡 #8 (`docs/M08-irl-test-plan.md` stale `transport_type` → `transport`) — RESOLVED at Stage A as a docs-only commit; 🟢 elevation (TD-009 strip ALL M0N from UI + version display) → M09 (deferred from Stage D fold-in attempt — not co-located zero-risk). Recorded.
  - **In-process seam architecture ADR** (M04+M05+M06+M07+M08 carry-forward, STILL OPEN). Owner: docs. The `*_with` seam + `Arc<dyn _>` injection pattern is demonstrated again at M08.6.B (`load_framework` is itself a path-agnostic `&Path`-parameterised public API, the same architecture pattern). The cumulative archetype count remains ~8×; the ADR remains overdue.
  - **v1.9 protocol iteration cluster** (M08 + M08.6 carry-forward consolidation). Owner: docs / protocol. ### Simplify pass outcome (v1.6 `<simplify_pass>`)

Per the M08.6.F `<deliverables><simplify_pass>`. One read-only review agent (the `code-simplifier` agent) ran against the cumulative M08.6 diff (`main..HEAD` = `6c486c5..b2819be`, 14 commits across A–E + V). **Proposal pass — `<approval_required>true</approval_required>` — no changes auto-applied.** Aggregate verdict: **the cumulative M08.6 diff is structurally sound.** The milestone's primary obligations are met correctly — `load_framework` is the single resolution boundary (V's Wire pass grep-confirmed); `save_framework` is its exact inverse; the canonicalization through `serde_json::Value` is one line at the right place; `applyLoadedFramework` is the load-only seam preserving ADR-0020's editor-local-view-state invariant; `paletteItemsForTab(tab, installed, framework)` composes the three sources with deterministic dedup precedence + a visible discriminator. No O(N²) loops, no unbounded allocations, no hot-path re-derivation material at v0.1 scale. The findings:

| ID | Proposal | Sev | Recommendation |
|---|---|---|---|
| RU-M08.6-1 | Extract shared `split_frontmatter` from `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/persist.rs:422-429` to `runtime-core` (a near-identical pattern exists in `crates/runtime-core/tests/round_trip.rs:140` as a test-local one-liner) | Med | Defer → TD-030.
