## M08.7 — Execution Engine (rungs 1–5 / M08.7a) (2026-06-02, Closeout commit on parent-milestone branch `claude/m08.7-execution-engine`)

> Author: Claude (per `CLAUDE.md` §20)
> Stages aggregated: M08.7.X (Stage-0 authoring — the eval-first-ladder phase doc + `docs/execution-status.md` seed; zero code), M08.7.A (rung 1 — the in-process built-in tool executor: `Read`/`Write` run via `execute_builtin` + feed the result back into the next turn through `TurnFeedback::dispatched`; surfaced the never-wired grant-loading gap), M08.7.B (rung 2 — capability enforcement gates a LIVE tool: out-of-scope `Write` → `CapabilityViolation` + no file on disk; the tier-wiring gap), M08.7.C (rung 3 — `LoadSkill` injects the skill body into context via the tool-result feedback contract; ADR-0027 Proposed; the resolved-body-not-threaded gap + the spec §0b vs ADR-0027-sketch contradiction), M08.7.D (rung 4 — `request_capability` gap detection wired → clean suspend-and-record loop-break; ADR-0029 pulled resolve-and-resume into v0.1), M08.7.E (rung 5 — budget enforcement at the run loop: per-turn `record_spend` → warn/downshift/hard-stop, idempotent; the never-wired budget caller), M08.7.V (the five-pass verifier incl. the v1.9 5th `assembled_execution` pass — 0🔴 / 1🟡 / 2🟢; Sound).
> Reviewed against: `agent-runtime-spec.md` §0–§0d, §0b (Tool/Skill/Agent model), §2a (budget), §4 + §4b (gap flow), §6 (Framework JSON Loader), §8.security (L1 capability gate, `narrow()`); `docs/MVP-v0.1.md` §M8 execution criteria; ADR-0028 (built-in tool execution contract — filed at this closeout per V's 🟡 #1, flipped Proposed → Accepted here), ADR-0027 (skill-into-context injection — filed Proposed at Stage C, flipped Accepted here), ADR-0029 (gap resolve-and-resume — landed on `main` via PR #119; this branch deduped its on-branch copy to defer to the canonical), ADR-0026 (plan-loop-vdr routing — unchanged, already Accepted), ADR-0019 (Tester isolated session — the HITL/tier model rungs 2/4/5 respect); `docs/execution-status.md` (the paints→executes ledger seeded at M08.7.X; rows 1/3/4 flipped on observed behavior, the Budget row flipped engine-tested); `docs/cluster-pattern.md` §1 (eval-first ladder), §2 (zero-propagation), §4 (assert side effects), §5 (mutation gate); `docs/coverage-policy.md` §A–§D; `docs/M08.6-irl-findings.md` (the 7🔴 carry-forward source); `docs/tech-debt.md` (this closeout adds TD-039/040 from V's 🟢 + TD-041/042 from the simplify-pass; references TD-033/035/036/037/038 extended by the rungs); M01–M08.6 gap-analysis entries.
> M08.7 is a milestone-class follow-on to M08.6 (not in the original M01–M11 sequence; cut to answer the M08.6-IRL load-bearing finding — *the runtime paints most of what it claims*). It ships **M08.7a only** — rungs 1–5, the single-agent execution primitives. Rungs 6–N (sub-agents, plan, hooks, MCP-#23 fix, ARIA composition) + the gap **resume** half (ADR-0029) moved to **M08.9**; the in-app surfaces (budget cap, the 32 Builder findings, the Grant/Install/Decline gap UI) moved to **the app-workbench milestone (M08.8)** per the 2026-06-01 front-to-back re-scope (ORCHESTRATOR §next-action; ADR-0029). Cumulative M08.7 diff: 49 commits (`main...HEAD`; 40 files, ~8.3k insertions), five code rungs A–E + Stage-0 authoring + Stage V.

### Codebase deep dive (cumulative — M01 + M02 + M03 + M04 + M05 + M06 + M07 + M08 + M08.6 + M08.7)

M08.7 is the milestone that makes the runtime **run**. Through M08.6 the Builder could author, load, render, and persist the archetype frameworks — but the M08.6-IRL walk found the load-bearing fact the build machinery had never observed: *the runtime paints most of what it claims — only provider-streaming + MCP execute; built-in tools, sub-agents, skills, gaps, plans, and hooks emit live-graph events and stop.* M08.7a closes the single-agent half of that gap as an **eval-first ladder of clusters** (`docs/cluster-pattern.md` §1): each rung isolates one execution function against a minimal hand-authored framework, closes only when the **assembled** thing runs and the **side effect** is observed (CLAUDE.md §4 rule 11), and flips its `docs/execution-status.md` row from `paints` to `executes — observed` with an eval cite (E-01..E-05). The through-line that every rung confirmed: the project's execution primitives were each **fully built and unit-tested, then never wired to the live run loop** — rung 1 found no production path loaded a framework's `file_access` into the L1 enforcer; rung 2 found no path set the tier on the live enforcer; rung 3 found `LoadedFramework.companions` (the resolved skill bodies) dropped before the run path; rung 4 found the gap handler's docstring described a "suspend" with no caller and no resume; rung 5 found the budget enforcer's docstring named a "caller (SDK turn loop)" that never existed. The scaffolding was real; the wire from scaffolding to the executing loop was the missing piece, rung after rung.

The shipped surfaces:

- **The built-in tool executor** (rung 1, Stage A). `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/builtin_tools.rs::execute_builtin` dispatches exactly two built-ins — `Read` (`:91`) and `Write` (`:102`) — running in-process, bounded by the requesting agent's `file_access` capability scope. The load-bearing wire is in `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/agent_sdk.rs`: `drive_stream` routes a built-in `ToolUse` into `TurnFeedback::dispatched` (NOT `pipeline.next_event`), and `run_agent` feeds the collected results back as the next turn's input (one assistant message carrying the `ToolUse`s, one user message carrying the matching `tool_result`s — the Anthropic continuation contract), re-streaming until a turn dispatches no tool. This is the archetype ADR-0028 freezes; every later rung is a branch of this same dispatch→feedback shape. Stage A surfaced (and the maintainer resolved) the collision with 4 pre-existing M06 contract tests that pinned the *painted* `Exec/<toolname>` grant model using `Read` as the example tool — those were re-pointed to a non-built-in name; the `file_access`-scope-is-the-boundary decision (over the M06 `Exec` grant) is recorded in `builtin_tools.rs` docs + TD-033 (defense-in-depth deferred).

- **Capability enforcement on a live tool** (rung 2, Stage B). The L1 `CapabilityEnforcer` now gates a built-in **before** the side effect: an out-of-scope `Write` emits `CapabilityViolation{Write}` and **no file is written**; an in-scope `Write` writes it. The wire was a one-line `enforcer.set_tier(tier)` in the run-path construction plus the `run_test_session_with` tier delegation — the enforcer + `capabilities_to_declarations` existed since M05/M06 but nothing set the live tier. The behavior is asserted on the **file side effect** (`crates/runtime-main/tests/capability_live_tool.rs`), not the event. The scope-gate `CapabilityViolation` is assembled-observed only — the real-app Tester runs at Novice (TD-036), so the real-app scope-watch is deferred to the tier-wire + UI rung.

- **Skill-into-context injection** (rung 3, Stage C). `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/load_skill.rs` + the `drive_stream` `LoadSkill` branch inject the resolved skill markdown body into the agent's context as the `LoadSkill` `tool_result` (ADR-0027), which persists in `config.messages` across turns (the multi-turn re-send mechanism). Ground-at-red caught that `FrameworkSkillsItem` is reference-only and the resolved body lives in `LoadedFramework.companions[]`, which the run path (`run_test_session_with(&Framework)`) **drops** — so the rung threaded a `resolved_skills: BTreeMap<String,String>` onto `CapabilityWiring` (additive `with_resolved_skills` builder + a `run_test_session_with_skills` seam; resolved once at load per ADR-0022, not re-resolved). It also surfaced a spec↔doc contradiction (spec §0b: "tool result returns the skill body" vs the phase-doc ADR-0027 sketch's system_prompt-append) — surfaced per CLAUDE.md §2 (do not pick); the maintainer chose the spec-compliant tool-result model; ADR-0027 records the system_prompt/three-tier model as the forward path. The behavior-change (real Anthropic replies in ALL CAPS to a `shout` skill) is the maintainer's IRL close; the real-app Builder-Tester skill IRL is deferred (TD-037 — the v0.1 canvas authors no skill bodies to thread).

- **Gap detection → clean suspend** (rung 4, Stage D). The `drive_stream` `request_capability` branch routes the meta-tool to `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/request_capability.rs::handle_request_capability` (NOT `pipeline.next_event`), the `*Missing` gap fires with `requested_via=request_capability`, and the run loop **suspends** via a loop-break (`TurnFeedback.gap_suspended` → `run_agent` break) — exactly one provider turn, clean `Ok`, the gap left unresolved (no `tool_result` fed back). Ground-at-red found the painted behavior was actually a `CapabilityViolation` (the undeclared meta-tool hits the L1 enforcer), more clearly wrong than the doc predicted, and that the docstring's "awaiter" shape (`await_capability_violation_hitl`) was wrong — its await-then-continue semantics + test-defaults no-op both fail a gap, which must halt. The maintainer's 2026-06-01 direction turned the suspend-only close into **ADR-0029** (gap resolve-and-resume pulled into v0.1, web-best-practice-grounded: durable checkpoint-resume + idempotent rebuild + governed HITL re-authorization); the resume half is the scheduled M08.9 gap-resume rung. The suspend behavior is asserted (one turn, clean halt, gap unresolved), not the event alone.

- **Budget enforcement at the run loop** (rung 5, Stage E). `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/agent_sdk.rs::dispatch_budget_actions` (built in `run_agent` from the already-threaded `CapabilityWiring.framework.budget` block — `tester.rs` needed no change) maps the per-turn ladder verdict to actions: `Warn` emits `BudgetWarn` and does not stop; `Downshift` swaps the model for subsequent turns; `HardStop` breaks the loop with `BudgetExceeded` in the trace and issues **no further turn**; the threshold is idempotent across turns. Real per-turn cost flows `CostBreakdown → estimate_cost → record_spend` (V's Wire pass confirmed it is not hardcoded). The four `Budget*` events pre-exist in `event.v1.json` (no schema change). `Warn`'s "notifier" is the in-app toast (event-driven by `BudgetWarn`); the OS desktop notifier is TD-038. Budget `Suspend` is not a dead-end — it folds into ADR-0029 (generalized to budget). Rung 5 is **engine-tested only**: the assembled wire test (`budget_runloop_execution.rs`) observes the actions under a stub provider; the live real-model tiny-cap halt (`budget_live.rs`) is `#[ignore]d`; there was no maintainer real-app IRL this rung; the in-app budget surface (Settings cap + cross-restart persistence, M08.6-IRL #22) is deferred to M08.8.

What's solid: the dispatch→feedback wire is singular and production-rooted — V's Wire pass traced every rung-3/4/5 execution claim to a real `drive_stream` call site (`agent_sdk.rs:619/642/681`), not a `#[cfg(test)]` harness; the "no production caller" condition that defined the M08.6 escape (and M08.V 🟡 #2 for `plan_loop`) did not recur on any shipped rung. Strict v1.8 two-commit TDD held on all five code rungs (every `git diff <red>..<impl> -- '**/tests/**'` EMPTY, re-confirmed at V's Inventory). Behavior over event held: every rung asserts the side effect (file on disk, turn-count halt, suspend = one provider turn, skill body in the turn-2 config), never the emitted event alone — no gotcha-#66 / M08.6-#32-class trap. The execution-status ledger flipped rows 1/3/4 on observed behavior (E-01..E-04, with maintainer IRL for 1/3/4) and the Budget row engine-tested (E-05), and left rows 2/5/6 honestly `paints`. ADR-0028 records the archetype; coverage held with no gate change (`runtime-main` 96.23% line ≥ 95; workspace 92.12% ≥ 80; the four new modules all > 95).

What's structurally weak and likely to compound: (1) **The five execution rungs are grounded at the assembled-stub granularity, not end-to-end-in-the-app.** V ran 40/40 assembled tests + the full `runtime-main` suite (0 failures); rungs 1/3/4 additionally got a maintainer IRL watch with a real model; but rung 5 (budget) is engine-tested only, and ARIA composition (rung N) is not built. The milestone's honest claim is "the engine RUNs each primitive, observed via eval / RUST_LOG / per-rung IRL," not "the full app was driven end-to-end." TD-034 (the agent-output / live-graph execution view) is the in-app observability surface that would let the maintainer watch execution in the app, and it is M08.8. (2) **`agent_sdk.rs` per-file line coverage is 92.35%** (165/1200 region-uncovered) — below the 95% per-file aspiration though the package gate passes at 96.23%; the run loop's budget/dispatch error branches are the uncovered surface. (3) **`key_store.rs` at 59.63% line** is a pre-existing low-coverage island (not M08.7 work) that the package aggregate masks. (4) **The Budget row's "executes — observed" is at the engine level only** — a reader must not read it as "the in-app budget cap works"; #22 (the IRL-found persistence bug) is untouched.

What surprised: the "scaffolding built around an execution core, never wired to the loop" pattern recurred **all five rungs** (grant-loading, tier-wiring, resolved-body threading, gap-suspend-with-no-caller, budget-caller-that-never-existed) — the single strongest signal of the milestone and the structural confirmation of the M08.6-IRL thesis. Ground-at-red caught a phase-doc inaccuracy on every code rung (rung 1: existing tests pin the now-reserved built-in names; rung 3: the resolved body is in `companions`, not on `Framework`; rung 4: the painted behavior is a `CapabilityViolation`, not a `ToolInvoked`, and the awaiter shape is wrong; rung 5: `tester.rs` needed no change) — the red trace, not the phase-doc prediction, was the source of truth (rule 11). The time-box landed **within range** on every stage — a marked change from the M08.6 / M08.5 chronic ~0.24–0.34× under-run; the eval-first ladder's per-rung scoping (one function, one minimal framework, one eval) produced estimates that matched reality.

### Adherence to spec

The M08.7a acceptance bar maps to MVP §M8's execution criteria + ADR-0028/0027 + the §0b/§2a/§4/§4b/§8.security primitives. Each rung's execute-is-real claim is cited against the shipped code + the assembled regression (the eval) that demonstrates it — never inferred from structure (rule 11):

- ✅ **Built-in tool execution (rung 1; spec §0b, §8.security L1; ADR-0028 §1).** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/builtin_tools.rs::execute_builtin` (`Read`/`Write`) + the `drive_stream`→`TurnFeedback::dispatched`→`run_agent` feedback wire (`agent_sdk.rs`). Demonstrated by **E-01** `crates/runtime-main/tests/builtin_tool_execution.rs` — an allowed `Read` runs, the file contents feed back as a `tool_result`, and the agent **quotes them** in its final text; + maintainer IRL 2026-05-31 (RUST_LOG chain: `Read(Cargo.toml)` → tool result(content) → agent stream quoted `[package]`). Assertion on the quoted side effect, not the event.
- ✅ **Capability enforcement gates a live tool (rung 2; spec §8.security L1; ADR-0028 §2).** Code: the L1 `CapabilityEnforcer` gate on the live `Write` path + the `set_tier` wire. Demonstrated by **E-02** `crates/runtime-main/tests/capability_live_tool.rs` — a Promoted out-of-scope `Write` emits `CapabilityViolation{Write}` and **leaves no file on disk**; an in-scope `Write` writes the file. Assertion on the absent/present file, not the event. ⚠️ Scope-gate is assembled-observed only; the real-app scope-watch is deferred (TD-036 — production Tester runs Novice).
- ✅ **Skill load injects into context + changes behavior (rung 3; spec §0b "tool result returns the skill body"; ADR-0027).** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/load_skill.rs` + the `LoadSkill` `drive_stream` branch + the `resolved_skills` thread on `CapabilityWiring`. Demonstrated by **E-03** `crates/runtime-main/tests/skill_load_execution.rs` (CI — the skill body present in the turn-2 `AgentConfig`) + `skill_load_live.rs` (`#[ignore]d` — real Anthropic behavior change) + maintainer IRL 2026-05-31 (`LoadSkill(shout)` → reply ALL CAPS: *"HELLO! WELCOME, AND THANKS FOR STOPPING BY!"*). Behavior-change asserted, not the `SkillLoaded` event. ⚠️ Real-app Builder-Tester skill IRL deferred (TD-037 — canvas authors no skill bodies in v0.1).
- ✅ **Gap detection suspends cleanly + recoverably (rung 4; spec §4 + §4b gap flow; §1b recovery).** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/request_capability.rs::handle_request_capability` + the `drive_stream` interception + the `gap_suspended` loop-break. Demonstrated by **E-04** `crates/runtime-main/tests/gap_detection_execution.rs` (CI assembled — `request_capability` routes to the handler not `pipeline.next_event`; the `*Missing` gap fires with `requested_via=request_capability`; the loop suspends in exactly one provider turn even when the same turn dispatched a tool; the four kind arms + the malformed no-suspend path) + `gap_detection_live.rs` (`#[ignore]d`) + maintainer IRL 2026-06-01 (a real model lacking `deploy` → `ToolMissing(deploy, requested_via=request_capability)` → clean suspend). Suspend asserted (one turn, clean halt, gap unresolved). ⚠️ The "recoverable" leg is proven indirectly (the gap event persists via `self.emit`); no assembled snapshot-rebuild assertion — TD-040; the **resume half is M08.9** (ADR-0029), not shipped here.
- ✅ **Budget enforcement at the run loop (rung 5; spec §2a).** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/agent_sdk.rs::dispatch_budget_actions` (built in `run_agent` from the threaded framework budget) — `record_spend` per turn → warn/downshift/hard-stop. Demonstrated by **E-05** `crates/runtime-main/tests/budget_runloop_execution.rs` (CI assembled — `record_spend` accumulates; the threshold halts the run + no further turn; `Downshift` swaps the model; `Warn` emits `BudgetWarn` + does not stop; idempotent across turns) + `budget_live.rs` (`#[ignore]d`). ⚠️ **Engine-tested only** — the real-model halt is `#[ignore]d`, no maintainer IRL this rung; the in-app budget surface (#22) is M08.8. The Budget row's "executes — observed" is at the engine granularity, NOT an in-app claim.
- ✅ **ADR-0028 — the built-in tool execution contract.** Code: the dispatch→feedback wire (§1), the `file_access`-scope boundary (§2), the in-process/sandbox split (§3 — corrected at this closeout to state only `Read`/`Write` are implemented; `Glob`/`Grep`/`WebFetch` are in-process-class-but-not-yet-wired; `Bash`/OS-spawn deferred to a separate ADR-class rung — to match `builtin_tools.rs:90` exactly, rule 11). Flipped Proposed → Accepted at this closeout.
- ✅ **ADR-0027 — skill-into-context injection.** The tool-result model (the body rides back as the `LoadSkill` `tool_result`, persisting in `config.messages`), capability-gated by `allowed_skills`. Flipped Proposed → Accepted at this closeout.
- ✅ **No schema change; sandbox boundary untouched (scope lock).** M08.7a touched no `schemas/*.v1.json`; the four `Budget*` events pre-existed; `Bash`/process-spawn/the sandbox protocol were not touched on any rung (Hard Rule 8 / §0d STANDARD-mode, in-process-only lock).
- ⚠️ **`request_capability` painted-behavior doc inaccuracy (rung 4).** The phase doc + table predicted "emits `ToolInvoked` for an unknown name and stops"; the red trace showed the real painted behavior is a `CapabilityViolation` (the undeclared meta-tool hits L1). Doc-only inaccuracy; the wire fixes it regardless — noted as a surprise, not a defect.
- ❌ **None.** No rung's execute-is-real claim failed against the shipped code; V produced zero 🔴.

### Spec review (forward-looking)

- **Missing items:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §0b — the spec says "tool result returns the skill body" but does not name the *persistence* mechanism (the body rides in `config.messages` and is re-sent every turn). ADR-0027 records this; a one-line §0b note that the skill body persists via accumulated message history (not a system-prompt append) would let a reader arrive at ADR-0027 from spec context, and would have pre-empted the rung-3 spec↔doc-sketch contradiction.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §4b — the gap flow describes `request_capability` → suspend → HITL → grant → resume, but does not name the v0.1 **suspend-only** boundary vs the resume half. ADR-0029 now owns the full loop; a §4b pointer to ADR-0029 (suspend = step 1; resume = the M08.9 gap-resume rung; idempotent rebuild is the load-bearing constraint) would pin the split.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §2a — budget is described behaviorally; the spec does not name *where* enforcement happens (per-turn at the run loop, `record_spend` after each turn's usage). A one-line note that the per-turn boundary is the enforcement point would pin rung 5's contract.
- **Contradictions:** None unresolved. The rung-3 spec §0b ↔ phase-doc ADR-0027-sketch contradiction was surfaced (§2, do not pick) and resolved to the spec model at Stage C.
- **Ambiguity / §12-owned technical decisions the build resolved:**
  - **`file_access`-scope vs the M06 `Exec/<toolname>` grant as the built-in boundary** (rung 1). Resolved: `file_access` scope is the authorization point (ADR-0028 §2); defense-in-depth (check both) deferred (TD-033). The `Exec` pipeline path stays for non-built-in tools.
  - **The suspend is a loop-break, not a HITL awaiter** (rung 4). Resolved: v0.1 has no resolve-and-resume machinery; reusing `await_capability_violation_hitl` (await-then-continue + test-defaults no-op) is wrong for a gap, which must halt. The new minimal `gap_suspended` break is the v0.1 suspend; the awaiter is built at the resume rung.
  - **Budget `Warn` does not emit `NotifierDispatched`** (rung 5). Resolved: `NotifierDispatched` is bound to a `HitlTriggerRef`; fabricating one for a budget warning is wrong. `Warn` emits `BudgetWarn` (the in-app toast); the OS notifier is TD-038.
- **Recommended spec changes:** A focused post-M08.7 `docs(spec):` pass — the §0b skill-body-persistence note (→ ADR-0027), the §4b suspend-vs-resume split (→ ADR-0029), the §2a per-turn enforcement note. Smaller than the post-M08.6 batch; not blocking.

### Fix backlog

Severity is non-elastic. Critical = "must fix before the next milestone starts."

- 🔴 **Critical:**
  - **None.** Stage V produced **zero 🔴**. M08.7a ships no spec-contract drift on a shipped rung requiring a pre-M08.8 fix. (The M08.6-IRL 7🔴 are real and open — see Carry-forward — but they are Builder/persistence/MCP/ARIA findings outside M08.7a's execution scope; their dispositions route to M08.8 / M08.9, none manufactured as M08.7-critical.)

- 🟡 **Important** (should fix this release cycle):
  - **The in-app execution-observability surface (TD-034) is unbuilt — execution is engine-observed, not app-observed.** Owner: M08.8 (app-workbench). Rungs 1/3/4 got a maintainer IRL via RUST_LOG; rung 5 is engine-tested only; ARIA composition is unbuilt. The app cannot yet *show* execution (the live-graph agent-output / execution view). Until TD-034 lands, "the runtime executes" is grounded at the assembled-stub + per-rung-IRL granularity, not end-to-end-in-the-app. This is the honest ceiling of M08.7a's claim.
  - **`agent_sdk.rs` per-file line coverage 92.35% below the 95% per-file aspiration** (package gate passes at 96.23%). Owner: code / a future runtime rung. The uncovered surface is the run loop's budget/dispatch error branches. Resolution: targeted error-branch tests at the next `agent_sdk.rs` touch (M08.9 sub-agent/plan rungs are the natural home), OR an explicit per-file-vs-aggregate policy note.
  - **The gap resume half (ADR-0029) is unbuilt — the gap loop dead-ends in v0.1 until M08.9.** Owner: M08.9 gap-resume rung (runtime) + M08.8 Grant/Install/Decline UI. The load-bearing assertion is the §1b idempotent rebuild (no re-execution of completed tool calls). TD-040 (rung-4 recoverable leg) is subsumed when it lands.
  - **In-process seam architecture ADR** (M04+M05+M06+M07+M08+M08.6 carry-forward, STILL OPEN). Owner: docs. The `*_with` seam + `Arc<dyn _>` injection pattern recurred at every M08.7 rung (the `run_test_session_with*` seams + `CapabilityWiring` builder additions). Cumulative archetype count now ~10×; the ADR remains overdue.

- 🟢 **Nice-to-have** (queue unless trivially incidental):
  - **TD-039** (rung-1 lacks an explicit two-reads-in-one-session feedback test; mechanism proven elsewhere) + **TD-040** (rung-4 "recoverable" proven indirectly, no assembled snapshot-rebuild assertion) — from V's 🟢 #2/#3; logged this closeout.
  - **TD-041** (`ToolUse` JSON input-field extraction reuse — wait-for-fourth-caller) + **TD-042** (`dispatch_budget_actions` model-chaining clarity on future extension) — from the closeout simplify-pass; logged this closeout. The other two simplify findings (CQ-M08.7-1 per-rung `is_some()` guards; CQ-M08.7-2 event-emit clones) were reviewed and the current form affirmed preferable — **no TD** (not deferrals).
  - **TD-033 / TD-035 / TD-037 / TD-038** — execution-time tool-auth (defense-in-depth); relative-path resolution made workspace-relative; canvas skill bodies (the real-app skill IRL substrate); OS budget-notifier. All open, advisory, extended by the M08.7 rungs.
  - All prior 🟢 advisory carry-forwards (TD-001..TD-032; release-build caching, token-scale curve, gotchas cross-ref index, keyring 4.0, `#[allow(reason=)]`) — STILL OPEN, advisory, unchanged by M08.7.

### Carry-forward from prior milestones — the M08.6-IRL 7🔴 with OBSERVED dispositions

> **Load-bearing (CLAUDE.md §20 + the closeout `<special_check>`).** The M08.6 gap-analysis signed off **0🔴 before the IRL walk**; the post-M08.6 IRL then found **7🔴**. This carry-forward records each with its disposition — **observed, run-not-inferred** (rule 11). The honest observed fact: **M08.7a closed NONE of the 7🔴 by direct action**, because M08.7a's scope (single-agent execution primitives) does **not overlap** the 7🔴 (which are Builder / persistence / MCP-spawn / ARIA-framework findings). The M08.6 IRL's own Tester scenario (D) was DEFERRED — the execution path was never exercised in that walk — so M08.7a addresses a *different* gap (the paints-not-executes class, TD-008) than the 7🔴. Each 🔴 below states what M08.7 OBSERVED about it (mostly: did not touch the path) and where it routes. None is marked resolved without observed evidence.

- **🔴 #12 (no "clear canvas" / "new framework" affordance)** — **NOT addressed by M08.7a (out of scope — Builder UX).** Observed: M08.7 touched no renderer/canvas code (the cumulative diff is `crates/runtime-main/src/sdk/` + tests + docs; zero `src/components/`). **Routed → M08.8 (app-workbench — the 32 Builder findings cluster).**

The runtime-side tier wire and the UI desync are distinct surfaces. **Routed → M08.8 (the tier-state-machine UI block, joined with the M08.6 🟡 #6/#20 tier items).**
- **🔴 #22 (budget cap doesn't persist across app restart — regression of the M08.G claimed close)** — **NOT closed; the budget *engine* now exists, the *persistence* bug is untouched.** Observed: rung 5 built the budget enforcement engine at the run loop (E-05, engine-tested) — so when M08.8 builds the in-app budget surface, the enforcement underneath it is real. But rung 5 did **not** touch the Settings cap input, the `set_global_budget` persistence, or the renderer-on-mount read that #22 flags, and produced **no cross-restart observation**. #22 remains open. **Routed → M08.8 (the in-app budget surface — Settings cap + cross-restart persistence; the app-workbench absorbs the M08.6.7 #22 candidate).**

### Gotchas graduation (v1.6+ protocol — eighth milestone to ship this section)

Per `STAGE-PROMPT-PROTOCOL.md` + the closeout `<gotchas_graduation>` (stages A, B, C, D, E + Stage V). Disposition: **kept** | **graduated** | **resolved** | **expired**.

| Stage | Gotcha / friction event | Disposition | Target/Resolution |
|---|---|---|---|
| A | Executing `Read`/`Write` broke 4 pre-existing M06 contract tests that pinned the *painted* `Exec/<toolname>` model using `Read` as the example tool (2 hung 3600 s on a HITL await) | graduated | Forward candidate for the phase-doc red-phase steps: "grep existing tests for wired built-in-name `ToolUse` injections — an execution change collides with any that pin the painted Exec-grant behavior." Recurs at every primitive whose name was used as a painted example. |
| A | `cargo test` stops at the first failing binary (alphabetical), masking the full blast radius | graduated | `--no-fail-fast` is required for blast-radius assessment. Candidate for `docs/gotchas.md` (test-scoping) + the stage-prompt scoping step. |
| A | `cargo-mutants` not installed; `cargo install` denied by the sandbox | kept (RECURRING — see E) | `cluster-pattern.md` §5 already sanctions the manual spot-check + `!`-command fallback when cargo-mutants is unavailable locally. |
| B | Stub-driven `cargo-mutants` produced 2 in-diff mutants, both unviable (a `()`-returning `set_tier` wire is below mutation granularity; `TestOutcome` is not `Default`) — the automated gate did not meaningfully exercise the wire; the manual spot-check substituted | graduated | The "one-line `()`-returning wire → no viable mutant → manual analysis is primary" pattern. `cluster-pattern.md` §5 covers it; a one-line note that delegating-statement rungs should *expect* the manual path is the forward candidate. |
| B | HITL `ground_at_red` triage: the Tester is HITL-less by design (ADR-0019); a violation folds into `TestOutcome.capability_failures`, no live HITL prompt | resolved | Triage outcome (b); recorded in the test file's B.4.3 doc + the B retro. Live HITL is a live-session concern, tested where a live `HitlSeam` is used. |
| C | The resolved skill body is in `LoadedFramework.companions[]`, dropped before `run_test_session_with(&Framework)` — not reachable from the run loop | graduated | Threaded `resolved_skills` onto `CapabilityWiring`. Forward candidate: the phase doc for any primitive rung should state **which struct carries the primitive's data into the run path** (the rung-3/4/5 "resolved-but-not-threaded" class). |
| C | Spec §0b (tool-result) vs the phase-doc ADR-0027 sketch (system_prompt-append) — the sketch's "a tool result vanishes after the turn" rationale is factually wrong (`run_agent` re-sends `config.messages` every turn) | resolved | Surfaced per §2 (do not pick); maintainer chose the spec model; ADR-0027 records the system_prompt path as forward. Forward candidate: check phase-doc ADR sketches against the spec before authoring (the "Schema/contract reality check" v1.9 cluster, continued from M08.6). |
| C | `clippy::missing_const_for_fn` on a test stub could not surface in red (the test file didn't compile until production symbols existed); landed as a separate labelled `style(...)` follow-up | resolved | The v1.8 two-commit convention handles it (mechanical test-file lint = separate labelled follow-up). Generalizes to every strict-TDD stage whose red test references new production symbols. |
| D | The "awaiter" shape (`await_capability_violation_hitl`) is wrong for a gap — its await-then-continue + test-defaults no-op both fail a halt; v0.1 has no resolve-and-resume machinery | resolved | The new minimal `gap_suspended` loop-break is the v0.1 suspend; the awaiter is built at the resume rung (ADR-0029 / M08.9.F). Recorded in the D retro + impl commit. |
| D | The painted behavior is a `CapabilityViolation`, not the doc-predicted `ToolInvoked` (the undeclared meta-tool hits L1) | resolved | The red trace is the source of truth for painted behavior, not the phase-doc prediction (rule 11). The "run the assembled thing" close gate caught the real shape. |
| D | `too_long_first_doc_paragraph` + `doc_markdown` clippy lints on NEW production doc comments only surface at green | resolved | Mechanical green-phase fixes, not red signals. Sibling to C's const-fn lint. |
| E | **`cargo-mutants` with a crate's `[lints] -D warnings` marks body-replacement mutants spuriously UNVIABLE** (a replaced body leaves params unused → `unused_variable` → compile error → "unviable"); the gate didn't exercise them until re-run with `RUSTFLAGS="--cap-lints=allow"` | **graduated → `docs/gotchas.md` candidate** | The standout reusable gotcha of the milestone. Any crate with `[lints] -D warnings` (most of this workspace) needs `RUSTFLAGS="--cap-lints=allow"` for cargo-mutants to actually exercise body-replacement mutants. Recommended for a `docs/gotchas.md` entry + a `cluster-pattern.md` §5 note. |
| E | `tester.rs` needed no change (the framework budget block is already in `CapabilityWiring.framework`); `NotifierDispatched` is bound to a `HitlTriggerRef` → `Warn` emits `BudgetWarn`, OS notifier = TD-038 | resolved | Grounding the actual data path beat trusting the phase-doc file list (rung 5 over-specified `tester.rs`). TD-038 logged. Budget `Suspend` folded into ADR-0029 (generalized to budget). |
| V | 🟡 #1 (built-in-execution ADR never filed; 0026 reused) | resolved (in-cluster at closeout) | Filed ADR-0028 + repointed refs + corrected the stale flip instruction + corrected the in-process-set overclaim. |
| V | 🟢 #2 (rung-1 two-reads test) + 🟢 #3 (rung-4 recoverable rebuild assertion) | resolved | Logged `docs/tech-debt.md` TD-039 / TD-040 this closeout. |

**Summary:** 15 stage-gotcha + friction + Stage-V entries across A–E + V → dispositions: **resolved** 9 (stage-local fixes / owned §12 reconciliations / V in-cluster absorptions); **graduated** 5 (forward-applicable — the painted-name test collision (A), `--no-fail-fast` blast-radius (A), the `()`-wire-no-viable-mutant pattern (B), the "which struct carries the data into the run path" rung-data-threading class (C), and the standout **cargo-mutants `[lints] -D warnings` → `--cap-lints=allow`** gotcha (E)); **kept** 1 (cargo-mutants-unavailable-locally, recurring A→E — the manual-spot-check fallback). **expired** 0. ### Simplify pass outcome (v1.6 `<simplify_pass>`)

Per the closeout `<simplify_pass>`. One read-only review agent (the `code-simplifier` agent) ran against the cumulative M08.7 diff (`main...HEAD`, 49 commits across X/A–E + V). **Proposal pass — `<approval_required>true</approval_required>` — no changes auto-applied.** Aggregate verdict: **the cumulative M08.7 diff is structurally sound.** The five rungs add a coherent execution engine with load-bearing discipline — each rung has a distinct `drive_stream` interception point, clean separation, and reuse of existing primitives (enforcer, ladder, events, emitter seam). Zero nesting in the dispatch chain (MCP → built-in → LoadSkill → request_capability → pipeline), each with its own pattern-match + `continue`. No O(N²) loops, no unbounded allocations, no hot-path re-derivation at v0.1 scale. The findings:

| ID | Proposal | Sev | Recommendation |
|---|---|---|---|
| RU-M08.7-1 | Extract a shared `tool_input_str(input, key)` helper — `dispatch_load_skill` + `dispatch_request_capability` repeat `input.get(key).and_then(as_str).unwrap_or_default().to_string()` (`agent_sdk.rs`) | Low | Defer → **TD-041**. Two production sites + one near-variant in `builtin_tools.rs`; below the CLAUDE.md §9 "wait for the fourth" bar. Revisit when a fourth `ToolUse`-input handler lands (M08.9 sub-agent/plan dispatch). |
| EFF-M08.7-1 | `dispatch_budget_actions` carries `current_model` mutation across the `actions` loop (correct for warn→downshift ordering today; subtle if a 3rd model-aware action lands) | Low | Defer → **TD-042**. The simplify-pass explicitly recommended **no refactor now** — the current form is correct and necessary. Clarity flag for future extension only. |
| CQ-M08.7-1 | The 4 `if let Some(wiring)`/`is_some()` guards in `drive_stream` (`:597/617/640/665`) repeat | Low | **No action — current form affirmed preferable.** The per-rung guards document which rungs require wiring; a unified guard would nest the whole rung stack and reduce clarity. Not a deferral; no TD. |
| CQ-M08.7-2 | `emit_builtin_result` clones `input`/`value` for two back-to-back `self.emit` calls + the `DispatchedTool` | Low | **No action — current form affirmed preferable.** Necessary owned-field clones; negligible at v0.1 token scale; micro-opt not warranted. Not a deferral; no TD. |

**Recommended maintainer-approved subset (focused refactor commit before the PR opens):** **none — the empty subset** (the M08 / M08.6 precedent; an explicitly valid `<simplify_pass>` outcome). The two genuine deferrals route to `docs/tech-debt.md` **TD-041/042** (appended this closeout); the two CQ findings were reviewed and the current form affirmed (no TD — they are not deferrals). ### Codebase deep dive (cumulative — M01 … M08.7 + M08.8)

M08.8 is the milestone that makes the M08.7 engine **visible and operable in the running app**. Through M08.7 the runtime *executed* its single-agent primitives (rungs 1–5, observed at the engine granularity) but the assembled Tauri app could not *show* it: agent output surfaced only through `RUST_LOG` (TD-034), and every production run silently ran Novice (TD-036). M08.8 closes both for the built surfaces and rebuilds the app to the committed Light Instrument design — and, decisively, holds every surface to the **real Tauri app driven via `tauri-driver`** (ADR-0021) + the maintainer IRL, never Playwright-mock-green (rule 11). The M08.6.V "Sound 0🔴 while the app was never run" escape did not recur: V's 5th `assembled_execution` pass drove the real binary for every surface (A 2/2, B 3/3, B.fix 5/5, B.fix2 6/6 incl. a live Anthropic run, C/C.fix tier specs on a clean Novice baseline — 22/22 assertions on a clean baseline).

The shipped surfaces:
- **The execution view** (A). `src/lib/graphStore.ts` turns the `stream_text` no-op into a per-session `outputBuffer` the DESIGN.md Output/Inspector rail renders live (mono "instrument register"); tool nodes retain `{input, output}` and are clickable → the rail (`InspectorPanel.tsx`, parameterized by a `store` prop) shows the selected node's payload over **either** the live `useGraphStore` or the scoped `useTestGraphStore` (the shared `createGraphStore` factory gives both the same surfacing). Closes the surfacing half of TD-034.
- **The Light Instrument system** (B + B.fix). B replaced the dark M03 `:root` with the DTCG three-tier token system (primitive→semantic→component CSS custom properties + the `[data-accent|density|direction]` theming hooks), built the 52/232/360 three-pane shell (`AppShell`), and added two reusable primitives — `Toast` (`role=status`/polite, no interactive children) and `Modal` (z-300, 86vh scroll, untruncated labels — closes #24). B.fix then restyled **every** surface to its `workbench.css` spec (hairline borders, restrained radii, the mono/tabular register from 8→30 mono selectors, segmented controls), built the two missing mockup surfaces (the Tester metric cards + the validation err-card), bundled the IBM Plex woff2 (ending reliance on the WebView2-blockable Google `@import`), and migrated `TesterModal` onto `Modal` (TD-043). The rename-free discipline (alias legacy `--node-*` names onto the new tokens; change property values not class names) let a ~2,700-line stylesheet rebuild keep ~620 class-existence tests green.
- **Reload-reconstruct** (B.fix2). A backend `replay_latest_session` command supplies the latest persisted session id after `reloadSession` wipes renderer `localStorage`, and the `replay.rs` translator was rewritten from a hand-rolled (and fabricated-fixture-pinned, zero-events-against-real-data) reinvention to a one-line `serde_json::from_value::<AgentEvent>` round-trip — deleting ~160 buggy lines. TD-044 closed; the fabricated-fixture disease logged as gotcha #94 + the TD-045 sweep.
- **Tier in the run loop** (C + C.fix). The Tauri `test_framework` command now reads `CurrentTierState` and threads the tracked tier through `test_framework_with`→`run_test_session_with_tier`→`enforcer.set_tier`, so a Promoted run reaches the L1 **scope** gate rather than being **tier**-denied first (TD-036 — the wire was one delegation call; the `run_test_session_with_tier` seam pre-existed). C.fix closed the **display** half C missed: the App mount seeds `currentTier` from `get_current_tier` (mirroring the `hasApiKey` seed) so the display reads the enforced tier across a reload (#19), and a tier-change toast confirms the transition (#20).

What's solid: every built surface is real-app-observed (not tests-green), with the assembled close bar enforced for all of them; strict v1.8 two-commit TDD held on every code stage (every `git diff <red>..<impl> -- '**/tests/**'` empty, V-confirmed at Inventory); the rename-free token/class discipline made a full design-system rebuild low-risk; diagnose-first + the rule-11 real-app run caught the B.fix2 fixture-fabrication bug a fully green unit+integration suite was blind to. What's structurally weak / will compound: (1) **the milestone's scope is the *foundation*, not the full loop** — budget-visible, gap-resolution, and save-from-scratch (the old D/E/F) are re-cut out (ADR-0031) and route to M11/M13; a reader must not read "operable foundation" as "the full author→run→resolve→save loop works." (2) **The Tester signal is tier-shaped but not yet honest** — a tier-limited run reads `passed=true` with no distinct badge (TD-047, the documented-defensible `fold_outcome` contract; the gap is observability) — M08.9's explicit job. (3) **The positive Promoted-Write-lands enforcement is assembled+IRL-grounded, not V-real-app-driven** (key/live-model-dependent) — the honest ceiling of the tier claim. (4) **The fabricated-fixture class (TD-045) is swept but not exhaustively cleared** — the drone projectors + `ipc.ts` hand-mirrors remain candidate sites for the same disease on any future replay/recovery/audit touch.

What surprised: the **"structural half shipped, user-visible half missed" pattern recurred twice** (B recolored→B.fix restyled; C wired→C.fix displayed) — the renderer sibling of M08.7's "painted-not-executed", and the reason the close bar is the *observed surface*, not the wired mechanism (rule 11). The eval-first within-range time-box estimation that began at M08.7 continued (every stage ~1 session, on estimate).

### Adherence to spec

The M08.8 bar maps to spec §9 (the Canvas/workbench surfaces), §8.security L4 (tier), `DESIGN.md` conformance, and ADR-0021's real-app close. Each claim is cited against the shipped code + the real-app E2E that demonstrates it (never inferred from structure — rule 11):

- ✅ **Execution observable in the app (A; spec §9; DESIGN.md Inspector/Output rail; closes TD-034 surfacing half).** Code: `src/lib/graphStore.ts` (`stream_text`→`outputBuffer`; tool `{input,output}` retention) + `src/components/InspectorPanel.tsx` (the `store`-parameterized rail). Demonstrated by `tests/e2e-tauri/execution_view.e2e.ts` (2/2 real-app; V 2026-06-05): streamed text in the rail, a `Read`-node click surfaces input + returned contents, tool node `data-kind=tool`/`data-status=complete`.
- ✅ **The Light Instrument system + the reusable primitives (B + B.fix; DESIGN.md §Colors/Typography/Layout/Elevation/Components; closes #24 + TD-043).** Code: `src/styles.css` (the DTCG `:root` + the per-surface restyle), `src/components/{Toast,Modal,AppShell,MetricCard,ValidationCard}.tsx`, the bundled `src/assets/fonts/*.woff2`. Demonstrated by `tests/e2e-tauri/visual_foundation.e2e.ts` (3/3) + `design_conformance.e2e.ts` (5/5) on the real app (V 2026-06-05): light canvas, three-pane shell, untruncated "Cancel", auto-dismissing toast, IBM Plex computed (bundled woff2 wins), segmented view-switch, hairline borders, Tester `modal--full`.
- ✅ **Reload reconstructs the graph (B.fix2; spec §1b recovery — rebuild from persisted signals, no re-execution; closes TD-044).** Code: `src-tauri/src/commands.rs::replay_latest_session` + the `src/sdk/replay.rs` serde round-trip + the App-mount replay ordering. Demonstrated by `tests/e2e-tauri/smoke.e2e.ts` test 6 (6/6 incl. a real Anthropic run; V 2026-06-05): a real run → reload → the graph reconstructs (`data-status=complete` after `reloadSession`). `applyEvent` idempotent on node id (graphStore.ts) — replay yields the same graph.
- ✅ **Tier in the run loop + truthful display (C + C.fix; spec §8.security L4; ADR-0030; resolves TD-036).** Code: `src-tauri/src/commands.rs` (`test_framework` reads `CurrentTierState`; `test_framework_with`→`run_test_session_with_tier`→`enforcer.set_tier`) + `src/App.tsx` (the mount seed + the tier_transition toast). Demonstrated by the assembled `commands.rs::test_framework_with_at_promoted_…`/`…_at_novice_…` (the scope-vs-tier gate contrast; neither writes the file out of scope) + `tests/e2e-tauri/tier_enforcement.e2e.ts` (2/2 UI-truth) + `tier_display.e2e.ts` (1/1 reload seed) on a clean baseline (V 2026-06-05) + the maintainer IRL. ⚠️ The **positive** Promoted-Write-lands path is assembled + maintainer-IRL grounded, **not** V-real-app-driven (live-model-dependent — CLAUDE.md §10).
- ✅ **No schema change; sandbox boundary untouched (scope lock).** `git diff main..HEAD -- schemas/` is empty; M08.8 touched no `schemas/*.v1.json`; the `AgentEvent` union already carried the payloads A surfaced; no drone/sandbox protocol change.
- ⚠️ **Tier-change toast register (C.fix; cosmetic).** `App.tsx:143` pushes the raw lowercase tier ("Tier changed to promoted") rather than the title-cased value the phase doc illustrated. Contract met (a toast names the new tier); register-inconsistent. → TD-048 (logged this closeout).
- ⚠️ **`design_conformance.e2e.ts:96` under-asserts (B.fix; test-completeness).** The test name says "with metric cards" but the body asserts only `modal--full`/`role=dialog`/close, not the `.metric` elements. The cards ship; the real-app regression guard for them is absent. → TD-049 (logged this closeout).
- ⚠️ **Tier-limited Tester signal not distinct (C; observability — DESIGN.md/spec §9 Tester surface).** `fold_outcome` does not fold an L4 `TierViolation`, so a tier-limited run reads `passed=true` with no badge — the documented, defensible contract (not a correctness bug). → TD-047, owned by M08.9 (the honest Tester).
- ❌ **None.** No built surface's app-observable claim failed against the real app; V produced zero 🔴.

### Spec review (forward-looking)

- **Missing items:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §9 (the Canvas) — the spec describes the workbench surfaces but does not name the **`tauri-driver` real-app close bar** (ADR-0021) as the conformance gate, nor the DESIGN.md Light Instrument token architecture (`docs/design/workbench-mockup/`) as the visual source of truth. A §9 pointer to ADR-0021 + DESIGN.md would pin "a UI surface is done when the real app shows it."
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §8.security L4 — the tier gate is described; the spec does not name **where** the live tier is set (`enforcer.set_tier`, threaded from `CurrentTierState` through the run-path construction) nor the Tester's tier model (runs at the user's tracked tier per ADR-0030, not a fixed sandbox tier). A one-line §8.security note + an ADR-0030 pointer would pin C's contract.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §9 Tester surface — the spec/DESIGN.md do not yet distinguish a **tier-limited** run from a clean pass (TD-047). The honest-Tester surface (a "tier-limited; promote to exercise" badge) should land in the spec when M08.9 builds it.
- **Contradictions:** None unresolved. The C-stage local-phase-doc vs origin "C=Budget/E=Tier" contradiction was a cross-machine staleness artifact (the §8 phase-doc pre-flight + the fast-forward resolved it); the phase-doc C.2/C.4 "smoke" naming (smoke intentionally excluded per ADR-0030) is a closeout-reconciliation note, not a code contradiction.
- **Ambiguity / §12-owned decisions the build resolved:** the Toast omits the mockup's × dismiss button (a `role=status` live region must not contain interactive controls — a11y over mockup-literalism, surfaced as a Stage-D divergence); the Tester migrates onto `Modal` only when its class-pinning tests move into a RED commit (B deferred, B.fix executed — the test-bearing-migration rule); the replay translator is serde-round-trip (B.fix2 — any new `AgentEvent` variant replays for free).
- **Recommended spec changes:** a focused `docs(spec):` pass — the §9 real-app-close-bar + DESIGN.md-source-of-truth note, the §8.security tier-set-point + ADR-0030 pointer, and (when M08.9 lands) the §9 tier-limited-Tester-signal note. Not blocking.

### The re-cut (ADR-0031) — recorded

The v0.1 success criterion was re-cut mid-milestone around **author-and-run**: the budget-visible (D), gap-resolve-and-resume (E), and UX-hardening/save-path (F) stages were **superseded and never built**; their work routes to **M11 (real-data / recoverability) / M13 (hardening / save-path)**, and generators + mentor to **v1.0**. `docs/MVP-v0.1.md`, §0d, and `docs/workbench-delivery-plan.md` are already reconciled (committed under ADR-0031). The post-M08.8 sequencing: **M08.9** (honest, drill-able Tester — TD-047 truthful verdict + run drill-down) → **M09** (workbench vertical slice) → **M10** (author-anything) → **M11** (real-data) → **M12** (execution breadth: sub-agents → plan → hooks → MCP-fix → composition; the gap **resume** of ADR-0029 lands here, which is why ADR-0029 STAYS Proposed → M12) → **M13** (hardening). ADR-0030 (tier) + ADR-0031 (re-cut) flip Proposed→Accepted at the PR (orchestrator, at merge); ADR-0029 stays Proposed.

### M08.8.V findings carry-forward

M08.8.V ran the five-pass fresh-context verifier (Inventory + Wire + Behavior + Multi-call + the v1.9 5th `assembled_execution` pass driving the real Tauri binary), bias-guarded (it did NOT read the A/B/B.fix/B.fix2/C/C.fix retros, the summary, or any gap-analysis beyond M08.7). Outcome **Sound but rough**, verification axes **14/15**, **0🔴 / 1🟡 / 2🟢**:

- **🟡 #1 (the tier E2E is non-hermetic w.r.t. persisted `tier.json`)** — **RESOLVED at this closeout.** The full local `test:e2e:tauri` read EXIT_CODE=1 on a machine whose `tier.json` was left Promoted by a prior run (CI is unaffected — a fresh runner has no `tier.json` → Novice default → green); after a Novice reset the two tier specs ran 3/3 green. Fixed by a `beforeSession` hook in `wdio.conf.ts` that seeds `tier.json`=novice before each spec's app launch (the correct seam — a mocha `before()` is too late, the backend reads the file at process startup), making the local gate hermetic regardless of persisted state. FINAL DISPOSITION (the fix is written + the seam is correct; the hermetic gate is verified by construction on a fresh runner — the local-wedge case the maintainer reproduced is exactly what the seed pre-empts).
- **🟢 #2 (tier-change toast title is raw lowercase, not the title-cased register the phase doc illustrated)** — logged `docs/tech-debt.md` **TD-048** this closeout. FINAL DISPOSITION for M08.8 (cosmetic; the contract — a toast naming the new tier — is met).
- **🟢 #3 (`design_conformance.e2e.ts:96` name over-claims — asserts the modal, not the metric cards)** — logged `docs/tech-debt.md` **TD-049** this closeout. FINAL DISPOSITION for M08.8 (the cards ship + are unit-tested; the real-app assertion gap is the debt).

V→closeout handoff disposition: **zero 🔴 (a clean handoff — no D.fix, no waiver); one 🟡 fixed at this closeout (the `wdio.conf.ts` before-session seed); two 🟢 logged (TD-048/049).** V's verdict was honest at its own granularity (rule 11): every in-scope surface grounded-by-real-app execution (the 5th pass drove the real binary, 22/22 on a clean baseline); the **positive** Promoted-enforcement was stated as a hypothesis-from-V's-seat (assembled + maintainer-IRL grounded, not V-driven — the key/live-model dependency), not smoothed. The closeout also backfilled the absent `M08.8.A-retrospective.md` (V Decision 4) — the cross-machine "retro-presence = stage executed" invariant now holds for all built stages.

### Gotchas graduation (v1.6+ protocol — ninth milestone to ship this section)

Per `STAGE-PROMPT-PROTOCOL.md` + the closeout `<gotchas_graduation>` (stages A, B, B.fix, B.fix2, C, C.fix). Disposition: **kept** | **graduated** | **resolved** | **expired**.

| Stage | Gotcha / friction event | Disposition | Target/Resolution |
|---|---|---|---|
| A | Stage shipped with NO retrospective (the §19 retro-presence invariant broken) | graduated | V Decision 4 → a standing closeout check: verify each shipped stage has a retro file before the summary lands. Backfilled at this closeout. |
| B | strict-TS `noUncheckedIndexedAccess` on new components only surfaced at green; happy-dom does not resolve viewport units (`maxHeight:'86vh'`); fake/real-timer interleave in one describe | graduated | A `<pre_red_mechanical_sweep>` (stub `tsc` on new components before the full run) for renderer stages would pre-empt the index-access fixes. "happy-dom doesn't resolve viewport units → assert inline `.style`" is a reusable testing bit. |
| B | A `role=status` live region must not contain interactive children — the Toast drops the mockup's × dismiss button | resolved | a11y over mockup-literalism (Soueidan/MDN); surfaced as a Stage-D divergence; auto-dismiss-only. The reusable bit: a live-region toast is auto-dismiss, not button-dismiss. |
| B / B.fix | A class/testid-pinning unit test makes a refactor **test-bearing** — the `TesterModal`→`Modal` migration was deferred at B (tests pinned `.tester-modal__*`), executed at B.fix by moving the test rewrite into the RED commit | graduated | The "test-bearing migration → schedule the test edit into a RED commit, never an impl commit" rule. Recurs at any class-pinned component refactor under strict-TDD. |
| B.fix2 | **Fabricated-fixture disease** — a hand-rolled translator (`replay.rs`) pinned by fabricated unit-test payloads stayed green while producing ZERO events against real data; caught only by the assembled-app run (rule 11) | **graduated → gotcha #94 (shipped)** | The standout reusable gotcha of the milestone. Any hand-rolled (de)serializer mirrored by unit fixtures is a candidate; prefer a serde round-trip. TD-045 sweeps the sibling sites (drone projectors, `ipc.ts`). |
| B.fix2 | In-source `#[cfg(test)]` tests rewritten in the IMPL commit — *literally* compliant with `**/tests/**`-empty, but a silent test rewrite in an impl commit | kept (protocol-iteration candidate) | Recommend a 3-commit structure (red `tests/` → in-source-test → impl) OR an explicit `TEST-REWRITE-IN-IMPL: <files>` impl-commit marker when in-source tests must change. Flagged, not changed this milestone. |
| C | A thin-delegation `()`-returning wire (`set_tier`) produces only unviable cargo-mutants → a hand-mutant (wrong tier into the call) gives real mutation signal | graduated (recurring — M08.7.B sibling) | `cluster-pattern.md` §5 covers it; delegating-statement rungs should *expect* the manual hand-mutant path. |
| C | Local phase-doc vs origin stage-identity contradiction (C=Tier vs stale C=Budget) — surfaced, not picked; fast-forwarded | resolved | The §8 phase-doc pre-flight + the cross-machine paste resolved it (the exact M04 PR #53 failure mode the rule guards). No doc fix (orch owns the C.2/C.4 "smoke" naming reconciliation — done at this closeout). |
| C.fix | C claimed "#19 fixed at the backend" with no display-layer evidence (enforcement-observed ≠ display-fixed) | resolved | Hard Rule 11: the display half was never touched by C; C.fix closed it + the re-IRL-with-restart is the only evidence licensing "#19 resolved". The grounded-claims rule working as designed. |

**Summary:** 9 stage-gotcha + friction entries across A–C.fix → dispositions: **graduated** 5 (the absent-retro standing check (A); the renderer `<pre_red_mechanical_sweep>` + happy-dom-viewport bits (B); the test-bearing-migration→RED-commit rule (B/B.fix); the fabricated-fixture disease → **gotcha #94 shipped** (B.fix2); the `()`-wire hand-mutant pattern (C, recurring)); **resolved** 3 (the live-region toast a11y call (B); the cross-machine stage-identity contradiction (C); the enforcement-observed≠display-fixed grounded-claims close (C.fix)); **kept** 1 (the in-source-test-rewritten-in-impl protocol-iteration candidate, B.fix2). **expired** 0. The standout signals: (1) the **"structural half shipped, user-visible half missed"** pattern recurred twice (B→B.fix, C→C.fix) — the renderer sibling of M08.7's paints-not-executes, and the reason the close bar is the *observed surface*; (2) the **fabricated-fixture disease** (gotcha #94) — a green unit+integration suite structurally blind to a bug that produced zero events against real data, caught only by the rule-11 assembled-app run.

### Simplify pass outcome (v1.6 `<simplify_pass>`)

Per the closeout `<simplify_pass>`. One read-only `code-simplifier` agent ran against the cumulative M08.8 diff (`main..HEAD`, 115 commits) — **proposal pass, `<approval_required>true</approval_required>`, no changes auto-applied** — focused on the four named candidate areas (the exec-view data plane, the restyle token usage, the tier seed + ipc wrapper, `TesterModal`). Aggregate verdict: **the cumulative M08.8 diff is structurally sound.** All ten findings (RU-1..RU-10) are **no-action — current form affirmed preferable**: the `stream_text` append is minimal and idiomatic; the `InspectorPanel` `store`-prop binding is the M08.8.A requirement (not a premature HOC); the legacy `--node-*`→token alias remap is a correct one-time rename-free bridge (post-migration deletion is a v1.0+ story); the App-mount tier seed intentionally mirrors the `hasApiKey` seed (parallel init paths, not repeated logic); the `test_framework_with` tier thread is non-negotiable per ADR-0030; the `TesterModal` run/promote loops are two-site (below the "wait for the fourth" bar); `MetricCard`/`ValidationCard`/`Modal`/`formatPayload`/`clear()` are each already in minimal form. The pass surfaced **no finding the verifier missed** of correctness or quality significance.

**Recommended maintainer-approved subset (focused refactor commit before the PR opens): none — the empty subset** (the M08 / M08.6 / M08.7 precedent; an explicitly valid `<simplify_pass>` outcome). No findings deferred to tech-debt (none rose to a deferral — all are current-form-affirmed). The "wait for the fourth" discipline held throughout the milestone.

**Claude:** I have generated this gap analysis after the built stages of M08.8 (A execution view → B + B.fix Light Instrument → B.fix2 reload-reconstruct → C + C.fix tier) + Stage V, as the M08.8.G closeout. This is my honest assessment of the cumulative code-vs-spec state across M01–M08.8. M08.8 delivered the **observable + operable foundation** of the v0.1 loop: execution is now watchable in the running Tauri app (A — TD-034 surfacing half closed), the Light Instrument design system is complete and real-app-conformant (B + B.fix — #24, TD-043 closed), reload reconstructs the graph from persisted signals (B.fix2 — TD-044 closed, gotcha #94 + TD-045 sweep), and runs enforce the user's tracked tier with a truthful display across restart (C + C.fix — TD-036 resolved, #19 closed-observed). Every built surface is **grounded-by-real-app execution** (the V 5th pass drove the real binary, 22/22 on a clean baseline) — the M08.6.V "Sound 0🔴 app-never-run" escape did not recur. **The honest ceiling (rule 11):** the positive Promoted-Write-lands enforcement is assembled + maintainer-IRL grounded, not V-real-app-driven (key/live-model-dependent); and M08.8's scope is the *foundation* — **D/E/F (budget-visible / gap-resume / save-path) were superseded by ADR-0031 and never built**, routing to M11/M13, with the gap **resume** (ADR-0029) → M12. The M08.6-IRL 5🔴 routed here are recorded with observed dispositions — **1 closed-observed** (#19 tier), **4 routed into the re-cut milestones** (#12/#22 → M11/M13; #17/#32 → M13 — owned by the superseded stages), none silently dropped. Stage V was **Sound but rough, 0🔴 / 1🟡 / 2🟢**: the 🟡 (non-hermetic tier E2E) fixed at this closeout (the `wdio.conf.ts` before-session seed); the two 🟢 logged TD-048/049. No schema change (`schemas/` diff empty); no coverage gate change (the four mirrors byte-consistent; §C M08.8 entry appended; `runtime-main` 96.27% ≥ 95; Vitest `src/` ≥ 80 every stage); the sandbox boundary untouched. The simplify pass found the diff structurally sound (empty approved subset). ADR-0030 (tier) + ADR-0031 (re-cut) flip Proposed→Accepted at the PR; ADR-0029 stays Proposed → M12. User review pending; per `CLAUDE.md` §20 this entry is **IMMUTABLE once committed** — future milestones report status updates via their Carry-forward sections only.

**Surfaced at:** 2026-06-05 (build-machine local time).

## M08.9 — Honest, drill-able Tester (the M09 trust prerequisite) (2026-06-06, Stage G closeout commit on parent-milestone branch `claude/m08.9-honest-tester`)

> Author: Claude (per `CLAUDE.md` §20)
> Stages aggregated: M08.9.A (truthful verdict — `fold_outcome` folds `AgentEvent::TierViolation` into `TestOutcome.tier_blocks` + a derived 3-state `verdict: TestVerdict`; `TesterModal` renders Pass/Fail/**TIER-LIMITED**; `passed` unchanged; closes TD-047), M08.9.B (run drill-down — `TesterModal` renders `outcome.trace` as verdict → per-tool-call input/result → raw via two behavior-preserving lift-to-shared extractions `formatPayload`/`RawDisclosure`), M08.9.V (the five-pass real-app verifier incl. the 5th `assembled_execution` pass driving the real Tauri binary — **Sound but rough, 1🔴 / 0🟡 / 0🟢**, the 🔴 a test-harness defect routed to D.fix), M08.9.D.fix (the committed Tester e2e regressions never executed their substantive assertion — a shared-session modal-scrim teardown defect; `afterEach`→`closeTester` in both specs; gotcha #95; closes V 🔴 #1).
> Reviewed against: `agent-runtime-spec.md` §9 (the Canvas/Tester surface), §8.security L4 (the tier gate); `DESIGN.md` (principle 1 feedback + progressive disclosure; principle 8 labels-true — the conformance target); ADR-0021 (the `tauri-driver` real-app E2E close bar), ADR-0030 (Tester runs at the tracked tier; a tier block is a user setting, not a defect), ADR-0031 (the v0.1 re-cut — M08.9 is the honest-Tester milestone preceding M09); ADR-0008 (the Stage-V verifier + the 🟢 tech-debt ledger); `docs/tech-debt.md` (this closeout resolves TD-047; TD-045/046/048/049 carry forward); `docs/coverage-policy.md` §A–§D (no gate change — §C M08.9 entry appended); gotcha #94 (producer-driven mirrors) + the new gotcha #95 (e2e modal `afterEach`); M01–M08.8 gap-analysis entries.
> M08.9 is a small, high-leverage follow-on under the ADR-0031 re-cut. **Scope: A (verdict) + B (drill-down) + V + D.fix.** Cumulative M08.9 code diff: `7143e92..HEAD` — 14 files, ~1,449 insertions / ~50 deletions (one Rust folder change in `tester.rs`; the rest renderer/CSS/TS + the e2e regressions). No schema change, no ADR filed.

### Codebase deep dive (cumulative — M01 … M08.8 + M08.9)

M08.9 closes the last honesty gap in the Tester result before M09's vertical slice relies on it. Through M08.8 the runtime *executed* the single-agent loop and *displayed* it (the Light Instrument workbench, the live execution view, the tier wire), but the Tester **verdict itself lied**: `fold_outcome` (`builder/tester.rs`) folded an L2 `CapabilityViolation` into `capability_failures` and an `ArtifactHashMismatch` into `integrity_blocked`, computed `passed = capability_failures.is_empty() && !integrity_blocked`, and dropped the L4 `AgentEvent::TierViolation` at `_ => {}`. So a Novice run blocked from writing a report returned `passed=true` with an empty failures list and `TesterModal` rendered a green **PASS** with no file on disk (TD-047, IRL-confirmed). The signal to fix it was already present — the `TierViolation { agent_id, tier, capability_kind, attempted_action }` sat in `outcome.trace`, unread.

The shipped surfaces:
- **The truthful verdict** (A). `fold_outcome` now folds `TierViolation` into a new `TestOutcome.tier_blocks: Vec<TierBlock>` (`tester.rs:203–208`) and derives a 3-state `verdict: TestVerdict` (`tester.rs:222–229`): a framework defect (L2 caps / integrity) ⇒ `Fail`; else a tier block ⇒ `TierLimited`; else `Pass`. `passed` is **unchanged** — a tier block is the user's tier setting, not a framework defect (ADR-0030), so a tier-limited-but-otherwise-clean run is `passed=true, verdict=TierLimited`. The hand-written `TestOutcome` Rust struct + its hand-written TS mirror (`ipc.ts:599–660`) stay in lockstep, producer-driven (gotcha #94 — the fold unit serializes a real `AgentEvent::TierViolation`). `TesterModal` renders the 3-state verdict badge keyed on `outcome.verdict` (`TesterModal.tsx:38–74`) — TIER-LIMITED shows the blocked action + a Promote affordance. No `schemas/` change, no ADR.
- **The run drill-down** (B). `TesterModal` renders `outcome.trace` as verdict → per-tool-call input/result → raw (`TraceDrilldown.tsx`'s `foldTrace` maps the trace to rows, pairing each tool invoke with its result/error). Reuse was achieved by two behavior-preserving lift-to-shared extractions: `formatPayload` (the M08.8.A Output-rail payload formatter, a module-private function not a component — lifted to `src/lib/formatPayload.ts`, reused by `InspectorPanel` + `TraceDrilldown`) and the Show-raw disclosure (lifted to `src/components/RawDisclosure.tsx`, which `ValidationCard` now delegates to with DOM/testids preserved so its tests pass untouched). Renderer-only; no new disclosure primitive, no backend/schema change.

What's solid: every behavioral claim is **grounded by real-app execution** (rule 11) — M08.9.V's 5th assembled-execution pass drove the real Tauri binary and observed both behaviors (a Novice Write run = verdict `TIER-LIMITED` + `tester-result--tier-limited` + the Promote affordance + no file; a Read run = drill a tool step → input payload (the real `Cargo.toml`) → Show-raw `tool_invoked`). The fix was genuinely small because the work was *composition* — fold a signal already in the trace (A: a ~3-line real-logic change), reuse two existing primitives (B) — exactly the phase-doc framing ("fold it, don't detect it"; "reuse it, don't build it"). Strict v1.8 two-commit TDD held on both code stages (red→impl test diff EMPTY, V-confirmed). What's structurally weak / honest ceiling: (1) the committed e2e regressions were **authored-but-never-run** until V's 5th pass — they crashed on a key-present machine (shared-session modal-scrim) and skipped on CI, so the merge gate was green while the assertion never executed (V 🔴 #1, closed by D.fix; graduated as gotcha #95 — the assembled-app-regression mandate's reason to exist, recurring). (2) the substantive real-model cases stay `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`-skip-guarded on CI (the documented ADR-0021/§10 posture — maintainer IRL is the compensating control), the same as `smoke.e2e.ts`. (3) the separate phantom-`passed` verify finding (`vdr.rs:98`, TD-046) is explicitly out of M08.9 scope (owner M9, before a verify producer lands).

What surprised: the "structural-half-shipped, behavior-unverified" pattern recurred in the *test harness* this time — a committed merge-blocking regression can be green-by-skip on CI and crash-on-key locally, so authoring an e2e regression ≠ running it; only the assembled key-present run proves the assertion executes. This is precisely the bug class Stage V's 5th pass exists to catch, and it caught it.

### Adherence to spec

The M08.9 bar maps to spec §9 (the Tester surface), §8.security L4 (the tier gate), `DESIGN.md` conformance (labels-true + progressive disclosure), and ADR-0021's real-app close. Each claim is cited against the shipped code + the real-app E2E that demonstrates it (never inferred from structure — rule 11):

- ✅ **The Tester verdict tells the truth (A; spec §9; DESIGN.md principle 8 labels-true; ADR-0030; closes TD-047).** Code: `crates/runtime-main/src/builder/tester.rs` (`fold_outcome` `TierViolation` arm `:203–208` + the verdict computation `:222–229`; `TestOutcome.tier_blocks`/`verdict` + the `TierBlock`/`TestVerdict` types) + `src/lib/ipc.ts:599–660` (the lockstep TS mirror) + `src/components/builder/TesterModal.tsx:38–74` (the 3-state badge). Demonstrated by the producer-driven Rust fold units (`fold_outcome_folds_tier_violation_…_passed_stays_true`; the both-tier-and-capability `Fail`-with-`tier_blocks` case) + the verdict vitest + `tests/e2e-tauri/tester_verdict.e2e.ts` (real-app, V 5th pass 2026-06-06: a Novice Write run reads TIER-LIMITED, not PASS, and writes no file). `passed` unchanged (tier ≠ defect).
- ✅ **The run is drill-able (B; spec §9; DESIGN.md principle 1 feedback + progressive disclosure).** Code: `src/components/builder/TraceDrilldown.tsx` (the `foldTrace` mapper + the row/expand render) mounted under the verdict in `TesterModal`, reusing `src/lib/formatPayload.ts` + `src/components/RawDisclosure.tsx`. Demonstrated by `TraceDrilldown.test.tsx` + the assembled-modal `TesterModal.drilldown.test.tsx` wiring test + `tests/e2e-tauri/tester_drilldown.e2e.ts` (real-app, V 5th pass: a Read run drills a tool step → input/result → Show-raw `tool_invoked`).
- ✅ **No schema change; the disclosure primitives were reused, not rebuilt (scope lock).** `git diff main..HEAD -- schemas/` is empty; `TestOutcome` is hand-written; B added no new disclosure UX (the two lifts are extractions of existing surfaces, DOM/testids preserved).
- ✅ **The committed merge-blocking regression actually executes its assertion (D.fix; ADR-0021; CLAUDE.md §5 v1.8 assembled-app-regression mandate; closes V 🔴 #1).** Code: `tests/e2e-tauri/tester_verdict.e2e.ts` + `tester_drilldown.e2e.ts` (the `afterEach`→`closeTester` + reverse-wait teardown). Demonstrated by the key-present `test:e2e:tauri` run: **12/12, exit 0**, with the TIER-LIMITED + drill-down cases executing (V proved the product correct via a throwaway harness; D.fix made the *committed* specs reproduce it). Graduated as gotcha #95.
- ⚠️ **The substantive real-model e2e cases skip on CI (key-guarded).** Honest ceiling: `tester_verdict.e2e.ts` / `tester_drilldown.e2e.ts` substantive cases require a live model (an Anthropic key) to emit the Write/Read `ToolUse`, so they `this.skip()` on keyless CI — the documented ADR-0021/§10 posture (maintainer IRL is the compensating control), identical to `smoke.e2e.ts` 3–6. The key-present local run is the executing-assertion evidence; D.fix's value is precisely that a key-present run no longer crashes.
- ❌ **None.** No built surface's app-observable claim failed against the real app; V produced zero false greens (the one 🔴 was a harness defect, product correct).

### Spec review (forward-looking)

- **Missing items:**
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §9 (the Tester surface) — the spec/DESIGN.md describe a Tester verdict but do not name the **3-state truth** (Pass / Fail / **Tier-limited**) nor the rule that a *tier-limited* run is not a PASS (the `verdict` is UI-truth layered on the back-compat `passed` bool). A §9 note pinning the 3-state verdict + the ADR-0030 "tier ≠ defect" basis would close the gap M08.8's gap-analysis flagged ("the spec does not yet distinguish a tier-limited run from a clean pass") — now built, should land in the spec.
  - `agent-runtime-spec.md` §9 — the spec does not name the **verdict → tool-payload → raw drill-down** as the Tester result's progressive-disclosure contract. A one-line §9 pointer to DESIGN.md principle 1 would pin it.
- **Contradictions:** None. The phase doc's Stage D/E/F (budget/gap-resume/save-path) were already superseded by ADR-0031 (recorded at M08.8); M08.9's scope is A+B only, consistent throughout.
- **Ambiguity / §12-owned decisions the build resolved:** "build no new disclosure primitive" vs the special-log anticipating a lift-to-shared — read as *inventing* a new UX is forbidden, *extracting* an existing one for reuse is the documented expectation (B lifted `formatPayload` + `RawDisclosure`); the Promote affordance reuses the existing `requestTierTransition` path (A); the verdict is UI-truth, `passed` stays for back-compat (A).
- **Recommended spec changes:** a focused `docs(spec):` §9 pass — the 3-state-verdict + tier-≠-defect note and the drill-down progressive-disclosure pointer. Not blocking.

### M08.9.V findings carry-forward

M08.9.V ran the five-pass fresh-context verifier (Inventory + Wire + Behavior + Multi-call + the 5th `assembled_execution` pass driving the real Tauri binary), bias-guarded (it did NOT read the A/B retros or any summary). Verification axes **15/15**; outcome **Sound but rough**, **1🔴 / 0🟡 / 0🟢**:

- **🔴 #1 (the committed Tester e2e regressions never execute their substantive assertion)** — **CLOSED at M08.9.D.fix** (`61f1b11`). The two specs share one app session per `describe`; Test 1 opened the Tester modal and left it open, so Test 2's view-switch click was scrim-intercepted → crash (suite 10/2, exit 1 with a key; `this.skip()` on CI). V proved the **product** correct on the real app via a corrected throwaway harness (TIER-LIMITED ≠ PASS; drill → payload → raw), so the defect was scoped precisely as **test-harness-only**. D.fix added an `afterEach`→`closeTester` + reverse-wait to both `describe`s (26 insertions / 0 deletions; assertions intact); the key-present `test:e2e:tauri` run is **12/12, exit 0** with the substantive cases executing. Graduated as **gotcha #95**.

V→closeout handoff disposition: **one 🔴 closed by a D.fix before this commit** (within the 2-iteration budget, iteration 1 — the fix path was pre-proven by V's throwaway); **zero 🟡, zero 🟢** (no tech-debt added). V's verdict was honest at its own granularity (rule 11): it drove the real binary and separated product-correct from harness-broken rather than smoothing a green. V Decision 3 (a standing e2e-tauri convention: a spec whose helper opens a modal must close it in `afterEach`) is **graduated to gotcha #95** at this closeout.

Per `STAGE-PROMPT-PROTOCOL.md` + the closeout `<gotchas_graduation>` (stages A, B; the V finding + D.fix folded in). Disposition: **kept** | **graduated** | **resolved** | **expired**.

| A | `clippy::too_long_first_doc_paragraph` on the new `TierBlock`/`TestVerdict` doc comments | resolved | Already covered by gotcha #48 (keep the first doc paragraph short); fixed first try. Sev-1, local. |
| A | The §8-vs-strict-TDD two-local-commit tension (two commits must exist to diff red..impl, but §8 forbids committing before approval) | kept | De-facto resolved every stage by keeping the commits local + unpushed; recurred at B. Candidate one-line protocol write-down (not changed this milestone). |
| A | The fix was ~3 lines of real logic — the signal/helper/disclosure surfaces all pre-existed | resolved | Confirms the phase-doc "fold it, don't detect it" framing; not a trap, a pattern-win. |
| B | strict-TS `noUncheckedIndexedAccess` discriminated-union narrowing only surfaces at green (`const step = steps[0]; if (step?.kind === …)`) | kept (protocol-iteration candidate) | A `<pre_red_mechanical_sweep>` (stub `tsc` on new components before the full run) for renderer stages would pre-empt it; recurred from M08.8.B. Flagged, not changed. |
| B | The "Output-rail payload component" was a module-private function, not a component; `ValidationCard` is a `role="alert"` card not reusable wholesale | resolved | The lift-to-shared was a function extraction (`formatPayload`) + a disclosure extraction (`RawDisclosure`), not a component reuse; DOM/testids preserved so existing tests pass untouched. The reusable bit: pin the *reuse boundary* to the actual shareable unit, not the phase-doc's framing of it. |
| V / D.fix | An `e2e-tauri` spec whose helper opens a modal MUST close it in `afterEach` — shared-session `it`s otherwise leave the modal scrim intercepting the next case's click; the trap hides on CI (key-guarded skip) and crashes only on a key-present machine, so a "green" merge gate ships a regression that never executed its assertion | **graduated → gotcha #95 (shipped)** | The standout reusable gotcha of the milestone — the assembled-app-regression mandate's reason to exist, in the test harness. Pairs with gotcha #89 (test:e2e:tauri is a CI-only gate; authoring ≠ running). |

### Simplify pass outcome (v1.6 `<simplify_pass>`)

Per the closeout `<simplify_pass>`. One read-only `code-simplifier` agent ran against the cumulative M08.9 code diff (`7143e92..HEAD`) — **proposal pass, `<approval_required>true</approval_required>`, no changes auto-applied** — focused on the named candidate areas (the verdict computation, the `foldTrace` trace-row mapper, the two lift-to-shared extractions, any TesterModal/drill-down duplication). Aggregate verdict: **the cumulative M08.9 diff is structurally sound.** All five findings (RU-1..RU-5) are **no-action — current form affirmed preferable**: the `fold_outcome` token-spend accumulate-then-finalize is idiomatic (RU-1); `foldTrace`'s consumed-index `Set` is encapsulated with no cross-codebase duplication (RU-2 — "wait for the fourth"); the `formatPayload` + `RawDisclosure` extractions are correctly scoped at exactly-twice reuse and preserve DOM/testid/class identity (RU-3); the `TestOutcome`/`TestVerdict` Rust↔TS lockstep is intentional and must NOT be schema-merged (RU-4, gotcha #94); the defect-dominates-tier verdict computation is clean and direct (RU-5). The pass surfaced **no finding of correctness or quality significance the verifier missed.**

**Recommended maintainer-approved subset (focused refactor commit before the PR opens): none — the empty subset** (the M08 / M08.6 / M08.7 / M08.8 precedent; an explicitly valid `<simplify_pass>` outcome).
